 mātar  sarasvati punar  punar aṣa natvā baddhāñjaliḥ kim api vijñapayāmi avaihi vāc cetasoḥ mama tathā bhava sāvadhānā vācaspateḥ vacasi na skhalataḥ  yathā ete viśva ārādhya iti atra viśva śabdena saṃsāri cetana vargaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ tasya eva tad ā ārādhaka tvāt  viśva īśāna iti atra samīhita phala saṃdohaḥ tasya bhagavat eka adhīna tvāt viśva kṛt iti atra upādāna samūhaḥ tasya eva tad kṛti vyāpya tvāt viśva saṃhāra kārī iti atra yāvat anitya nivahaḥ tasya eva tad vināśya tvāt viśva śaktiḥ iti atra yāvat kāryāstomaḥ tasya eva tad śakti viṣaya tvāt viśvajñāta iti atra yāvan jñeya prapañcaḥ tasya eva pad jñāna viṣaya tvāt viśva vyāpīyatra yāvat mūrttimat dravya rāśiḥ tasya eva viśeṣataḥ tad vyāpya tvāt itarasya tu tad dvārā viśvamūrtiḥ iti atra yāvat kāraka grāmaḥ tasya eva sākṣāt  tad prayatna adhiṣṭheya tayā asmad ādi śarīra samāna tvāt  ata eva na tatra śarīra antara apekṣā sākṣāt prayantān adhiṣṭheyeṣu hi sā syāt  daṇḍa ādivat  na tu sākṣāt prayatna adhiṣṭheyeṣu śarīravat  pinākī iti tu viśiṣṭa śastradhāradhamittaka nāma saṃkortanena prārabdha vighnasya protsāraṇam eva samīhitam iti sūcayati hetu hetumat bhāvena śaḍka uttarābhyām yojanā jyāyasī yathā avasthita yojanāyām tu artha pauna rūkti aprasarktā stuti tvam eva samādhāna madhyavaseyam iti namāmi ityādi dharmaḥ  nivartakaḥ vijñānam śarīra ādi vivikta ātma sākṣātkāraḥ vairāgyam rāga abhāvaḥ aiśvaryam bhūta indriya jayaḥ tad śānipe ata eva nidhaye vāc viśat hīnām adharma hetukaḥ hi avivekaḥ aviveka hetukam avairāgyam avairāgya mūlam anaiśvaryam tad mūlāḥ ca vacasām aviśuddhayaḥ tisraḥ khalu etāḥ tatra prathamā nirabhidhayatā dvitīyā viparītā amidheya tā tṛtīyā niṣprayojanāmigheya tā tā etāḥ katham bhūta indriya jayinaḥ  mahā muneḥ bhaviṣyanti ajita bhūtasya hi vivakṣoḥ tathāvidha prayatna aniṣpatteḥ nirabhidheyā vāc  bhavati ajita indriyasya ca viparyāsa vipralipsā hetukaḥ viparīta arthaḥ  vacana sandarbhaḥ ajita manasaḥ ca pramāda unmādavataḥ  niṣprayojanaḥ etāḥ ca vacasā ām aviśuddhīḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāneṣu sūtrakāra eva prapañcayiṣyati saḥ  ayam na tathā iti bhavati vāc viśuddhīnām nidhiḥ ata eva tāyī tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa kṣama saṃpradāya pravartakaḥ evam para apara gurūn natvā śiṣya buddhi samādhānāya samāhita vaiśiṣṭyam darśayati grantha iti nanu tātparyaṭīka iti vadatā pravṛtti pāṭava artham grantha saṃkṣepaḥ  darśitaḥ na ca śiṣyāṇām kathantā saṃbogha vidhurāṇām rāddhānta mātra parigrahaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ  vivakṣitaḥ tathā tve vā upaniṣada eva santu santu vā śava muṣṭi nyāyena ācārya upadeśāḥ kim anena iti ata āha nirasta akhila dūṣaṇa iti nanu evam grantha tātparyām vyākhyeyam dūṣaṇāni ca nirasyāni iti punar api grantha gauravam iti ata āha grantha vyākhyā  chalena eva iti nanu cirantare asmin nibandhe mahājana parigṛhīte bahavaḥ  nibandhāḥ tathāvidhāḥ santi iti kṛtam anene iti ata āha icchāmi iti nanu yadi granthakāra saṃpradāya vicchedena te nibandhāḥ katham kunibandhāḥ atha saṃpradāya u vicchinnaḥ katham tava api iyam vicchinna saṃpradāyā tātparyaṭīkā su nibandha iti ata āha ati jaratīnām iti uddyota kara saṃpradāyaḥ  hi amūṣām yauvanam tad ca kāla paripāka vaśāt  galitam iva kim nāma atra trilocana guroḥ sakāśāt upadeśa rasāyanam āsāditama mūṣām punarnavībhāvāya dīyata iti yujyate na ca kunibandha paṅka magnānām tad dātum ucita matas tasmāt utkṛṣya sva nibandha sthale sanniveśana rūpa samuddharaṇam eva sāṃpratam iti arthaḥ tatra bhagavataḥ  akṣapādasya muniṣu madhye pravara tvam śruti ādibhya eva su prasiddham kim anena saṃkīrtanena na ca etad atiśayena sāṃpratam upayujyate jagat upaśama nidāna śāstra praṇetṛ tvam ca tasya tad praṇayanam eva prakaṭayat asti tena api kim prakaṭitena sva nibandhasya tad viṣaya tā api tad vyākhyānāt eva labhyata iti kim tayā api kathitayā na ca asya nyāya mahodadheru utta ānatā pratibhāsa eva agratas  kartum ucitaḥ tasmāt  bhavitavyam atra tātparyeṇa tad āha atha iti tad apanīyata iti tad iti diś rāga ādi samutthāpitam śāstra ācchādakam kuhetu saṃtama samapaneya tvena parāmṛśatā śāstrasya eva ayam nibandha iti darśitam bhāṣyasya ca tad vivaraṇa rūpasya śāstra śarīra rūpa tayā na śāstrāt ādhikyam manyate mīmāṃsāyāḥ  iva vedāt  ata eva na atratyaṭīkāyāḥ vāttikāntena virodhaḥ etena śāstrasya yaḥ  nibandhaḥ  bhāṣya granthaḥ sa ku tārkikā jñāna nivṛtti hetuḥ kariṣyata iti vyākhyānam ṭīkā virodhena upekṣaṇīyam nanu sūtra ukta prayojana anuvādaḥ punar  kimartham na hi idam anūdya kiñcid  vidheyam pratiṣedhyam veha vidyate iti ata āha sūtra iti atha sva nibandhasya prayojana vattā pradarśanena kim siddhi atīti ata āha prekṣāvat iti nanu vyutpitsavaḥ  vyutpattim aghi kṛtya pravartante atas  vyutpādana pravṛttau vyutpattiḥ eva amīṣām prayojanam iti kim apareṇa prayojanena ityata āha vyutpāda mātrasya iti dvividham hi prayojanam mukhyam gauṇa ca tatra mukhyam puruṣa artha eva itarat  tu tad aṅgam iti tatra mukhya arthinaḥ tad sādhānam abhyarthayamānāḥ tatra pravartanta iti tad api prayojanam evati atas  mukhye prayojane sati gauṇam prayojanam tasmiḥ tu asati tad api na syāt iti niṣprayojana tā eva avatiṣṭhate na ca svātantryeṇa eva asya mukhyam prayojanam asti iti atas  yasya idam aṅga tasya mukhyam prayojanam asti iti darśite prekṣāvān pravarttitaḥ  bhavati iti abhisandhiḥ vārttika kṛta iti arthaḥ itas  api ṭīkā khaṇḍalakāt antar bhāvita phalavat sannidhauvaphalam tad aṅgam iti nyāyāt  śāstra aṅgām eva idam na bhāṣya aṅgam iti mantavyam na hi bhāṣyasya svātantryeṇa mukhyam prayojanam asti yena vārttikam tad aṅga tām iyāt tasmāt  yathāśruti sundaram iti nanu karmendriya niyamaḥ śama iti su prasiddham śāntaḥ  dānta ityādi upaniṣatsu na ca asau puruṣa arthaḥ atas  na mukhyam prayojanam iti ata āha atra ca iti nanu jagataḥ śamāya iti durghaṭam asaṃbhāvitā tvāt aśakyā tvāt ca na tāvat  kaścid  jagat upacikīrṣuḥ kvacid  pravartate yatas  muneḥ api tathā tvam saṃbhāvayāmaḥ paṭhanti ca muneḥ api vanasthasya ityādi na ca śakyam etad  bubhukṣūṇām pravartayitum aśakyatvāt  na ca jagat eva mumukṣati tasmāt anuṣṭhātā eva vyutpādyaḥ śāstra antara labdha brāhmaṇatva dirūpaḥ śiṣyaḥ tasya ca rūpāṇi śama dama ādi saṃpattiḥ nitya anitya vivekaḥ aihikā muṣmika bhāga vairāgyam mumukṣu tā ca iti yaḥ tu anadhikārī eva pravartate karma kāṇḍa iva brahma kāṇḍe sa na phala bhāj  bhavati tatra etad  syāt  na tāvat upeya viṣayeyam adhikāra cintā tasya puruṣa prayatna aviṣaya tvāt iṣyamāṇa tā mātrasya ca aniṣadhāt  kim nāma upāya viṣayā tasya eva śāstra viṣaya tvāt  puruṣa pravṛtti viṣaya tvāt ca iha ca apavarga iva tad artha tayā tattva jñānam api upeyam eva asiddha tvāt  upāyaḥ tu pramāṇam na ca veda adhyayanavat anumānasya pratyakṣasya ca upādānam śūdra ādikam prati niṣiddham yena tatra api etasya anadhikāraḥ syāt  tathā sati dhūmāt api vahim adhigacchan pratyakṣāt  vā pratyavāyī syāt  adhīyāna iva vedam na ca ātma gocare pratyakṣa anumāne śūdra ādeḥ viśeṣataḥ niṣiddhe snātasya caṇḍāla darśanam iva brāhmaṇa ādeḥ prāyaścitta anupadeśāt pratyuta striyaḥ  vaiśyāḥ tathā śūdrā ye ca anye pāpa yonayaḥ ityādi smṛteḥ adhikāra eva avasīyate tasmāt  yathā sa eva viśiṣṭaḥ svargaḥ  vaidika yāga ādi anadhikṛtena api upāya antareṇa traivarṇika śuśrūṣā ādinā sādhyate tathā upāya anteṇa anumāna ādinā yadi ātma adhigamaḥ kriyate śūdreṇa api tadā kīdṛśaḥ  doṣaḥ satyam kim tu anumānam api āgama avirodhena anusandhīyamānam atha niścāyakam na tu tad viruddham api yad āha yad tu pratyakṣa āgama viruddham nyāya ābhāsaḥ saḥ iti sa ca āgama avirodhāt avirodha niścayaḥ tad artha niścaya adhīnaḥ tatra ca anadhikṛta eva ayam śūdrāti tad nirapekṣaḥ tu anumāna mātra śaraṇaḥ  nara śiraḥ pāvitrya ādivat anartham eva samāsādayet  tasmāt āgama eka vākya tayā pravṛtte śāstre tad adhikārī eva adhikārī iti śūdra ādayaḥ  anadhikṛtā iva atas  yāvat adhikāri paraḥ  ayam jagat śabda iti kecid  tatra āha parama kārūṇikaḥ  hi iti santi eva hi kecid  karuṇā mṛdu manasaḥ  yeṣām jagat eva mitram anyathā bhūtā iva u abhayam dattvā iti vidhi vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ niṣkāraṇam eva para duḥkha prahāṇa icchā kāruṇyam sā ca yathā ekam duḥkhita paśyataḥ  bhavati tathā jagat eva duḥkhita paśyataḥ kim na syāt  bhavati ced  tad prahāṇa upāya pravṛttau kā nāma anupapattiḥ nanu karuṇā ārdra hṛdayaḥ  api am vyutpisum eva vyutpādayet na tu viparītam na hi badhireṣu gāyanaḥ  gāyati iti ata āha tatra yadi na kaścid iti na hi rogī mandabhāgya tayā caraka ādi upadeśe na pravartata iti tad artha tā tasya nivartata iti arthaḥ nanu anadhikṛta vyutpādane pratyavāya mātrakam apaśyan  ayam katham avadheya vacanaḥ syāt  paśyan vā na pravarteta kāruṇika tayā paśyan  api pravartate ced  pramādī syāt  tathā ca para lokāt abibhyataḥ  asya vacane kaḥ śraddhā asyati ityata āha na ca iti yadi api prahīna moha tvāt eva asya pāpa puṇyayoḥ utpattiḥ eva na asti vakṣyati hi na pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya hīna kleśasya iti tathā api kleśa hāneḥ durūha tvāt  pratyavāya utpattim abhyupagamya tad abhāvāya tapaḥ prabhāva uktaḥ nanu evam api prakṣālanāt hi paṅkasya dūrāt asparśanam varam iti ata āha tathā ca iti na hi gāḥ paṅka magnāḥ paṅka pralepa bhayāt anukampā paravaśāḥ samarthā na uddharanti api tu uddhṛtya paḍkam prakṣālayanti iti arthaḥ nanu yadi anadhikṛtaḥ katham phala bhāgī tathā ced  katham anadhikṛta iti abhisandhāya uktam prapañcayati tapaḥ prabhāva eva hi iti yathā hi teṣām tapaḥ prabhāvāt evaṃvidhāḥ pāpmānaḥ  vilīyante tathā tapaḥ prabhāvāt eva satya saṃkalpa tayā anadhikāriṇaḥ  api phala bhāgina iti na kaścid  virodhaḥ na ca phala apekṣayā teṣām anadhikāraḥ kim tarhi karma apekṣayā anadhikṛtena tu kṛtam karma viguṇam sanna phalāṃya paryāptam iti api na viśiṣṭa yājaka sāt guṇyāt eva tasya paripūrṇa tvāt  yājaka eva tvayā ājyam yājayan pratyavāyam āsādayet  rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇan  iva vidvān sa ca tīvra tadeṇa tapasā eva vilīyata iti arthaḥ tarhi mahājanaḥ  yena gataḥ sa panthāḥ iti nyāyena vayam api anadhikṛtān vyutpādayāma iti ata āha na ca iti nanu ku tārkikāṇām ajñānam nivartayatā kim anena śāstrasya upakṛtam syāt iti āha ku tārkikaiḥ iti ajñānam asamyak jñānam iha karma ārambhe prārabdhasya antarāya viraheṇa parisamāpti kāmayamānā abhīṣṭa devatā namaskāra pūrvakam prekṣāvantaḥ pravartante dṛśyate ca tatra tatra bahuśoṃ vyabhicāraḥ kṛta namaskārasya api samīhita asiddheḥ viparītasya api samīhita siddhaḥ viparītasya api samīhita asiddheḥ na ca atra vṛṣṭi kāmaḥ kārīrī nirvapet  itivat  prārabdha parisamāpti kāmaḥ  devatām namaskuryāt iti śrutiḥ asti yena vyabhicore api karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyam kalpayāmaḥ tasmāt ar tha kāma iha vaṭe prativasantam yakṣam pūjayet itiva daprāmāṇika prasiddhi vijṛmbhitam etad iti abhisandhāya kim u na kṛtaḥ  vāttika kṛtā iṣṭadevatā namaskāra iti ata āha avigīta iti pratyakṣam iva avigīta śiṣṭa ācāraḥ  api śruti sadbhāve pramāṇam eva nirmūlasya ca śiṣṭa ācārasya asambhavāt apramāṇa mūlakasya ca prāmāṇika vigāna viraha anupapatteḥ tathā ca satyabhāvaḥ karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyam avalambate asati ca bhāvaḥ janmāntarīya su kṛta saṃpattim anvaya vyatireka abhāva darśanam tvāgama itara pramāṇa gocaram kārya kāraṇa bhāvam apākaroti iti arthaḥ yad yavam kim anena na kṛta iti ata āha parama iti yadi kṛtaḥ tad  kim indraluptena gataḥ yena na dṛśyata iti ata āha na niveśita iti atra eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ  na khalu iti na khalu iṣṭa devatā namaskāravat tad niveśanam api kvacid upayujyata iti arthaḥ nanu evaṃbhūtam śiṣṭa ācāram śiṣyā api grāhayitavyāḥ na ca tad niveśana vyatirekeṇa te grāhitāḥ syuḥ iti ata āha maṅgalya antaravat iti tatra iti śāstre vyākhyātavye nanu daṇḍaka sūtrasya anuvādaḥ  na asti iti ata uktam saṃkṣepata iti nanu ādi sūtra tvam asya su prasiddham eva abhisaṃbandha vākya tvāt  tad kim anena udīritena ityata āha ādi grahaṇena iti nanu śāstra niḥśreyasayoḥ anena saṃbandhaḥ  varṇyate tatas  saṃbandha vākyam idam iti yuktam abhistu kimartham iti ata āha abhimata iti asti hi śāstra niḥśreyasayoḥ vācya vāyaka bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ  api saṃbandhaḥ na ca asau  iha abhimtaḥ prekṣāvat pravṛtti anaṅga tvāt na hi vācakāt  vācya pratīteḥ vācyasya niṣpattiḥ yatas  mumukṣuḥ vācake pravartatām upāye tu upeya arthaḥ  pravartate tena hetu hetumat bhāva eva vivakṣita iti arthaḥ nanu na atra śāstram tasya niḥśreyasa hetu tvam vā śrūyata iti ata āha pramāṇa ādi iti rūḍha padātikrame kim tātparyam ityata āha na hi iti yadi api śiṣyate anuśiṣyate pramāṇa ādi kam anena iti śāstram iti vyutpattyā atra api kāraṇa tā gamyate tathā api śāsaka saṃbaddha vyāpāravat tayā na tu śiṣya saṃbaddha vyāpāravat tayā sā ca iha vivakṣitā anyathā pramāṇa ādīni tattvataḥ  jñātvā api tāvat na mucyate yāvat na anuśiṣyāt iti tad idam uktam padārtha tattva avagama karaṇa tayā iti na svarūpeṇa iti ca nanu hetutva karaṇa tve na viṣaya bhedena bhavitum arhata iti ata āha tena iti ubhayoḥ api hetuḥ śāstram karaṇam ca kim tu padārtha tattve jñāpakatayā niḥśreyase tad vyāpāravataḥ karaṇa tayā iti arthaḥ tad idam uktam tathā ca iti evam ca sati śāstrasya niḥśreyase karttavye padārtha tattva jñānasya nirūkti balena vyāpāra tve darśite vyāpāra vyāpāriṇoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāravatā śāstreṇa vyāpāra viṣayasya pramāṇa ādeḥ pratipādya pratipādaka bhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāra viṣayeṇa pramāṇa ādinā vyāpārasya tattva jñānasya viṣaya viṣayībhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāreṇa tattva jñānena vyāpārulasya niḥśreyasasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tathā vyāpāra viṣaya phalayoḥ hetu hetumat bhāvaḥ saṃbandha sūcitaḥ  na antarīyaka tvāt na hi atad hetukaḥ tad vacā pāraḥ  nāma na api atat karma tad vacā pāra viṣayaḥ na api tad phalān anuguṇaḥ tad vacā pāraḥ tad vacā pāra viṣayaḥ  vā iti pajcasu vaktavyeṣu upalakṣaṇa artham dvayam āha śāstra pramāṇāt iti enam eva vyutpatti labhyam vyāpāram abhipretya tattvasya jñānam iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī bhāṣya kāreṇa darśitā iti na karaṇa vyutpattiḥ virūddhā nanu śiṣya ācārya śāstra tad vyākhyānānām api saṃbandhāḥ kaiścid  samāna tāntrikaiḥ pradarśitāḥ te kasmāt na pradarśyante iti ata āha tad idam abhidheyā iti na hrāsti iti etāvat mātreṇa eva pradarśanīyam kim nāma yāvatī apratipādite prekṣāvat pravṛttiḥ na syāt  tāvat  pradarśyate na ca śiṣya ācārya ādi saṃbandhāḥ prekṣāvat pravṛtti aṅgam teṣām pravṛtti phala tvāt  pravṛtti uttara kālam hi śiṣyaḥ pratipādyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ca ācāryaḥ śāstram vyākhyeyam vyākhyātā ca sa ityādi sidhyati na ca śāstra ācārya ādīnām svarūpa pratipādanam api upayujyate pramāṇa antara siddha tvāt tasmāt  prayojanam abhidhayam tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ  abhidheyaḥ tad dvārā śāstrasya prayojanena saṃbandha iti etad arthatva ime prathama sūtrasya nyāyyam iti arthaḥ nanu yasya mithyājñānam saṃsāram pratanoti tasya eva tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa hetuḥ ātmā ca tathā tad anyeṣām tu śāstra abhidheyānām api na niḥśreyasa hetu tvam tathā ca na niḥśreyasa saṃbandhaḥ iti ata āha yad padārtha iti nanu pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva jñānasya yadi niḥśreyasa hetu tā śāstra pravṛtteḥ pūrvam eva pramāṇa siddhā niṣprayojanam śāstre prayojana abhidhānam māna antara siddhe upadeśa anapekṣaṇāt  atha ita eva tad niścayaḥ  dusttaram itaretara āśraya tvam pravṛttaḥ  hi prayojanam niścinuyāt  niścita prayojanaḥ ca pravarteta na ca pravṛtteḥ prāk eva muni vacanāt niścinoti prathama sūtra eva prayojanā niścayena pravṛtti anupapatteḥ tatra api ca pravṛtti artham prayojana antara abhidhāne anavasthā tad aniśvaye api ādyā pravṛttiḥ ced  uttarottara pravṛttau  api tathātva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt  prayojana ādi abhidhānam anarthakam iti kecid  tad anupapannam tridhā hi puṃsām citta vṛttayaḥ anubhava icchā prayatnaḥ ca iti tatra anubhavaḥ  na icchām anuvidhatte aniṣṭasya api upalabdheḥ icchā tu puruṣa arthe svarasa utthitā tad sādhane ca tathā tvā anumāna utthāpyā prayatnaḥ tu sādhana viṣaya eva tatra sādhana gocara āviccha prayatnau ādyā pravṛttiḥ iti ucyate na tu anubhavaḥ phala gocarā vā icchā pravṛttiḥ cena tayoḥ api prayojana niścaya apekṣā syāt  na hi upekṣaṇīyam niṣprayojanam iti na anubhūyate na api sukham prayojana antara śūnyakiti na iṣyate na api mumukṣuṇā anapekṣite svarge yāga ādikam tad sādhana tayā na anubhūyate puruṣa artha sādhane tu icchā lakṣaṇā vā prayatna lakṣaṇā vā pravṛttiḥ na svarasa siddhā na hi kaścid  kṣudhī duḥkha prahāṇam tṛpti sauhitya sukha vā ananusaṃdhāya anna mattum icchati prayatate vā tasmāt  yatra yaḥ pravartayitavyaḥ sa tad sādhyam artham daśayitvā yatas ca yaḥ  nivartayitavyaḥ sa tad sādhyam anartham darśayitvā iti uktam pracojana ādikam tad tu śrotā katham śraddhāsyati aśraddadhānaḥ  vā katham pravartsyati iti avaśiṣyate tatra āha viniścitā iti yadi api muneḥ āptatva avadhāraṇe prayojana anabhidhāne api prayojana sāmānya niścayaḥ  bhavati eva prayojanavat idam śāstram āpta ukta tvāt iti tathā api na asau pravṛtti aṅgam na hi prayojanavat iti eva pravartate kim tarhi asmad apekṣita prayojanavat idam iti kṛtvā sa ca prayojana viśeṣaḥ  vacanāt eva avasīyata iti sārthakam etad abhidhānam tad idam uktam prayojana ādi viniścitya viśeṣata iti śeṣaḥ viniścayaḥ ca śāstra upāyakam eva idam niḥśreyasam iti ākāraḥ  na tu avaśyaṃbhā vi prayojana ākāraḥ kṛṣi ādau  avagraha ādivat atra api antarāya saṃbhavāt tad idam prayojanasya pravartaka tvam uddeśya tayā na tu pravṛtti viṣaya tayā tena na iṣṭa abhyupāyatā vidhi virodhaḥ nanu muneḥ āptatva aniścaye kim tad vacane pravṛttiḥ na asti eva tathā sati tasya āptatva niścayaḥ  api katham iti ata āha āptatva aniścaye tu artha saṃśayāt  śāstra sādhyatayā iti śeṣaḥ nanu saṃśayān asya katham prekṣāvataḥ pravṛttiḥ iti āha na khalu iti yadi api ca sasya adhigamasya kṛṣi ādi sādhya tayā saṃśayaḥ  na asti tathā api bhaviṣyat tayā asti eva tathā api tam uddiśya prekṣāvantaḥ pravartante yathā ca tatra śata eka aṃśikaḥ phala abhāvaḥ phalakoṭistu utkaṭā tathā atra api na hi indriyā pāta jaḥ  ayam saṃśayaḥ kim nāma āptatva aviniścaya hetukā prāmāṇya śaḍkyā samākṛṣṭaḥ vastutas tu sūtrāt  prayojana ādi niścaya ākāram eva vijñānam iti arthaḥ nanu saṃśayaḥ prayojana ādi vākya abhāve api sulabhaḥ viśeṣa smṛtiḥ tu arthitva viśeṣāt  bhaviṣyati iti āha na ca iti yad vacanena hi yaḥ pravartate sa tad vacanāt eva viśeṣa smṛtim apekṣate na svātantryeṇa na hi roga ārtaḥ  mama idam roga nivṛtti sādhanam bhavet na vā iti yatra tatra ucchṛḍkhalaḥ svayam utprekṣya pravartate kim nāma anavadhṛta āpta tvasya api vaidyasya eva vacanāt  anyathā tvayam prayojana abhidhānam anadhigacchan anartham api āśaṅketa kim niṣprayojanam idam kāka danta parīkṣā granthavat uta aśakya sādhana prayojanam mṛtyu hara hima mahīdhara uttarasā anusiddha saṃjīvanī kathanavat atha anabhimata prayojanam āryāvarta nivāsinam prati dākṣiṇāti asya mātula kanyakā pariṇaya prakrama upadeśavat atha abhimatasya api śakyasya api prayojanasya laghīyasi upāya antare sati api guruḥ ayam upāyaḥ pipāsum prati gīrvāṇa taraḍgiṇī tīra samīpa kūpa khanana upadeśavat etāsu ca anartha saṃbhāvanāsu na pravartate na ca prayojana abhidhāne api etāsām avakāśaḥ loka vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt  na hi kaścid  vaidya vacanāt eva mā śaḍkya nivartate yathā svayam utprekṣya iti bhāvaḥ tad anarthakam niṣprayojanam iti arthaḥ aśakya anuṣṭhāna tvam upāyasya asiddham iti ata āha tathā hi iti iha dvividhaḥ pramāṇa śabdasya arthaḥ pramīyate anena iti ca pramāṇam pramitiḥ pramāṇam iti ca tatra prathamam adhikṛtya uktam prameya ādīnām tattva jñānam pramāṇa tattva jñāna adhīnam iti nanu idindrayā ādīnām ajñāyamānānām eva sva viṣaya pariccheda janaka tvam paśyan  api katham evam brūyāt iti ata āha na hi iti pramāṇa tvena ajñāyamānam pramāṇam sva viṣayam paricchinatti na tu avadhārayati tad ca iha vivakṣitam iti arthaḥ kim iti na avadhārayati na hindriyam ajñāyamānam aniścaya ākāram eva jñānam janayati iti ata āha tāvat mātrasya iti yadi api niścaya ākāram eva jñānam ādhatte tathā api tathābhūtasya eva bhūyaḥ bhūyas  prameya virahaḥ labdheḥ viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ca saṃdehaḥ tad avaskandati iti arthaḥ tad kim kvacid api avadhāraṇam na asti eva tathā sati toyam eva idam ityādikaḥ  laukikaḥ pratyayaḥ tathā pūrva pakṣiṇaḥ kvacid api viniścayaḥ  na asti eva iti ādikaḥ ca abhimānaḥ  viruddhi etetyata āha api tu iti yadi kvacid  prameya tattva avadhāraṇam parama arthaḥ tadā pramāṇa tattva avadhāraṇa dvāreṇa eva pramāra antareṇa tu bhavat na pāramārthikam iti arthaḥ bodhaka tvam bodha janaka tvam bodha janana avacchinnā sattā iti yāvat  avyabhicāri tvam aviparīta anubhava janaka tvam aviparīta anubhava janana avacchi nnā sattā iti yāvat  evam ca upadhi dvaya avacchinnāyāḥ sattāyā upādhi bhedāt  bhinnāyā iva ekasmin  arthe samavāyaḥ kṛtakatva anitya tvayoḥ iva na viruddhaḥ tena avyabhicāri tvena jñāyamānena iti śeṣaḥ pramāṇya avadhāraṇam tarhi kkopayujyata iti ata āha tad eva hi iti pramāṇam hi pramākaraṇam na ca karaṇatva ādayaḥ sāmānya viśeṣāḥ santi sāmānya saṃkara prasaṅgāt  kim nāma sādhakatama tvam eva karaṇa tvam tad viśeṣakaḥ tu kriyā viśeṣa eva sa ca atra pramā lakṣaṇaḥ pramā ca aviparīta upalabdhiḥ atas  aviparīta anubhava janakatva lakṣaṇam avyabhicāri tvam eva prāmāṇyam iti arthaḥ yadi evam tad avadhāraṇa pūrvakam eva prameya ādi avadhāraṇam astu iti ata āha tad ca iti pramākaraṇa tvam hi na anavadhāritāyām pramāyām avadhārayitum śakyam iti arthaḥ tarhi pramātvam eva avadhāryatām na hi tad api aupādhikam yena upādhi anavadhāraṇe na eva avadhāryeta ityata āha tathā hi iti vijñānasya pramāyāḥ prāmāṇyam pramātvam svatas  veti asya sva ātmanā vā sva grāhakeṇa vā iti arthaḥ tatra prathamam dūṣayati na khalu iti dharma dharmiṇa uḥ abheda pakṣe anātma saṃvedanam iti etad eva dūṣaṇam āna ātma saṃvedana tā ca upapādayiṣyata iti hṛdayam bheda pakṣe prāk eva iti yaḥ  hi yad  gṛhṇāti sa tad dharmam api gṛhṇīyāt iti saṃbhāvyeta api yaḥ tu dharmiṇam eva na akalayati tasya dharma grahaṇa vārtā api kva yadi api ca śabda gandhādayaḥ  vyoma bhūmi ādya grahe api gṛhyante tathā api na tad dharmatayā iti arthaḥ sva grāhakeṇa vā iti dūṣayati na api iti tad hi mānasam vā syāt  laiḍgikam vā ubhayam api manasaḥ  jñāta tā lakṣaṇāt  liṅgāt  vā aviśiṣṭāt  jāyamānam katham iva tad ābhāsa viśiṣṭam gṛhṇīyat  viṣaya viśeṣāt  tu tathā tve apramāṇyasya api svata eva grahaṇa prasaṅgāt  tatra api viṣaya vaiśiṣṭa casya sattvāt  pramāyāḥ prāyika tayā tad vāsanāyāḥ samutkaṭa tvāt apramā api samutkaṭa tvāt apramā api pramā iti eva gṛhyate tatas  bādhaka adhīnam eva aprāmāṇyam āsaṃjita rajata tāyām iva śuktikāyām śuktikā tvam iti yadi tathā api āsaṃjakasya api yadi āsaṃjaka tvam avagatam katham na svatas  aprāmāṇya grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tatra api prāmāṇya ārope tu katham na anavasthā na ca kṛtrimam rūpam aparibhūya grahaṇam grahaṇām iti ucyate saṃśayena abhibhūta tvāt  māyā liḍgini jhaṭiti parivrājaka buddhivat  tasmāt  jñānam gṛhyata eva iti eva na yadi tu daivāt  gṛhyate tadā jñānam iti eva  na tu pramāṇam apramāṇam vā iti arthaḥ nanu yadi svīyāt  svata iti na nirvahati vakṣyamāṇena ca nyāyena na api paratas  asti ca ayam pramāṇa apramāṇa pravibhāga vyavahāraḥ  niḥśaṅkaḥ tatas  sva saṃvedana naya eva astu tena hi ayam nirvahet  na hi tatra kiñcid anavasthā ādikam paśyāma iti ata āha etena iti sva saṃvedananayaḥ  hi na tāvat  pramāṇa siddhaḥ kadācid  pramāṇa vyavahāra sauṣṭhavāt  svīkriyeta api yadi ayam tena nirvahet  na tu etad asti yathā hi pramāṇam sva ātmānam gṛhṇat  prāmāṇyam api gṛhṇāti tathā tad ābhāsam api tad ābhāsatva gṛhṇīyāt  tathā ca sarva mithyā jñānāt  apravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ na ca tatra api pramāṇi āropāt  pravṛttiḥ sva ātma bhūtasya apramāṇi asya svasa vedana tayā grahaṇe samāropa asaṃbhāvāt  agrahaṇe vā sva saṃvedana naya anupapatteḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt  svarūpa grahaṇe api na aprāmāṇya rūpa dharma grahaṇam iti yadi tadā prāmāṇyasya api agrahaṇam syāt  tasmāt  sva saṃvedana naye api sva rūpa vedana mātram syāt  na tu prāmāṇya ādi vedanam iti arthaḥ paratas  vā iti dūṣayati na api iti tad gocaram tad gocara gocaram madhya pada lopāt  prātyakṣike ca vahni jñāne prātyakṣikam eva vahni jñāna antaram iti yāvat  tad ca dvividham samāna indriya jam indriya antara jam ca evam anumāne api anumāna jñāna antaram tad liṅga jam liṅga antara jam ca evam śābde api śābda jñāna anantaram tad āpta śabda jam āpta antara śabda jam ca iti samāna jātīya saṃvādaḥ  darśitaḥ artha kriyā ityādinā kārya liṅgakam tad gocara ityādinā ca akārya kāraṇa liṅgakam anumāna trayam vijājīya saṃvāda rūpam darśitam upalakṣaṇam ca etad  āpta upadeśa jam api saṃvādakam jñānam bhavati eva jñānam bhavati eva saḥ  ayam pramāṇye niścetavye saṃvādaḥ  yadi api vyadhikaraṇaḥ tathapi artha tathā tvam ava dhārayan  arthavat tvam pravartakasya api avadhārayati iti etāvatā tathā eva upavarṇitaḥ dūṣayati tad ca sarvam iti evam pramātu asya duradhigama tvam āpādya tad āyatta avadhāraṇe pramāṇānām pramāṇa tve yojayati yadā ca iti nanu yadi prāmāṇya avadhāraṇena eva pravṛttiḥ tadā sā eva sārvalaukikī svata ityādi vikalpān phalgūkariṣyati atha tad avadhāraṇa vyatirekeṇa api pravṛttiḥ apratyūhā tadā mā avadhāri prāmāṇyam kim naḥ chinnam ityata āha tad evam iti vaidikam vyavahāram adhikṛtya ca idam śāstram pravṛttam na laukikam iti abhisandhiḥ prakṛte yojayati tasmāt iti nanu nitya yoge matubh iti durghaṭam pramāṇa arthayoḥ eva anitya tvāt paraspara samavāya bhāvāt ca ityata āha nitya tā ca iti nanu avyabhicāraḥ  api vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ pramāṇa prameyayoḥ na asti iti ata āha iyam eva ca iti saḥ  ayam avisaṃvadādaḥ  visaṃvāda abhāvaḥ  avyabhicāra lakṣaṇam avyabhicāra svarūpam tu lakṣya bhūtam bhūta artha paricchedaka tvam lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ abhinna āśraya tvāt avyabhicāra svarūpam tu lakṣya bhūtam bhūta artha paricchedaka tvam lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ abhinna āśraya tvāt sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti mantavyam yadi api deśa avasthā bhede kāla bhedaḥ  api artha siddhaḥ tathā api yathā kathañcit kāla bheda mātram vivakṣitam atra iti jñāpana artham tad grahaṇam tathā hi dūra sthe sthāṇau puruṣarpatyayasya kāla antare api visaṃvādaḥ  na asti yāvat  na pratipattā nikaṭa sthaḥ  bhavati pratyetavya eva vā yāvat na nediṣṭhaḥ syāt  evam svapna avasthāyām artha pratyayasya kāla bhede api tāvat na visaṃvādaḥ  yāvat na jāgara avasthā anubhavaḥ na ca vācyam evam sati kim kāla bheda grahaṇena iti deśa avasthayā uḥ abhede api kāla krameṇa api kvacid  visaṃvāda darśanāt  yathā su nipuṇa nibhāla nāt āpāta jātasya kāma ātura kāminī jñānasya bhede api kvacid  kāla antare visaṃvādāt  tad upagrahaḥ tad anena indriya ādīnām kāla krama bhāvinaḥ sahakāri bhedāḥ sphuṭatara pratīti hetavaḥ sarva eva saṃgṛhītāḥ yadi api ca pramāra viṣayau  eva visaṃvāda avisaṃvādau saṃbhava vyabhicāra lakṣaṇau tathā api avisaṃvādasya dhruva viṣayatva pratipādana artham svarūpa grahaṇam sarvasya jñānasya dharmiṇī avisaṃvādāt iti pravṛtti sāmarthyāt iti vyadhikāraṇaḥ  hetuḥ atas tad artham āha samartha pravṛtti janaka tvāt iti yadi api samartha pravṛtti tvād iti uktesamañjasam tathā api pravṛttiḥ yasya iti sambandhe ṣaṣṭhī sa ca pramāṇa pravṛttyoḥ janya janaka bhāva eva iti sa eva darśitaḥ nanu na tāvat  pramāṇi asamartha pravṛtti janakatvayoḥ avinābhāvaḥ pratyakṣeṇa śakya grahaḥ tayoḥ eva apratyakṣa tvāt  prāmāṇyam hi samartha pravṛtti janakatva anumeyam tad ca anvaya vyatireka anumeyam eva iti na api anumānena anvaya grahaḥ prāmāṇyasya kvacid api asiddheḥ siddhau vā kim anumānena anumā anantara siddha tve tu anavasthā eva ityata āha yadi punar iti atra ca upekṣā jñānānām pakṣa tvena anupādānāt na bhāga asiddhiḥ vyatirekī ca sarvatra sa pakṣa abhāvam abhyupetya pravartata iti nāsādharaṇa anaikāntika tā na ca vācyam etasya eva anumānasya arthavattva anavadhāraṇe katham pramāṇānām arthavattva siddhiḥ tad avadhāraṇe vā katham kevala vyatireki tvam iti dvividham hi anumānasya arthavat tvam avinābhāva lakṣaṇam pramā janana lakṣaṇam ca tatra sva viṣaya paricchede kartavye avinā abhāva avadhāraṇam eva apekṣate na pramākaraṇatva avadhāraṇam iti anavaghṛta prāmāṇyena eva anena pramāṇānām pramāṇa phalatva lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam sādhyata iti sarvam sundaram etena etad api nirastam yad  prāmāṇya anavadhāraṇe aprāmāṇya anavadhāraṇam api katham prāmāṇya niścayena hi tad  niścīyate tad anavadhāraṇe tu vyatireka niścayaḥ  api katham vipakṣasya tathā tvā niścayāt iti svarūpataḥ  dharmataḥ ca anavadhāritena eva satā pramāṇena sva viṣaya niścaya siddheḥ nanu na asti eva asau vādī yaḥ prāmāṇya aniścaye api vipratipadyeta na hi prāmāṇyam svīkṛtya tad niścaye vipratipattiḥ svīkārasya niścaya mūla tvāt  na ca asvīkṛtya pramāṇa śūnya vipratipatteḥ sarvatra sulabha tayā sarva vāda vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra vilopa prasaṅgāt  aniścite ca prāmāṇye tad atad rūpa saṃdehaḥ  api kvacid  durlabhaḥ viśeṣa smṛteḥ abhāvāt  tad pūrvaka tvāt ca sarva saṃśayānām na api sarvatra aprāmāṇyāsañjanam prāmāṇya grahaṇa upāya nirākaraṇasya aprāmāṇye api tulya tvāt  vikalpa nirmitam avicāra manoharam prāmāṇya ādikam ādāya api na asya durvicārasya nirvāhaḥ prāmāṇya anabhyupagame vikalpa nirmāṇasya api asiddheḥ na ca vikalpa nirmite na saṃśaya ādi vyavahāraḥ samasti na hi vāji viṣāṇam vā iti kaścid  sandigdhe na api nara viṣāṇam iti kasyacid  viparyayaḥ tasmāt asti prāmāṇya ādikam tad niścayaḥ ca tad upāyaḥ tu cintām arhati evam ca anvayaḥ  asti eva tad  katham kevala vyatireki anumānam iti āśaḍkya saṃpratipatti rūttaram anvayavyatirekī vā iti kevala vyatireki vādaḥ tu anvaya anabhyupagamena kṛta iti abhisandhiḥ anumānasya iti upalakṣaṇam svata iti ca tad itarasya api svatas  paratas ca prāmāṇya siddheḥ iti nanu samartha pravṛtti janaka tvāt iti etāvatā eva sādhya siddheḥ pramāṇator atha pratipattau  iti samartha viśeṣaṇam vayadhi karaṇa cetyata āha pravṛtti janaka tvam tu iti prāmāṇya ādi abhidhāna dvārā hi śāstrasya niḥśreyasena saṃgatiḥ na tu sva rūpeṇa tatas  yathā pramāṇa ādi tattva jñānam sādhya tayā prayojanam pratijñāyate tathā pramāṇa ādi abhidheya tayā api pratijñeyam bhavati yathā atha atas  dharma vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti dharmasya vyākhyeya tvena eva pratijñā samānatantre na ca tad abhidheya tā pratijñānam atra tasmāt abhidheyattva apratijñānāt na pramāṇa ādayaḥ śāstreṇa abhidhīyanta iti śrotṛ buddha canurodhena aśaḍkya sūtra kāra hṛdaya anurodhena vārttikam uttarayati syāt etad iti śiṣyā kāṅkṣā krameṇa hi śāstram idam pravṛttam anapekṣita abhidhāne anavadheyatva prasaṅgāt  na ca śiṣyā kāṅkṣā kim vakṣyati bhavān iti kim tu niḥśreyasam kutaḥ adhigamyata iti tatra uttaram pramāṇa ādi tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigama iti tatas  katham iti tatas  ke kati kiṃlakṣaṇāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ iti tatra uddeśa vibhāga lakṣaṇāni iti tatas  katham iti tatra dvitīya ādhyāya ādi iti etad ca sarvam anubhava siddham na atra api vacana apekṣā ukta āboddhāram prati tu vyākhyātāraḥ  bhavanti yata evam aya māhā iti tad anubhava siddham api pramāṇa ādi abhidhāyaka tvam yaḥ kutaścid  vyāmohāt na pratipadyate tam prati vyākhyātā śāstrasya puruṣa śreyaḥ  abhidhāyaka tvāt iti āha iti arthaḥ nanu śreyaḥ  abhidhāna mātreṇa api na pramāṇa ādi abhidhānam sidhyati na hi pramāṇa ādi padārthā eva śreyaḥ atha svayam eva vivarīṣyati tad padārthāḥ pramāṇa ādaya iti tathā api tad śāstram śreyaḥ  abhidhatta iti anene kim atha śreyaḥ śabdasya pramāṇa ādaya eva arthaḥ tarhi śreyaḥ punar  sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ iti kim iti ata āha yadi api iti yadi api śāstra punar  puruṣaḥ punar  śreyaḥ punar iti pratipadam gṛhītvā vivaraṇam prakṣayeṇa iti antena sphuṭa avabhāsam na ca puruṣā rāgādimanta iti ādau  api vivaraṇatva aśaḍkā prakṛtena asaṃbandhāt na hi rāga ādimantam prati śāstram na sa sādhanam śreyaḥ  abhidhatte na ca tam prati na tad  śreyaḥ  yena vīta rāgaḥ  vivicya gṛhyatām tathā api tasmāt  tad  śāstram puruṣa śreyaḥ  abhidhatta iti madhya patita upasaṃhāra eva vivaraṇa viccheda bhramaḥ  mā bhūt iti etad artham avacchinatti upabhogāt  prakṣayeṇa iti antena iti nanu samūhaḥ  vyūha viśiṣṭa iti asaṃgatam paryāyatvāt ityata āha vyūha iti te khalu amī samūhāḥ praṇetṛ puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ sva artha anurodhinaḥ  vetyata āha eka smṛti iti yadi api ekārtha pratipādana avacchinnā varṇāḥ padam iti etāvat eva lakṣaṇam tathā api etad eva lakṣaṇam kṣaṇa bhaḍgurāṇām katham iti etad uktam eka smṛti samārūḍhā iti samūhaḥ padam iti vārttike śeṣaḥ pada samūhaḥ sūtram iti vārttikam tad ca anupapannam vākya viśeṣaḥ  hi sūtram na ca vākya sāmānyam api pada samūha mātram gauraḥ caḥ puruṣaḥ  hastī ityādeḥ api vākyatva prasaṅgāt ityata āha evam sva artha iti samūhaḥ  veditavyaḥ sūtra tvena iti śeṣaḥ sūtra samūhaḥ prakaraṇam iti vārttikam tatra ca ava antara samūha bhede kāraṇa abhāvāt śāstram eva sūtra samūha rūpam prakaraṇam iti prāptam iti ata āha evam kvacid iti tad yathā prayojana abhidheya saṃbandha pratipādanam ekam artham adhikṛtya prathama dvitīya sūtrayoḥ samūhaḥ prakaraṇam evam pramāṇa prakaraṇam prameya prakaraṇam nyāya pūrva aṅga prakaraṇam nyāya āśraya prakaraṇam nyāya āśraya prakaraṇam nyāya svarūpa prakaraṇam nyāya uttarāṅga prakaraṇam iti ādyūhyam prakaraṇa samūhaḥ ca āhnikam iti vārttikam tad idam prakaraṇānām avāntara eka vākyatāyām asatyām na sidhyati iti ata āha prakaraṇānām iti asti hi amīṣām prakaraṇānām sa parikara nyāya lakṣaka tvam ekam iti tad samūha āhnikam uttarasmiḥ ca āhnike nyāya nyāya ābhāsa viveka upāya lakṣaṇam ekam tatra api kathā prakaraṇam hetvābhāsa prakaraṇam chala prakaraṇam puruṣa aśakti liṅga prakaraṇam iti evam prathame lakṣaṇa madhyāya arthaḥ dvitīye pramāṇa parīkṣā tṛtīye kāraṇa rūpa prameya ṣaṭka parīkṣā caturthe kārya rūpa prameya ṣaṭka parīkṣā pañcame puruṣa aśakti liṅga viśeṣa lakṣaṇam iti evam dvitīya adhyāyāt au  āhnika prakaraṇa saṃgatīḥ tatra eva darśayiṣyāmaḥ tad idam uktam evam tatra tatra veditavyam iti tatra tatra iti āhika ādau  iti arthaḥ nanu ca tatra eka prakāraḥ  api na darśitaḥ katham tatra tatra veditavyam ityata āha etāḥ ca iti nanu śāstrasya sa sādhana puruṣa śreyaḥ  abhidhāyaka tvam pratijñāya śāstra svarūpa darśanam kkopayujyata iti ata āha tad evam iti śāstra svarūpa ākhyāna pūrvakam tad artha kathanam sugamam bhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ nanu pratīti siddham pramāṇa ādīnām ṣoḍaśa tvam kim iti anūdyata iti atas tad nirākaraṇīyām āśaḍkām āha nanu iti sāmānya viśeṣaḥ sādharmya viśeṣaḥ yatas  asya iti pada samūhasya śāstrasya padārthāḥ padānām samūhinām arthāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ tasmāt  śāstram vākya rūpam puruṣa śreyaḥ  vākya artha rūpam abhidhatte samādhānam iti śeṣaḥ katham niḥśreyasāya kalpanta iti āpātatas paramārtha taḥ  teṣām kālpanika tve niḥśreyasam api kālpanikam tatas tad artham prayāsaḥ  viphalaḥ tasya āyatna siddha tvāt iti āśayaḥ kalpanā kośasya ananta prasara tvāt ananta ātmāna iti āpātatas paraka arthataḥ  nirātmāna iti āśayaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna iti pramāṇa dvaya upanyāsaḥ sva siddhānta viruddhaḥ  vāttika kṛta iti āha pramāṇa ādaya iti na upamāna viṣayā iti yadi api upamānasya saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pariccheda phalasya śabde pramāṇe asti eva upayogaḥ agṛhīta samayasya śabdasya apramāpaka tvāt  samayasya ca prāyaśa upamānena akalanāt  tathā api na tena te sākṣāt  viṣayīkriyante pramāṇa ādaya iti arthaḥ nanu yadi sākṣāt upamānasya prakṛta anupayogāt anabhidhānam tarhi śabdaḥ  abhidhīyatām sa hi sākṣāt upayogī ityata āha yadi api iti tatra api iti āgama viṣaya parāmarśaḥ āgamaḥ  hi yatra pravartate tad viṣayam eva pratyakṣam anumānam vā apekṣate te tu sa mūle api na sviṣaya pravṛttam pramāṇam apekṣete tatas  mūla asaṃpluta viṣaya tvāt te eva darśite iti arthaḥ vainayikā iti viśiṣṭaḥ  nayaḥ śāstram nyāya śāstram tad janya buddhi virahiṇa iti arthaḥ na etāna viviñcate samāropitāt  rūpāt iti śeṣaḥ śuśrūṣā ādiḥ iti ādi grahaṇena śravaṇa ādau pāṭavam saṃdigdhasya api jijñāsā na bhavati eva anabhimata apavargasya ityata uktam  śiṣyasya iti śiṣya tayā mumukṣutā ādi saṃpattim upalakṣayati vipratipannaḥ  api kathām ārabhamāṇaḥ  api amumukṣuḥ galite ahaṅkāre na sa apekṣaḥ  bhavati iti atas  niṣphalaḥ  jalpa vitaṇḍa ārambha iti ata āha śiṣyamāṇasya iti mohāt api mokṣam icchata iti arthaḥ jalpa vitaṇḍābhyām vigalite ahaṅkāre iti yojanā sa apekṣasya sataḥ pratipādyata iti vākya śeṣa agre kenacid  pramāreṇa iti prathama sūtra pāṭha prakāreṇa iti arthaḥ nanu asaṃdigdhasya api saṃdigdhīkaraṇe kim asya prayojanam iti ata āha asaṃdigdhaḥ  api iti tathā ca pramātaṇām sa apekṣāṇām iti śeṣaḥ te abhī durlalitāḥ śiṣyā yadi mokṣa ādau  api indriya ādi apekṣante tadā katham pratipādyā iti atas  vārtikam pūrayati kañcid iti dṛṣṭa prayojana upayoginam pratyakṣa upalabhyamānam iti arthaḥ dṛṣṭa prayojana upayoginam eva anumeyam jijñāsava iti uttaratra api pūraṇīyam iti āha evam uttaram api iti nanu etauvatā api jijñāsava iti uttaratra api pūraṇīyam iti āha evam uttaram api iti nanu etauvatā api sa apekṣā anena eva śāstreṇa pratipādyāḥ pratyakṣa anumānābhyām ca iti paraspara vyāhatam iti ata āha ayam abhisandhiḥ iti parama puruṣa artha sādhanam tu jijñāsava iti śeṣe nyāyena iti śeṣaḥ iha yadi api sukham dṛṣṭam eva vidhāyaka pramāṇa gocara eva ahita nivṛttiḥ adṛṣṭā eva niṣedhaka pramāṇa gocara eva iti yathāsaṃkhyam api saṃbhavati tathā api śreyaḥ punar  sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ ca iti atas  na kiñcid adhikam uktam bhavati iti pramāṇa aviśeṣa saṃbandha kathanam eva param na ca tena idānīm asti prayojanam na ca abhimata śreyaḥ viśeṣa nirdhāraṇe kartavye vidhi niṣedha gocaratva upavarṇanam upayujyata iti abhisaṃdhāya anyathā vyācaṣṭe tatra api iti tad śreyaḥ sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ ca iti tad śabdena dvayam api śreyaḥ tu ena parāmṛśyata iti arthaḥ yathāsaṃkhyam śaḍkām nivārayati na vyāsa jya iti dṛṣṭam sukham iti atra drṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa śabdayoḥ artham udāharaṇa mukhena spaṣṭayati sraj candana iti aihikam iti arthaḥ svarga ādi iti āmuṣmikam iti arthaḥ uktam anyatra api iti diśati evam iti ahita nivṛttiḥ api aihikyāmuṣmikī ca iti arthaḥ na evam vāttike rūyata iti ata āha cakāra lopāt iti cakārayoḥ loparat iti arthaḥ tena dṛṣṭam sukham adṛṣṭam ca tathā ahita nivṛttiḥ ca iti vāttika arthaḥ tad ayam saṃkṣepaḥ dṛṣṭam śreyaḥ tad ca sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ ca sukham api aihikam āmuṣmikam ca duḥkha nivṛttiḥ api aihikyāmuṣmikī ca iti tatra sukha lakṣaṇam śreyaḥ  dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam vā na etad śāstra sādhyam tasya sraj ādi yāga ādi sādhya tvāt ātyantikasya ca tasya abhāvāt  ahita nivṛttiḥ api anātyantikī dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa bhinnā na etad śāstra sādhyā tasyāḥ prasakta kaṇṭaka ādi hisā ādi parihāra sādhya tvāt tad aprasaktau tu asādhya tvāt ata ātyantikīm ahita nivṛtti nirdhārayitum punar bhinatti iti āha ahita nivṛtteḥ iti nanu yadi nivṛttiḥ iti nanu yadi nivṛttiḥ prāgabhāvaḥ  duḥkhasya sa katham ātyantikaḥ uttara anta anavacchedaḥ  hi ātyantika tvam prāgābhāvasya ca tathā tve prāk iti eva na syāt  atha nivṛttiḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ sa ca sarva eva ātyantika iti kutaḥ nivṛtteḥ ātyantikatva vyutpādanam iti ata āha ātyantika tvam iti nivṛttasya nivṛtta jātīyasya punar anutpādaḥ tatra eva ātmani iti śeṣaḥ nanu ekaviṃśati prabheda bhinna duḥkṣa hāniḥ eva ātyantikī duḥkha nivṛttiḥ tad katham hānyeti vāttikam ityata āha sa ca iti nivṛttyā nivṛtti svarūpeṇa lakṣyate atra ca kārya śabdena duḥkham uktam kāraṇa śabdena śarīra indriya viṣaya buddhayaḥ anuṣaḍgi sukham duḥkhena eka kāraṇa tvāt atha śarīra ādiṣu nivṛtteṣu api dukham kim na bhavet  mā bhūd duḥkham sukham kim na bhavet  na hi anyasmin  atyanta nivṛtte anyat na bhavati tathā ca anu ṣaḍga asukhi ni vṛttiḥ kim upavarṇyaya iti ata āha na hi iti kāraṇa vinā bhavat kāryam kārya tām ava jahyāt  atḥ śarīra ādiṣu asatsu duḥkhavat  sukham api na bhavati tasya api tad kāryatvāt bhavat vā śarīra ādiṣu satsu eva bhavet  tathā ca duḥkham api bhavet  kāraṇa sadbhāvāt iti arthaḥ atra eva arthe vāttikam yojanayati tad idam uktam iti anena eva kāraṇam avidyā tṛṣṇe kārya apravṛttiḥ anuṣaḍgiṇau dharma adharmau  iti ṭīkā vyākhyānam apahastitam śarīra ādīnām duḥkha tvam anubhava bādhitam iti ata āha gauṇa iti nuna ghrāṇa ādi sūtre pañca indriyāṇi prasiddhāni na ca pradeśa antare api ṣaṣ iti ata āha ṣaṣṭham iti tantra yuktyā iti bhāvaḥ nanu viṣayā api anitaretara sādhana sādhyāḥ pad ca eva vibhāge parīkṣāyām ca siddhāḥ na tu ṣaṣ iti ata āha tasya iti yadi api buddhi sukha duḥkhāni api manasaḥ  viṣayaḥ tathā api tasya eva viṣaya tvena duḥkhatva upacāraḥ  cat viṣayī kriyamāṇam duḥkham upajanayati vakṣyati hi viṣayā bodhya tvāt iti na ca buddhiḥ budhyamānā duḥkha hetuḥ vakṣyati hi buddhayaḥ tu sākṣāt iti sukha duḥkhayoḥ tu duḥkha hetu tvam eva na asti sukhasya vijātīya ārambhaka tve api rāga mātra ambhaka tvāt  duḥkhasya tu vijātīya ārambhaka tvāt eva icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ tu pratīyamānā eva sākṣāt  duḥkha janayanti tathā hi mumukṣuḥ tāvat icchāmi dveṣmi yoga abhyāsāt anyatra prayata iti pratītya eva duḥkhī bhavati ahita sādhana tvena icchā dveṣa prayatnānām tena avadhārita tvāt anyaḥ  apīṣyamāṇa alābhe bubhukṣitaḥ  asmi pipāsitaḥ  asmi iti pratītya duḥkhī bhavati hitam eva ahitam upalabhya dviṣataḥ  nivṛtta bhramasya hitam eva dveṣmi dhiḍ mām iti duḥkham evam aniṣṭa eva arthe iṣṭa buddhyā prayatamānasya nivṛtte bhrame tathā alasasya prayatnam upalabhya eva duḥkham iti etāvatā eta eva manasaḥ  viṣaya tvena nirdiṣṭāḥ nanu jarā kuṣṭa ādi upahata dehasya upalabhyamānam eva śarīram duḥkha hetuḥ tatra api viṣaya tvena eva duḥkhatva upacāraḥ syāt iti ata āha yadi api iti anyathā asya duḥkha hetu bhāvaḥ  asādhāraṇa iti śeṣaḥ viṣaya tvena puraridam na ṣaḍbhyaḥ  bhidyate asādhāraṇa indriya saṃbandhāt tu bhidyate na tu sva rūpeṇa viṣayāṇām ananta tvāt iti arthaḥ iha yadi api anuṣaḍgaḥ  avinā abhāva iti vakṣyati vāttikakāraḥ tad upapattaye ca samāna nimitta tā sā māna ādhāra tā samāna upalabhyatāḥ tathā api na tāvat mātreṇa avinā abhāvaḥ  nirvahati sādhāraṇa nimittāyām api hi anyatarā sādhāraṇa nimitta nivṛttau  ekatara nivṛttau itarāna vṛtti saṃbhavāt ata eva ādhārasya upalabdhi sādhanasya ca sāmye api ekatarasya kāraṇa abhāvena abhāve api anyatara sabhdau  ena avinā abhāva iti āśaḍkya sukhasya duḥkha anuṣaḍga upapattaye duḥkha hetu anuṣaṅgam eva āha sādhana iti atas  na dvitīya sūtra vārti kaṭīkābhyām virodhaḥ sādhana pāratantryam kāryā tvāt  akāryasya ca sukhasya abhāvāt  pāratantryam ca daṃḥkha hetuḥ yad āha sarva para vaśam duḥkham iti kṣayitvam ca sukhasya samavāyikāraṇavat tvāt tad api duḥkha hetuḥ iṣṭa viyogaḥ  hi duḥkham janayati iti kṣayitvam kāme sati iti tu vyākhyānam duḥkha hetava iti bahuvacana viruddham atas  svatantram eva idam hetu trayam kāma icchā sā ca sukha tad sādhanayoḥ vyāpikā na hi sukha tad sādhanam vā anicchataḥ sukham nāma sukha sādhanam ca tad api sulabham durlabham ca tatra durlabha icchā duḥkha eka phalā eva sulabha icchātu aniṣiddha sādhana gocarā niṣiddha sādhana gocarā ca tatra niṣaddha sādhāna gocarā api svarūpataḥ kāryataḥ ca adharma janana dvāreṇa avaśyam duḥkha phala iti aniṣiddha sulabha sādhāna gocarā api śarīra pāṭave satsati vā tatra asati duḥkha hetuḥ eva śarīra ādi pāṭave api sa vighnā nirvighnā ca tatra sa vighnā duḥkham eva prasūte nirvighnā api aniṣṭa saṃbhinna viṣayā tad viparītā ca tatra prathamā avaśyam duḥkha hetuḥ dvitīyā tu viphalā saphalā ca tatra prathamā duḥkha hetuḥ eva dvitīyā tu sa vilamba phalā avilambphalā ca tatra prathamā avaśyam eva duḥkha hetuḥ dvitīyā api anāyati viśuddhā tad viparītā ca tatra prathamā duḥkha hetuḥ eva dvitīyā tu viṣayasya piriṇa tivirasa tvāt  duḥkham eva prasūte ati vyāmohāt  viṣayeṣu eva magnasya icchā antaram eva vā ubhayathā api anartha mūlam iti evam sukha anuṣaktaḥ kāmaḥ  api duḥkha hetuḥ iti iha yadi api rāga dveṣa moha pravṛttayaḥ  api duḥkha tadanuḍgi sādhana bhāvāt indriya ādivat  duḥkha tvena parisaṃkhyātum ucitāḥ tathā api na śarīra indriya ādi vyatirekeṇa am ūṣām ātma lābhaḥ  duḥkham prati vyāpāraḥ  vā indriya ādīnām punar deṣa pravṛtti abhāve api duḥkham prati vyāpāraḥ  jīvanmuktasya asti eva pravṛtti phalam tu dharma adharmau yadi api sukha duḥkha hetū tathā api ekaviṃśatividha duḥkha maya saṃsāra nṛtya śālā mūla stambha tvāt anayoḥ na atra parisaṃkhyānam na hi bhāvini janmāntare śarīra indriya aviṣaya buddhi sukha duḥkhāni āhatya vyāpriyante yathā dharma adharmau etad eva abhisaṃdhāya kāraṇa rūpa dharma adharma uccheda krameṇa kārya rūpa ekaviṃśatividha duḥkhasya ucchedaḥ vārttika kṛtā darśita iti tathā eva vāttikam avatārayati ukta prakāra iti iha ca āgāmi dharma adharma nivṛttau  upāyaḥ tad sādhana pravṛtti parityāgaḥ utpanna nivṛtau tu upabhoga iti darśitam tad ubhayam api anupapannam vāc buddhi śarīra ambham parityajya jīvitum aśaktayatvāt  mṛte api śadīra ādi antarajralepasya dupaneya tvāt  upabhāgaḥ ca aśakyaḥ aniyata vipāka samaya tvāt ananta tvāt ananta phala tvāt ca bhoga avasthāyām api ananta karma antara utpāda na tāyā avarāmāt  atha kathañcid upabhoga anutpādābhyām utpanna an utpannayoḥ śakyaḥ prakṣayaḥ tarhi śāstra vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ tatas  eva tad siddha iriti āśaḍkya vārttikasya upaskurūte saṃśaya ādi iti saṃśaya ādi ityādi padena caturdaśā api nyāya parikara tvena saṃgṛhītāḥ param anyāya iti anene mūlamūlībhāva vyavasthitāni catvāri api pramāṇāni nyāyaḥ  mārga iva nyāya mārgaḥ niḥreyasa bhūmeḥ prāpti hetu tvāt  dvādaśavidhā iti ātma ādi prameyam tad anena śāstrasya avasara upayogau darśitau tattva paribhāvanā iti anena abhyāsasya tad evam pūrva uktena nyāyena mokṣamāṇasya śāstre pravṛttiḥ tatas  parikara parijñānam tatas  nyāya mārga pariśodhanam tatas tena dvādaśavidha prameya āsādanam tatas  abhyāsaḥ tatas  prasaṃkhyānam tatas  sa mūla doṣa anuṣaṅga nirmokṣaḥ tatas  apravṛttiḥ tatas  āgāminoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ asaṃcayaḥ iti evam anāgataḥ pravāhaḥ  nivāritaḥ yadi api ca yāvat śarīra ādi bhāvinī pravṛttiḥ tathā api doṣa anuṣaṅga sahakāri virahāt na asau pravṛttiḥ tad kārya asamartha tvāt iti utpanna bhogam upapādayati anādi iti yadi api yathā anādau bhāva paramparāyām karmāṇi pracīyante tathā apacīcante api na hi ārambhe param bhavasya anāditā na nūpabhoge karma ārambhaḥ  hi adhikāriṇi śarīre tad ca śarīra koṭi madhya patitam ekam śarīram kadācid  kiñcid  kvacid eva bhogaḥ tu na asti eva tad śarīram yatra na asti bhogasya tad āyatana tvāt  tasmādāya vyaya paryālocanayā parimitam eva karma ata eva niyavipāka samayam api tasya ca krama bhāvibhiḥ api kiyadbhiḥ kaiścid eva śarīrai rūpa bhogāt  prakṣayaḥ  api na durūpa pādaḥ tathā api āgama prāmāṇyāt kāya yaugapadyasya api prasaṃkhyāna phala tayā siddha tvāt ananta āma niyata vipāka samaya tām ca abhyupagamya eva parihṛtam vibhūtimatā aneka kāla upabhogyam api ekadā bhujyata iti atra samudra pānam udāharaṇam yogardhi prabhāva sampannaḥ  vividha phala bhoginaḥ  vicitra svabhāvān ekadā eva bahūn kāyān icchā mātreṇa eva nirmimīta iti atra daṇḍaka araṇya sṛṣṭiḥ ūdāhaṇam iti iha kecid  āhuḥ duḥkha nivṛtti puruṣa artha eva svarūpataḥ  na bhavati sa upādhi tvāt  sukham duḥkha abhāve sati eva bhavati iti sukha sādhana antaravat duḥkha abhāvaḥ  api mṛtyate na nu sa eva puruṣasya samīhita iti tad uktam varam vṛndāvane araṇye kroṣṭa tvam abhivāñchitum na tu vaiśeṣikī muktim gautamaḥ  gantum icchati iti tad anupapannam viparyāsasya api saṃbhavāt  bhojana ādi sukhe sati eva hi bubhukṣā ādi duḥkham nivartata iti duḥkha nivṛtti artham eva bhojana ādi sukham mṛgyate na punar tad eva tasya samīhitam iti kim na kalpayate kvacid  duḥkha bhāve api sukhasya iṣyamāṇa tvā diti ced  na duḥkha nivṛtteḥ api kvacid  sukha abhāve apīṣyamāṇa tvāt eva duḥkha nivṛttau satyām sukham eva bhaviṣyati iti abhisandhiḥ tāvat asti iti ced  na sukha avasthāyām niyamataḥ  duḥkha virahaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti abhisandheḥ tatra api saṃbhavāt  tasmāt  yadi api duḥkha hānau sukham sukhe ca duḥkha hāniḥ niyatā tathā api paraspara nirapekṣam eva puruṣa artha tvam anayoḥ icchayoḥ api asaṃkīrṇa viṣaya tvāt anyaḥ tu āha bhavati eva hi duḥkha hāniḥ puruṣa arthaḥ kim tu anubhūyamāna tayā na hi viṣa ādi janya moha avasthāyām duḥkha nivṛttiḥ iti tad artham prekṣāvantaḥ pravartante tasmāt  mokṣe duḥkha hāneḥ ananubhūyamāna tvāt na puruṣa artha tvam iti tad uktam duḥkha abhāvaḥ  api na āvedyaḥ puruṣa artha tayā iṣyate na hi mūrcchā ādi avastha artham pravṛttaḥ  dṛśyate sudhīḥ iti tad api anupapannam putra ādi viyoga janya duḥkha hānim icchataḥ  keṣāñcid  viṣa śastra udūndhana dau  api pravṛtti darśanāt  prekṣāvantaḥ  na evam kurvanti iti ced  na puruṣa arthatva avirodhāt  na hi para dāreṣu śāstra niṣedhāt kuśa nivāritāḥ prekṣāvantaḥ  na pravartanta iti na tatra kāmaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ api tu alpīyaḥ sukham mahān anartha iti nivṛttiḥ tathā viṣādau  api pravṛttasya śāstra garhita tvāt alpīyān anarthaḥ  nivartate mahīyān pravartata iti na te pravartanta iti iyam eva hi prekṣā yad  puruṣa artha tve api lokaśāstra virodha parāmarśaḥ na tu apuruṣa artha tvāt eva svarūpeṇa iṣyamāṇa tā mātra nibandhana tvāt  puruṣartha tāyāḥ ataeva na yatra lokaśāstra virodhaḥ tatra vyādhi ādi paripīḍitāḥ prayāga vaṭa prapāta anaśana ādinā api deham tyajantaḥ prekṣāvantaḥ  dṛśyante na hi kaścid  duḥkha nivṛttim anubhaviṣyāmi iti tad sādhane pravartate api tu duḥkha hāsyāmi iti api ca duḥkha nivṛtteḥ anubhūyamāna tā mātram vivakṣitam duḥkha nivṛtti sattau  adhiḥ vā ādyaḥ ced  tuṣyatu durjanaḥ carame janmani anubhūyata eva samādhi prabhāvāt  ātyantikī duḥkha nivṛttiḥ anāgatā vartamānā api aciram anubhūyata eva dvitīye tu prasakta kaṇṭaka ādi hetuka daḥkha nivṛtteḥ apuruṣa arthatva prasaṅgaḥ sarva dānanubhūyamāna tvāt  tathā tve vā viṣaya antara saṃcāra abhāva prasaṅgāt  nivṛtteḥ sarvadā tādavasthyāt iti tasmāt  sarva dān anubhūyamānā api yathā kaṇṭaka ādi janya duḥkha nivṛttiḥ puruṣa artha tayā puruṣam prayojayati tathā śāstra artha bhūtā api tad idam duḥkha nivṛtteḥ apuruṣa artha tvam ananubhūyamāna tayā eva ca apuruṣa artha tvam iti pakṣa dvayam ati nirvalam iti etad iti upekṣya tṛtīyam śaṅkate syāt etad iti tad uktam asatyāni durantāni samavyaya phalāni ca aśakyāni ca vastūni na ārabheta vicakṣaṇaḥ iti siddhānta vārttikam uddīpayati yadi api iti tad anena madhu viṣa saṃpṛkta anna bhojana dṛṣṭāntena samavyaya phala tvam apavargasya nirākṛtam yathā hi atra anarthasya bhūyas tvam arthasya tu kṣudra tvam na tathā apavarge api iti etena etad api nirastam yad uktam yathā duḥkha śabalam saṃsāra sukham anādeyam tathā sukha śabala tayā duḥkham api upādeyam kim na syāt  dṛśyante hi sukha arthinaḥ  yagādi duḥkham anubhavanta iti yasya duḥkham upādeyam heyam tasya kim ucyatām heya hīnasya kā muktiḥ kena vā api upadiśyate iti yaḥ tu ghanatara duḥkha timira nirantarāt saṃsāra kāntārāt  sukha khadyotikāsu dyotamānāsu api bibheti tam prati ayam nirasta tamaskatayā sugamaḥ  mārga upadiśyata iti tad idam uktam tena mā bhūt atat ityādi nanu evam sati na asya sarva artha tā tathā ca jagataḥ śamāya iti anena virodha iti ata āha avivekinām api iti yadi api kasyacid apravṛttau  api na sarva artha tā asya hīyata iti prapañcitam adhastāt tathā api heyam heya tvena agṛhṇantaḥ  mandāḥ kāruṇikeṇa grāhayitavyā iti arthaḥ nanu śāstreṇa tattva jñānāt  vairāgyam vairāgyāt ca śāstre pravṛttiḥ iti durūttaram itaretara āśraya tvam iti ata āha śāstre pravṛtti iti duḥkhāt udvijataḥ  bhoga vaimukhya mātram iha vairāgyam vivakṣitam na tu rāga abhāva eva iti arthaḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra artha tayā dvaividhya śaḍkām apanayati aika rūpyam dvairūpyam ca iti nanu puruṣa bhede api pravṛtteḥ dvaividhyam eva na hi kaścid  sukham prāptum iva duḥkham api āptum pravartate na api kaścid  duḥkha hānāya iva sukha hānāya api ityata āha puruṣa bhedaḥ  rāga vairāgyābhyām iti nanu sukhasya heya tvam eva kuta iti ata āha prāptavyasya iti avivekinām tu pravṛttiḥ dvi rūpa iti uktam vārttika kṛtā iti śeṣaḥ prakṛtam upasaṃharan  eva aprakṛta upanipāta śaḍkām api apanetum vṛttavartiṣyamāṇe anukīrtayati tad anena iti tad avayavam vivarītu mukta tātparya sphoraṇa artham iti śeṣaḥ alaukika tvāt  lokasya asmad ādeḥ niti aparokṣa tvāt ayuktam aprāmāṇikam vipratiṣiddham mithas  vyāpaka viruddham pravṛttyai niṣkampa pravṛttyai kim tarhi pramāṇam iti gṛhītam iti anuvartate rajata jñānam idam śukla bhāsvara rūpavat  dravyam rajatam iti evam jñānam iti arthaḥ paricchinatti uktam artham ālambya paricchitti rūpam jāyata iti arthaḥ śuktikā jñānam api iti idam śukla bhāsvara rūpam śuktikā dravyam na rajatam iti jñānam iti arthaḥ yadi evam katham anayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāva iti ata āha kevalam iti rajata samāropa apavādābhyām iti samāropa apavāda svabhāvatayā iti arthaḥ tad evam pariccheda dvāreṇa paricchedakam unnīyata iti paricchedasya eva sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ paricchedatva apariccheda tve darśite na ca ekasya eva jñānasya viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ jātyā hi buddhiḥ anubhavaḥ smṛtiḥ ca tatra smutiḥ apramā eva anubhavaḥ tu svarūpa anubhavaḥ  asvarūpa anubhavaḥ ca saḥ  ayam viṣaya kṛtaḥ  viśeṣaḥ nānā viṣayā ca ekā buddhiḥ bhavati eva tatas ca sā eva buddhiḥ svarūpa avasthitena arthena nirūpyamāṇā pramā asvarūpa avasthitena nirūpyamāṇā tu apramā iti tathābhūta avacchinna anubhava tvam eva pramāṇa tvam atathābhūtena tu avacchinnam apramāṇa tvam iti bhavati apramāṇasya api sāmānya paricchedaka tvam iti racitā bhūmiḥ kim etāvatā iti āha asti tāvat asādhāraṇam kāraṇam asamarthāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tathā eva unnīyamānam tasya ca vyāpāraḥ  viparīta artha pariccheda eva asādhāraṇaḥ tad ca evaṃbhūta vyāpāra upakaraṇam apramāṇam iti vyavahniyate evam ca pravṛtti sāmarthyā sāmarthya saṃdehe api yadi tad janakam apramāṇam asamarthā eva sā atha na tad apramāṇam tad janyā pravṛttiḥ api na asamartha iti apramāṇān niyataḥ samartha pravṛtti vyatirekaḥ pramāṇam ca atra ubhaya vyatireka grāhakam viruddha kārya tvam liṅgam prakṛta kāryasya tad vyatireka grāhi ca pratyakṣa madhyavasā iyam iti na apramāṇāt artha vyabhicāriṇor athavyabhicāri jñāna vyāpārāt iti arthaḥ siddhaḥ  vyatirekaḥ ki cāta iti ata āha tathā ca iti arthavat tvam artha avyabhicāri tvam artha avyabhicāri anubhava janaka tvam iti arthaḥ nanu tasyāḥ  iti atra katham anantara tvena prakṛta ām asamarthām vihāya vyavahitvena aprakṛtā api samarthā eva pravṛtti parāmṛśyata iti ata āha asamarthā tu iti pūrva prakāntam yogyam eva prakṛtam ucyate na tu anantara uktam iti arthaḥ nanu anuditasya anuvādaḥ kkopayujyata iti ata āha saṃprati iti pūrvam vyākhyātum idānīm ākṣeptum iti arthaḥ ākṣepa samādhānayoḥ sphuṭa avabhāsi tve api saṃgraha vivaraṇayoḥ pauna rūkti am pariharan  āha ākṣipati iti saṃdehāt api pravṛtteḥ tatra tatra darśanāt  niru ucchvāsam ākṣepam ujjīvayati na tāvat iti amum eva artham bhāṣyeṇa saṃvadati sā iyam iti uktā bhāṣya kutā iti śeṣaḥ kim atas  yadi evam iti ata āha na ca iti artha viniścaya ukta rūpaḥ śreyaḥ hetuta anumāna sahita iti yāvat  prāmāṇya avadhāraṇam śreyaḥ hetu tāliṅga parāmarśa prasava ucitam antareṇa iti arthaḥ evaṃrūpa tā ca prāmāṇya avadhāraṇasya vyāpti smaraṇa sāhityam eva iti tasya api bījam samuccinoti śreyaḥ hetuta anumāna nimitta vyāpti grahaṇam ca iti tābhyām vinā iti svarūpa niścaya śreyaḥ hetuta anumānābhyām vinā iti arthaḥ vyāpti grahaṇa ānantarye api tad phalasya eva anumānasya yogyatayā prakrānta tvāt  imam eva vārtika artham pariśodhayan sphuṭayati tad idam uktam iti niścaya anumāne na prāmāṇya avadhāraṇa anumāna bīja bhūta vyāpti grahaṇābhyām vinā te ca na pravṛttyā vinā pravṛttiḥ ca na niścaya anumānābhyām vinā iti ākṣepa saṃkṣapaḥ iha ca dvidhā pravṛttiḥ aihikaphalā āmuṣmikaphalā ca tatra amuṣmikaphalā prāmāṇya avadhāraṇa pūrvikā eva aihikaphalā tu apekṣita upāya tā jñāna mātra adhīnā artha niścayam api na apekṣate prāk eva pramāṇa srūpa jñānam kutastarām tad viniścayam yatra api pravṛtteḥ prāk eva pramāṇa tattva viniścayaḥ tatra api asau sva hetu balāt āyataḥ  na pravṛttim prati prayojakaḥ anyathā ekāntika vijayā niścaye prāmāṇyākṣepaka eva vijigīṣuḥ kathāyām na pravarteta na hi jalpataḥ  vitaṇḍayataḥ  vā avaśyam aikāntikaḥ  vijayaḥ tasmāt arthā niścaye api pravṛttiḥ iti ubhaya vādi siddham hṛdi nidhāya siddhāntam upakramate tatra brūma iti dṛṣṭa artheṣu iti adṛṣṭa artha āgama ādi vyudāsaḥ tatra pravṛtteḥ phala abhisaṃbandha aniścayāt  anabhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu iti abhyāsa daśa āpannā pitṛ vacana ādi vyudāsaḥ te hi pramāṇa tayā pravṛtteḥ prāgava niścīyante abhyāsa śva aviparītaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ tena sva ātmani abhyāse api pravṛtti sāmarthyāt eva tad niścayaḥ  viparīta abhyāsa virahāt sa ca viṣaya gocaraḥ tad na āntarīyaka artha gocaraḥ  vā tad jātīyatva avadhāraṇa upāyaḥ  yatra svarūpataḥ  api na asti tatra pravṛtti sāmarthyāt eva tad gocarasya prāmāṇya avadhāraṇam yathā vaidya vacanāt anartha nivṛtti saṃbhāvayataḥ  asaṃstuta pradeśa sthiteṣu mūleṣu yatra tu svarūpa abhyāsaḥ  asti eva tad gatam tu śreyaḥ sādhanam abhyastam tatra pravṛtti sāmarthyena tad sādhanatva grāhiṇaḥ prāmāṇyam yathā angiḥ pāka ādi samartha iti saṃbhāvita āpta tvasya vacanāt upalabhya svayam pacataḥ yatra api śreyaḥ sādhana tve abhyāsaḥ svarūpe tu anabhyāsaḥ tatra api svarūpa gocarasya eva prāmāṇyam pravṛtti sāmarthyāt avasīyate yathā agniḥ pāka ādi samartha eva iti niścitavataḥ  apariśīlita vana vahnau sarvatra eva artha bhūyaḥ tvam viparyaye tu anartha māndyam saṃbhāvayataḥ pravṛttiḥ sva rūpa śreyaḥ sādhanatva niścaye api phala saṃdeha iva iti āha naḥ khalu iti tad amī saṃśayānā api pravartamānāḥ phala iva sva rūpa śreyaḥ sādhana tvayoḥ iti śeṣaḥ pramāṇasya sva rūpa grāhiṇaḥ śreyaḥ sādhanatva grāhiṇaḥ ca iti arthaḥ tattvam pramāṇa tvam artha avyabhicāri pramāsādhana tvam iti yāvat  viniścitya artha avi abhicāri pramāvi niścaya dvāreṇa iti śeṣaḥ tad jātīyasya anyasya etāvatā eva samartha tve abhyāsadaśā āpannasya iti dṛṣṭa artha pramāṇa saṃgraha artham pravṛtti sāmarthyāt  prāk eva samarthāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ pūrvam eva iti tena ayam arthaḥ yadi api dṛṣṭa artheṣu abhyāsadaśā āpanneṣu api pravṛtti sāmarthyam asti tena api ca prāmāṇyam avadhārayitum tatra śakyate tathā api tad jātīyatva lakṣaṇena eva liḍgena pravṛtteḥ prāk eva avadhārite prāmāṇye tad pramāturu uttara kālam pramitsā eva na asti tad nibandhana tvāt ca anumāna pravṛtteḥ yadi punar  pramitsā anapekṣam eva samartha pravṛtti janaka tvam parāmṛśyate tadā kā kṣatiḥ tena api anumīyatām prāmāṇyam pramāṇa saṃplavasya api vyavasthāpanāt iti nanu kim idam tad jātīya tvam na tāvat  pramāṇa jātīya tvam sādhya aviśiṣṭatva prasaṅgāt  na api samartha pravṛtti janaka jātīya tvam tad hi samartha pravṛtti saṃbandhaḥ  vā syāt  tad upahitaḥ  vā niyata prāc abhāvaḥ na tāvat ādyaḥ pravṛtteḥ prāk eva iti vacanāt  na api uttaraḥ tasya atīndriyasya liḍgam vinā pratyetum aśakyatvāt  liḍgam ca tasya prāmāṇya eka niyatasya yadi asti tadā prāmāṇyam eva tena anumīyatām kim tad jātīyatva anumānena prāmāṇya aniyatasya tu tasya anumānena kim na api pratyakṣa siddha eva kaścid dharmaḥ tad jātīya tvam pratyakṣa tve tu tasya anabhyāsa daśa āpanana gocare api pramāṇe pratīti prasaṅgāt  tathā ca tatra api pravṛtteḥ prāk eva prāmāṇya avadhāraṇam syāt  vyāpteḥ api prāk eva pratīta tvāt  na hi ayam kvacid api tad jātīya tvena prāmāṇyam na anumitavāt  tatra na asti eva tad jātīya tvam kim pratyakṣeṇa pratīyatām iti ced  na abhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu tad jātīya tvena prāmāṇye anumīyamāne pravṛtti sāmarthya anumita prāmāṇyasya sādhana vikala tayā dṛṣṭānta ābhāsatva prasaṅgāt  tasmāt  tad jātīya tvam atiriktam na paśyāma iti satyam tathā api jñānasya viṣya nibandhana tvāt  tad tad viṣaya upādhaya eva te te jñāna upādhayaḥ taiḥ tairūpādhibhirūpādhīyamānam jñānam eva tad jātīyam tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam bhavati te ca upādhayaḥ pratibhedam sva saṃjñābhiḥ abhidhātum aśakyā iti tad jātīya tvam iti anayā vācaḥ bhaḍgyā darśitāḥ ata eva atra vīpsā draṣṭavyā tad tad jātīya tvam iti tathā hi anubhavaḥ tāvat  svarūpa prakārau  ālambate tatra dharmi svarūpeṇa upadhīyamānaḥ  anubhavaḥ pramā eva iti tena rūpeṇa anubhūte tasmin pramātvam eva anubhūtam bhavati iti agre sphuṭībhaviṣyati prakāra viṣayaḥ tu anubhava ubhayathā kaścid  svarūpa prakāreṇa upādhīyate kaścid asvarūpa prakāreṇa api iti atas  kvacid  saṃśayaḥ tatra svarūpa prakāreṇa upahitam anubhava vivektum viśiṣṭāḥ prakāra upādhayaḥ  bhavanti te ca niyamena vibhrama viṣaya virodhi tayā nirdhārita svabhāva bhedā guṇa ādaya eva tad idam sāmānyatas tāvat lakṣaṇa sahacarita lakṣya viṣaya jñāna tvam eva jñāna gatam tad jātīya tvam iti pratyakṣe gatiḥ yadā tu apratyakṣe lakṣye lakṣaṇena jñānam janyate tadā anumānam tad iti tasya anyathā eva gatiḥ bhaviṣyati iti tatra dravye gandhavati pṛthivī jñānam ityādi sāmānyatas  kara caraṇa ādimati śarīra jñānam ityādi viśeṣataḥ guṇeṣu ketakī ādau saurabha jñānam śaḍkha ādau śveta jñānam ityādi karmaṇi tu avātulena tiṣṭhatā tīvra vega asaṃskṛtena calat jala ādi su accha vilokana ādi virahiṇā yad  dravyam calati iti upalabhyate tad  tathā iti evam teṣu teṣu viśeṣeṣu te te viśeṣā vyabhicāra virodhinaḥ  na pratipadam anukramitum śakyante tad evam tad tad upādhi viśiṣṭa tad tad viṣaya anubhava tvam eva tad jātīya tvam iti mantavyam tad evaṃbhūtasya jñānasya viṣayana antarīyaka tvena upādhi abhyāsa eva abhyāsa daśā āpanna tvam yatra tu sa eva arthaḥ  bhūyaḥ bhūyaḥ abhyastaḥ tatra saṃvādaka tvam eva tad jātīya tvam evam tāvat  bāhya pratyakṣam samarthitam pratyakṣa samāna nyāya tayā āgamasya prāmāṇyam samarthayati evam ca iti atra api tad jātīya tvam āpta praṇetṛka tvam abhyāsadaśā āpanna tvam punar etasya bhūyas darśanena mantra āyurvede tad jātīya tvāya prāmāṇya avinā abhāva siddhiḥ mantra āyurvedasya anabhyāsa daśā āpanna tvam tad asiddhaḥ nivedayiṣyate sūtrakāreṇa dvitīya adhyāye yathā ca prāmāṇyam pravṛtti sāmarthyena avadhāryate anabhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu tathā prāmāṇyam api pravṛtti viparyayeṇa yathā ca pravṛtteḥ prāk eva abhyāsa daśā āpanneṣu tad jātīya tayā prāmāṇyam avadhāryate tathā prāmāṇyam api iti mantavyam upādhi virodhaḥ ca tad jātīya tvam tad abhyāsa eva abhyāsa daśā āpanna tvam yathā candramasi candra dvaya jñānam śaḍkhe pīta jñānam guḍe tikta jñānam ityādi tasmāt  sandigdhe pravṛtti sāmarthyam avadhāraṇīyam iti syāt etad  sāmarthya punar asyāḥ phalena abhisaṃbandhaḥ atha phala jñānasya eva prāmāṇyam katham avadhāraṇīyam iti atra keṣāñcid matam āha na ca iti na punar u udanyā upaśamam api parīkṣyata iti udanya upaśamanam api iti arthaḥ tad etad anupapannam phala jñānam hi phalasya siddha avasthasya sādhanān arha tayā niṣprayojanī bhūta tvāt  vā na parīkṣyet  tad tad jātīya jñānasya sarvāsu avasthāsu artha avyabhicāritayā niḥśaṅka tvāt  vā iti na tāvat ādyaḥ phalasya siddha avastha tve tadvat  tad sādhanībhūtasya api niṣprayojanī bhūta tvāt aparīkṣyatva prasaṅgāt  uttara uttarulābhisaṃdhānena tad sādhanam parīkṣyata iti ceta phale api evam astu siddha eva hi phale parīkṣite tad sādhanasya tathātva siddhau  uttara uttarulābhisandhiḥ syāt  na api dvitīyaḥ phala jñānasya api bhūyaḥ bhūyas  spapna ādi avasthāsu vyabhicāra darśanāt  svastha avasthasya phala jñānam na vyabhicarati iti ced  evam tarhi pirīkṣitam eva phala jñānam syāt  tathā hi yad  svastha avasthasya phala jñānam tad avyabhicāri iti vyāpti siddhau yatra eva tathābhūta jñāna tvam paśyati tatra eva avyabhicāram avadhārayati iti anena abhiprāyeṇa āha vayam tu iti asya api abhyāsa daśa āpanna tvam prāmāṇya avinā mūta liḍga upalambhaḥ tathā tad jātīya tvam punar  svastha avasthasya phala jñāna tvam eva etena icchā dveṣa prayatna jñānam vyākhyātam nanu yad vijñāna dṛṣṭāntayitavyam tasya api prāmāṇyam katham sādhanīyam evam tad tad sādhanasya api dṛṣṭānta paramparāyāḥ katham iti ata āha na ca iti phala jñānasya iti upalakṣaṇam tad jātīya tvena liḍgena prāmāṇye sa adhiyitavye yad yad  dṛṣṭāntīkriyate tasya tasya iti mantavyam yadyavam pravṛtti sāmarthyam anavakāśam eva na hi asti tad vijñānam yad  sarvathā eva apūrva viṣayam tathā ca pramāṇator atha pratipatti pravṛtti sāmarthyayoḥ katham anādi tvam āha vārttikakāra iti ata āha eteṣu ca madhya iti śaḍkitavyabhicāram tad jātīyatva aparāmarśāt iti śeṣaḥ yadi api phalam na pravṛtti viṣayaḥ tathā api tad sādhana gocarāyāḥ tad saṃtāna gocarāyāḥ  eva vā pravṛtteḥ tad jātīya phala antara saṃbandhaḥ tad na āntarīyaka vijātīya phala saṃbandhaḥ  vā svasya nara antarasya vā pravṛtti sāmarthyam phala jñānasya draṣṭāvyam tad evam samāna nyāya tayā rūpa ādi bāhi artha pratyakṣa prāmāṇya samarthanā anantaram śabdra prāmāṇyam samarthya tad ubhaya upapattaye samāna nyāya tayā eva āntara pratyakṣa jñāneṣu madhye phala jñāna prāmāṇyam samarthitam samāna nyāya tayā eva icchā dveṣa prayatna gocarasya api jñānasya prāmāṇya samarthanam sūcitam iti anaṃvyavasāyaḥ  avaśiṣyate tasya ca anumāna samāna nyāya tayā anumāna prāmāṇya samarthana anantaram eva samarthanam kariṣyata iti abhiprāyavān āha anumānasya iti dvidhā hi vyabhicāra śaḍkā kāraṇataḥ sva rūpataḥ ca sā ca vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā grāhakaiḥ eva pramāṇaiḥ apanīyata iti bhavati nirasta samasta vyabhicāra śaṅkam anumiti jñānam tasya evaṃbhūtasya svata eva prāmāṇyam niścīyata iti śeṣaḥ nanu pramāṇatva aviśeṣe api katham anumiteḥ eva svatas  na pratyakṣa ādeḥ ityata āha anumeya iti anumiti jñānam hi arthasya tathā tvam vyavacchindat eva utpadyate vahnimān eva ayam iti tathā ca anuvyavasānena anuvyavasīyamānam idam sva sva artha avadhāraṇa ātmakam eva avasīyate na ca aviparīta arthaka tvam anubhavasya anadhyavasya tā avadhāraṇa ātmaka tvam asya avasitam bhavati tathā ca tad  avaśyam avaseyam tad eva ca prāmāṇyam kadācid evaṃbhūta anuvyavasāye api viparyayatva śaḍkā tad avaskandati iti avaśiṣyate sā ca liṅga samuttha tvāt eva na asti na hi viśeṣa darśana grasta utpattau śaḍka avakāśaḥ tad etad āha na hi iti liṅga ākāram vijñānam niścita avyabhicāram iti śeṣaḥ pratyakṣa śābda jñāne tu na ayoga vyavaccheda ātmake api tvāropa anārāpa sādhāraṇa viṣaya mātra avabhāsinī tathā ca anuvyavasāyena api tathā eva anubhūyete na tu avadhāraṇa ātmaka tayā iti na tayoḥ svatas  prāmāṇya grahaḥ atha daivāt ayoga vyavaccheda ātmake eva utpadyete anuvyavasīyete ca tadā ca niyāmakam antar bhāvyā eva tad abhāve tu aviśeṣāt avadhāraṇa ātmaka tvam paribhūya tad atad rūpa sādhāraṇam eva avatiṣṭheta iti āśayavān niyāmaka abhāvam eva āha pratyakṣa jñānam tu iti dhūma ādi yukta dhūma dhvaja ādi jñāne hi yadi api arthasya api arthena avyabhicāraḥ  asti yadi api ca arthāt api tathābhūtāt eva tad jñānam jāyate tathā api avyabhicāraḥ  vā tad grahaḥ  vā prāktanaḥ tatra akiścitkara eva indriya āpāta mātrāt eva yugapad ubhayoḥ api eka jñāna avabhāsitayā parāmarśa kāla anapekṣaṇāt aparāmṛṣṭasya ca aniyāmaka tvāt  tad idam uktam api tu sattā mātreṇa avasthitāt iti avyabhicāriṇaḥ  api iti śeṣaḥ etena śaḍkā mātram apanīyate jñāna antaraiḥ iti yad uktam kaiścid  tad nirastam śaḍkā hi saṃśaya eva abhidhīyate sa ca tattva nirṇaya vyatirekeṇa apanetum aśakya eva iti tattva nirṇaya upāyaḥ  anusartavyaḥ tathā ca jñāna svarūpa grāhiṇaḥ kauṇṭhye pratyakṣa ādi antara abhāve ca anumānam eva upāya iti tad āha pravṛtti sāmarthyam iti syāt etad  yadi pratyakṣa śābda jñānayoḥ paratas  prāmāṇyam tad  kim idānīm anuvyavasāyasya api parata eva tathā ca liḍgam niścitam eva niścāyakam iti anena nyāyena liṅga antara paramparā jñānam anavasthām avatārayati iti ata āha jñāna gata iti atra api sā eva yuktiḥ atad rūpa vyudāsena eva sva viṣayam ālambya eva utpatteḥ tathā eva anubhavaḥ utpatteḥ eva ārabhya viṣaya viśeṣa grahaṇa grasta tvāt ca na śaḍka avakāśaḥ viśeṣaḥ ca anuvyavasāya tvam eva na hi ajānat na api kaścid  jānāmi iti anuvyavasyati na ca śuktikā ākāre jñāne rajatam jānāmi iti syāt iti tad idam uktam tādṛśasya iti upalakṣaṇam ca etad  sa bāhī abhyantaram dharmi mātra gocaram api pratyakṣam svata eva pramāṇam vibhramasya api nirālamba nasye kvacid anupapatteḥ iti uktu yuktim hṛdi nidhāya atidiśati etena iti upamānam upamitiḥ iti arthaḥ vyākhyātam svatas  avadhārya prāmāṇyatayā iti śeṣaḥ na hi ati deśa vākya artha jñāna sādṛśya jñānayoḥ prāmāṇye niśvite upamitiḥ ābhāsībhavati yadi api ca anumāna upamāna anuvyavasāya dharmi jñānānām api prāmāṇyam paratas  api śakya graham eva santi hi tatra api yathāyogam liṅga sādṛśya jñāna samutthatva ādīni tad jātīyatva liṅgāni tathā api koṣṭha gatyā svata eva prāmāṇya grahaḥ  atra na svayam iti sa eva darśitaḥ vipratipannam prati tu parata eva sādhanīyam tad iti parama arthaḥ atas  svata eva iti avadhāraṇam na ayoga vyavacchede na api anya yoga vyavacchede kim tarhi atyanta ayoga vyavaccheda iti nanu etauvatā api vijñāna karaṇānam indriya ādīnām prāmāṇyasya kutas  siddhiḥ na hi phala yathārtha tvam eva amīṣām prāmāṇyam iti ata āha sevadanasya ca iti nanu indriyādayaḥ  yadi artha vyāmi cāriṇaḥ katham arthadhiyam avyabhicāriṇī janayeyuḥ tathā tve vā rāsabhaḥ  api vahna dhiyam avyabhicāriṇī janaced  aviśeṣāt ityata āha na ca iti yathā ārdra indhanam dahanavyami cārī api dahana saṃbandhāt  dahana avi abhicāriṇam dhūmam janayan  niyoga paryanuyogau  arhati kāraṇa svābhāvyāt  tathā indriya ādi api artha vyabhicāriṇam tathāvidha sahakārī upabṛṃhitam tena arthena saṃbandhāt  tad artha avyabhicāri jñānam janayet iti arthaḥ tad etad prāmāṇyam na avaśyam sarvatra avadhāryate tadā śrayasyā eva saṃvedanasya sarvatra anavadhāraṇāt tathā sati ca anavasthāyā viṣaya saṃcāraḥ  na syāt  tasmāt  tīvra saṃvegi tayā yad tu saṃvedanam avaśyam saṃvedanīyam yatra yatra ca aparaḥ  viśaṣataḥ sāmānyatas  vā vipratipadyate jijñāsate vā tatra tatra prāmāṇyam uktena apāyena avadhāraṇīyam iti atas  na anavasthā iti āśa yavān upasaṃhāra vyājena uktam artham saṃkalayya āha tasmāt atha saṃdehāt iti nanu artha aniśvayena api pravartamānaḥ  na hi tad sādhana tām anumāya pravartitum arhati arthitva abhāvāt na hi tad sādhanatva anumānam vyāpti grahaṇam vinā na ca saḥ  api pravṛtti vinā iti tad avastham eva itaretara āśraya tvam iti ata āha arthasya iti yadi api prāmāṇya aniścayavat apekṣita upāyatva aniścayena api tatra tatra pravartate tathā api apekṣita upāya tām pākṣikīm api urarīkṛtya pravṛttiḥ na ca tad saṃśayaḥ tasyām api anupalabdhāyām anyatra api syāt  atas  punar api upalabdhiḥ āyāta iti atas  anāditām ādāya eva parihṛtam artha pratipattiḥ iti vārttike yadi api artha śabdaḥ  apekṣita upāyam eva āha tasya eva pravṛtti viṣaya tvāt  aryamāna tvāt ca tathā api dharmi mātra pratipatti anumeya pratipattyoḥ bhinna kāla tvāt apekṣita tvāt ca tathā eva vyācaṣṭe artha pratipattiḥ iti nanu pramāṇasya prayojanavat tvam ākṣiptam vā samādhīyeta jijñāsitam vā jñāpyeta na tāvat ādyaḥ na hi asti puruṣaḥ  yaḥ pramāṇam niṣprayojanam iti brūyāt  tad mūla tvāt sarva puruṣa artha siddheḥ yasya tu puruṣa arthaḥ  na asti sa nirūcchvāsa eva śīryeta na api dvitīyaḥ tasya saṃśaya ādivat  sūtra pāṭhā anantaram eva jñāpayitum ucita tvāt ityata āha tatra idam iti na iyam pramāṇa prayojana jijñāsā kim nāma śāstra artha aubhūtasya parama nyāyasya niḥśreyasam prati guru pāya tve manyamānena laghīyati pravṛtti upāyam vidyamāne śāstra ārambha eva ākṣipyate sa ca samādhātum ārabdha iti arthaḥ daśānām duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam mumukṣutā dāḍhrayā artham ātmanaḥ  yāthātmyam sakala upādhi vinirmukta tvam tasya bhāvanam dhyānam ādi grahaṇena tu tad upāya bhūtāḥ pravṛttayaḥ  yama niyama āsana prāṇāyāma dhāraṇā lakṣaṇa gṛhyante ātma tattva sākṣātkāra iti samādhiḥ vairāgyam paramā vaśīkāraḥ paripākaḥ sa vāsana kleśa nirmokṣaḥ etena sāḍgopāḍgaḥ  yogaḥ  darśitaḥ śaḍkāmukvā bhāṣyam uttarayati tatra idam upaniṣṭhata iti tathā api nyāyasya guru pāya tve na parihṛtam nyāya nirṇota arthasya api pravṛtti apekṣāṇāt pravṛttasya nyāya anapekṣaṇāt ityata āha etad uktam bhavati iti nanu ubhayoḥ api tulya tve kutaḥ viśeṣāt  pramāṇam eva vyutpādyate na pravṛtti parītyata āha tathā api iti śravaṇa manana nididhi āsana sākṣātkāra lakṣaṇāyāḥ  pravṛtteḥ svarūpataḥ phalataḥ ca pramāṇa antarbhūta tvāt tad vyutpādanam eva pravṛtti vyutpādanam na ca pravṛtti vyutpādanena pramāṇam vyutpāditam bhavati na hi pravṛtteḥ phalam pramāṇam tad svarūpam vā iti arthaḥ nanu śāstra arthasya prayojana vyutpādana avasare pramāṇam arthavat iti kutas  na hi pramāṇam śāstrarthaḥ api tu nyāya iti ata āha sāmānya abhidhānam ca iti tad anena prabandhena niṣprayojanatva aśakya prayojanatva anabhimata prayojanatva upāya gaurava śaḍkāḥ parihṛtāḥ tad  kim aparam avaśiṣyate yad artham loka vṛttam anūdyata iti atas  prathama  tātparyam anusmārayan  eva vārttikam avatārayati prāmāṇya iti apramāṇena iti atra api yadi api vāñmanasa visaṃvādaḥ niṣedha vidhi upāya eva hi pramāṇam tasmāt niṣedha upāyatām jānataḥ  api apramāṇena niṣedhāmi iti vacanam manaḥ visaṃvādyava tathā api vyāmohāt api upapatteḥ evaṃbhūta abhiprāya sthairye api na asmākam kācid  kṣatiḥ iti etāvatā anujñā eva attaram dattam vāḍmanasayoḥ visaṃvāda iti prāmāṇya agrahe pramāṇena iti evam vaktum na śakyate tatas  pramāṇena iti evam vadataḥ  avaśyam prāmāṇyam manasi viparivartate tathā ca agṛhīta prāmāṇyena iti vacanam manaḥ visaṃvādi iti arthaḥ loka vṛttam abādhitaḥ  vyavahāra iti arthaḥ nanu pramāṇena khalu ayam jñāta ityādi bhāṣyam loka vṛtta anuvādaḥ  astu pramāṇata ityādi punar  katham iti ata āha kāraṇa pradarśana dvāreṇa iti na hi loka vṛttam svarūpeṇa upayujyate kim tarhi tasya avaśya abhyupeya tayā tad upāyaḥ  api avaśya abhyupeya iti anena abhisandhinā sa upāyam eva tad anūdyata iti arthaḥ āgāmi bhāṣye heya ādīnām sphuṭa tvāt  tasya idānīm akṣara arthaḥ  vyākriyata iti mā śaḍkiṣṭhā iti āha asya eva iti vārttika saṃbaddhaḥ  granthoḥ athapadāni iti ākāraḥ  vārttika granthaḥ tasya tādṛśa eva bhāṣya gataḥ  bhāṣya saṃbaddhaḥ  granthaḥ tasya iti arthaḥ amidheyānām paurvāparya niyamāya guṇa pradhāna bhāve jijñāsyamāne abhidhāna rūpasya śāstrasya kaḥ prastāva iti ata āha śāstra śabda iti evam tarhi heya ādīnām śāstra artha rūpa tayā na pṛthak koṭi tvam tathā ca eka koṭika tayā kim apekṣya guṇa pradhāna bhāva cintā ityata āha atra ca iti katham punar anena pramāṇa ādi caturvargaḥ  atra labhyate iti vārttikam anukta upālabhbhaḥ mā bhūt ityata āha tena iti tad mūla tvāt  itara siddheḥ iti siddhiḥ pratītiḥ niṣpattiḥ ca tatra heya upāyayoḥ pratītiḥ eva adhigantavyasya tu pratītiḥ niṣpattiḥ ca yadi api ca hānasya api pramāṇa rūpasya pratītiḥ asti eva tathā api pramāṇāt eva iti tad itarā iti uktam niṣpattiḥ tu hānasya ajñānāt eva yasmāt  kim tad jñānena jñānāt  tu yasmāt  tasya pramāṇa āyattatvam eva iti bhāvaḥ pramātṛ ādi caturvarge tu pramātṛ prameyayoḥ siddhiḥ pratītiḥ eva pramāyāḥ ca niṣpattiḥ api iti tad idam uktam pramāyāḥ ca tad kārya tvāt iti nanu pramātṛ ādīnām api prayojanavat tvāt arthavat iti anena kim pramāṇasya ādhikyam āhitam iti ata āha atiśāyane matuciti nanu asya caturvarga dvayasya niḥśreyasa adhigamam prati vikalpaḥ samuccayaḥ  vā ubhayam ā api anupapannam abhinna tvāt  tathā hi ya eva arthaḥ pramātā prameyam pramitiḥ iti sa eva heyaḥ  adhigantavya iti ya eva arthaḥ  hāna upāyau  iti sa eva pramāṇam iti saṃśaya ādīnām api nyāya parikara tayā nyāya śarīra tvāt  tasya ca pramāṇa tvāt iti tasmāt  abhinna tvāt  na vacana bhaḍgi bheda mātreṇa vikalpaḥ na api samuccayaḥ na hi bhavati tarūṇā vā vṛkṣeṇa vedam sādhanīyam tarūvṛkṣābhyām vetyata āha vivakṣā bhedenati tad anupapatteḥ iti ata anena nimitta bhedam abhipraiti tena ayam arthaḥ yadi api ubhayatra api ṣoḍaśa eva padārthāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ tathā api yathā pramāṇtvena pramāṇam jñeyam tathā hāna tvena api anyathā hāna antaram anuśriyeta nirarthakam ca pramāṇaṃsyāt  pramāṇa tve ca ajñāte hānatā na nirvahet  yathā ca sva rūpeṇa saṃśayāt ayaḥ  jñeyāḥ pramāṇa parikara tayā tathā hāna upāyatayā api anyathā upāya antaram anuśriyeta nirarthakāḥ ca ete syuḥ parikara tve ca ajñāte upāya tā na nirvahet  yathā ca śarīrādayaḥ  daśa prameya tayā jñeyāḥ tathā heya tayā api anyathā aheyāḥ syuḥ heya antaram ca anuśriyeta prameya tve ca ajñāte heya tā na nirvahet  yathā ca apavargaḥ prameya tayā jñeyaḥ tathā adhigantavya tayā api anyathā adhigamya antaram anuśriyeta anupādeyaḥ ca syāt  prameya tayā ca ajñāte adhigantavya tā na nirvaheta yathā ca ātmā prameya tayā adhigantavyaḥ tathā pramātṛ tayā api anyathā pramātṛ antaram anuśriyeta anavasthā ca syāt  prameya tve ca ajñāte sa upādhi nirūpa adhi rūpa tayā heya upādeyate na nirvaheca ātām yathā ca buddhiḥ buddhi tvena tathā tabhdedaḥ pramiti tayā api anyathā pramiti antaram anuśriyeta niṣphalam vā pramāṇam syāt  prameya tve ca ajñāte heya tā na nirvahet iti tasmāt  ta eva pramāṇa ādayaḥ ubhayathā jñāyantām iti vivakṣitvā ubhaya caturvarga upādānam kṛtam iti arthaḥ yad api uktam kaiścid  heya hāna upāya adhigantavyeṣu eva caturṣu puruṣa arthaḥ parisamāpyate yathā loke heyaḥ kaṇṭakaḥ hānam upānat  tad upāyaḥ tu pādukā kṛdātiḥ adhigantavyaḥ  duḥkha abhāvaḥ śāstre ca heyaḥ  rogaḥ cikitsā hānam tad upāyaḥ  nidāna jñānam adhigantavyam ārogyam iti atas caturṣu vaktavyeṣu ṣoḍaśa padārtha varṇanam kkopayujyata iti tadā api nirastam caturvargasya eva vivakṣā bhedāt  ṣoḍaśadhā bhedena abhidhānāt  vivakṣā bhedasya ca upapatti pratipadam bhāṣya kāra eva darśayiṣyati etad avagamyā eva yena adhikam coditam tad matam apākaroti etena iti vyākhyāyate avayavaśa iti viśeṣaṇe kriyāyāḥ tātparyam na tu viśeṣye iti arthaḥ etad eva attaratra sphuṭayati tatra asya avayaveṣu iti kasmāt  pramāṇāt iti na abhihitam evam hi asaṃdigdhā eva pañcamī syāt iti arthaḥ asya iti prakṛta pañcamī parāmarśe liṅga asaṃgati rityata āha asya iti pañcamyāḥ taseḥ prayogam darśayitvā pañcamī vyatirekeṇa taseḥ ākṣepa samādhāne asaṃgate iti ākṣepam vyākhyāya avatārayati vacana vyāpti artham iti nanu pramāṇābhyām pramāṇaiḥ iti bhavatam saṃplavaḥ pramāṇena iti tu katham iti ata āha yatra dvaya uditi viṣaya eka tā mātra saṃplavaḥ na tu kāraṇānām samuccayaḥ tathā sati phala bhedaḥ  na syāt  na api samuccitānām karaṇa tvam tathā sati vyāpāra bhedaḥ  na syāt iti jñāpana artham iti arthaḥ ata eva iti eva kāraḥ sādhakatama antaram vyavacchindan tasya vyāpāram phalam ca vyavacchinatti na tu asya sva vyā pārulayoḥ ita reta ra nairapekṣyam darśayati tasya saṃplave api saṃbhavāt iti arthaḥ kasmāt  punar  karaṇa arthaḥ  gamyate prakṛti pratyayayoḥ katarasmāt iti arthaḥ ayam āśayaḥ yadi tṛtīyayā karaṇa tvam abhidhīyate kim prakṛti sthena lyuṭpratyayena atha tena eva kim tṛtīyayā iti jñāpakasya kārakatva śaḍkā mā bhūt ityata āha artham artha adhigatim iti nanu hetu karaṇa bhāvaḥ  avagamyatām iti etad artham vibhakti vyāptiḥ āsthīyate pramāṇam iti prātipadikāt eva sākṣātkaraṇa tvam arthataḥ  hetu tvam gamyata iti kim vibhakti vyāptyā ityata āha atra ca iti na ca vācyam karaṇa bhāvena api pramāṇa phalayoḥ tādātmyam pratiṣedddhum śakyam tad  ki tad na āntarīyaka hetutabhdāvāmidhāna artham pañcamya iti sādhākatva mātrasya eva sāmarthye tam abarthasya asamartha tvāt  tatra vipratipatteḥ ca kasmāt iti praśna artham abhipretya āha pramāṇa pratipadikā iti tad evam anuvādaka tvam samarthayatā lyuṭtṛtīyayoḥ pauna rūkti am samāhitam na ca anuvādaka tvam śabda abhyāsasya prayojanavat tā vyatirekeṇa sidhyati iti atas  prayojanam darśayati pramākāraka antarebhya iti laukike tu prayoge saṃkhyā abhidhānāt vibhakteḥ sārthaka tvam draṣṭavyam iti viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvena saṃplava ākṣepaḥ  asaṃgata eva agni ādi viśiṣṭe parvata ādau pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ saṃplavāt ityata āha viśiṣṭaḥ  bhinna iti viṣayatva sāmānya abhiprāyam eka vacanam artha samārthya samuttham pratyakṣam yatas  ator atha gocaram tad  kim hetu tvam eva viṣaya lakṣaṇam na iti āha sa eva ca artha iti kim atas  cadyevam iti ata āha na ca sāmānyam iti nanu ca sāṃvyavahārikam sva lakṣaṇam api evam eva ityata āha sva lakṣaṇam iti deśa kālān anugatam vicāra saham iti arthaḥ nanu yadi api pratyakṣam na sāmānya rūpam avagāhate tathā api yadi anumānam api sva lakṣaṇam avagāheta tatas  eva tāvatā api saṃplavaḥ syāt iti ata āha na ca iti nanu bhavatu anumānam sāmānya mātra niyatam pratyakṣam api hi atra pravartsyati bhaviṣyati ca sāmānyam api sattvāt ākāra ādhāyakamatas  api saṃplava siddhiḥ iti ata āha na ca iti bhavitum arhati parama artha sat iti śeṣaḥ vicāra asaha tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ tad  kim sāmānyasya asattvāt sva lakṣaṇe ca pratibandha graha asaṃbhavāt anumānam nirviṣayam eva ityata āha tad idam iti tad  kim anumānam apramāṇam eva aparama artha gocara tvāt yadi evam katham tad anyat ullikhyānyatra pravartayati katham ca tad avisaṃvādakam katham ca bādhita ākāram pramāṇa tayā vyavahiyata iti ata āha tasmāt iti nanu pramāṇa antareṇa saha saṃplavaḥ  bhaviṣyati anayoḥ ityata āha na ca iti nanu asti śabda ādikam ityata āha pramāṇasya iti nanu na antarbhavati eva asva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvāt  viṣaya apratibaddha tvāt cetyata āha anantarbhāve ca iti nanu sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇayoḥ vyavasthāyām api pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ viṣaya antare saṃplavaḥ  bhaviṣyati anayoḥ asti hi viṣaya antaram tadvat iti āha na ca iti na hi asatā sāmānyena paramārtha sat  sva lakṣaṇam tadvat  bhavitum arhati sat asatoḥ saṃbandha abhāvāt iti arthaḥ saḥ  ayam gahanaḥ panthā iti āśayavān āha yathā ca etad iti viśeṣa iti atra yadi karmakārakam na ca tatas tadvat nāma aparaḥ  asti iti ata āha viśeṣa iti saṃplavam amṛṣyamāṇa  idam āha mīmāṃsaha iti śeṣaḥ adhigatam ca artham ityādi vārttikasya adhigatatva ādi va ārttikāt adhika artha tām vivakṣatra āha syāt etāt ityādi adhigater athe pramāṇa antarasya na tāvat artha adhigamam pratyupayogaḥ tasya prāgave pramāṇa antara siddha tvāt na api anttarottara vyavahāra pravāha nirvāha prati tasya api tad janya saṃskāra prabhava smṛti saṃtati siddha tvāt  na ca vācyam smṛti saṃtatiḥ adhigati saṃtatiḥ vā astu vyavahāra pravartinī na kaścid viśeṣa iti smṛtivat upadarśita artha mātra viṣaya tayā tāsām apramātvena tad sādhānasya apramāṇatva prasaṃgāt  tāsām ca tatas  eva smṛtitva prasaṃgāt  smṛti saṃtateḥ ca avaśyaṃbhāvitayā tatas  eva vyavahāri siddhau  adhigati saṃtati kalpanāyām kalpanā gaurava prasaṃga āditya āśayavān piṣṭa peṣaṇam eva upasaṃharati adhigatam iti nanu anyathā iti vārttike yadi kāraṇa gatam anya prakāra tvam vivakṣitam tadā kāraṇa gata prakāra bhede api na kaścid  viṣaya gataḥ  viśeṣaḥ piṣṭa peṣaṇa parihāra upayogī darśitaḥ syāt  atha viṣaya gata eva pramārabhadaḥ  darśitaḥ tadā anadhigata artha gantṛ tayā kutas  saṃplavaḥ na ca viṣaya abhede api pramāṇa bhedāt  kaścid  phala prakāra bhedaḥ prakṛta upayogavān asti iti ata āha ayam abhisandhiḥ iti piṣṭa peṣaṇe niṣphala tvam vā syāt  aviśiṣṭa phala
