viśeṣa niṣedhena kaṇṭhataḥ anumāna prāmāṇya niṣedhoḥ athatas  pratyakṣa prāmāṇya vidhiḥ ca vivakṣitaḥ na ca etad ubhayam api pramāṇam antareṇa sidhyati na ca atra pratyakṣam eva prabhavati iti cintitam ādi vākye na api śabda upamāne sva pratyaye tayoḥ anavakāśāt  para pratyaye api dharmya siddheḥ siddhau  api parasya āptatva aniḥ cayāt  tasmāt atīndriya vidhi niṣedhayoḥ anumānam anaḍgīkṛtya aśakya tvāt aśakyā apahnavam anumānam iti arthaḥ dṛṣṭa sādharmyam ca niyatam iti śeṣaḥ katham tena eva tasya aprāmāṇyam iti vyāghāta mātram vivakṣitam tena ayam arthaḥ yadi anu mānam apramāṇam katham tena eva vidhi niṣedha siddhiḥ atha tena vidhi niṣedha siddhiḥ katham tasya aprāmāṇyam iti kim ca anumānam anaḍgīkṛtya para pratyāyanāya śabda prayogaḥ  api ayam aśakyaḥ para vedana pratipatteḥ ava tad antareṇa aśakya tvāt na ced  para pratyāyanam nūnam aunmattyam āviṣkaroti vaktuḥ iti āha api ca iti sūtre vibhāgaḥ  api asti iti vyavacchidya āha lakṣaṇa sūtra tātparyamāhā iti syāt etad ativyāpakam iti atra avyāpakam ca iti api draṣṭavyam ata ubhaya vyutpādana upasaṃhāra virodhaḥ vigraha traya pradarśanam vigraha trayam draṣṭavyam iti arthaḥ vyāpti smṛti sahāyāt  dvitīya liṅga darśanāt eva anumiti siddheḥ alam tṛtīya liṅga darśana kalpanayā iti yathā śruta bhāṣya anusāriṇaḥ tān risyati na ca iti sa eṣa saṃskāra udbodham adhikam abhyupagacchataḥ  doṣa uktaḥ yaḥ tu sahakāri lābhāt anyaḥ na kaścid udbodhaḥ  nāma iti manyate tam pratyāha vinaśyat avasthasya iti na hi vyāpti smaraṇa mātrāt anumitiḥ na api liṅga darśana mātrāt kim tarhi vyāpti viśiṣṭa liṅga darśanāt  na ca vyāpti viśiṣṭam liṅgam ekaikasya ubhayasya vā gocaraḥ kim tu svatantram ubhayam ubhayasya na ca svatantra ubhaya jñāne api viśiṣṭa jñānam bhavati tad idam uktam paraspara vārtā anabhijña tayā svatantra sva sva viṣaya paryavasita tayā mithas  ghaṭana ayogaḥ  viśiṣṭa pratyaya yoga iti arthaḥ na ca svatantram etad ubhayam eka ātma samavāya mātreṇa anum iti bhāvayiṣyati iti vācyam dvitīya liṅga darśanam hi vasatu gatyā liṅga viṣayam iti etāvatā eva vyāpti smṛteḥ sahakāri liṅgatva rūpa ullekhitayā vā na tāvat ādyaḥ dūrāt  dhūma viṣaya vastutva jñānasya api prakāra antara āyāta vyāpti smṛtim prati sahakāritva prasaḍgāt dvitīyaḥ tu dvitīya liṅga darśane na asti eva tad idam uktam vṛttyā salvayam ghaṭayet  vyāpāreṇa na rūpataḥ  na ubhaya samavāyitā mātreṇa atiprasaḍgāt iti tasmāt  liṅgatva ullekhi tṛtīyam liṅga darśanam āstheyam itti āha tasmāt iti iha tādātmya tad utpatti svarūpa ādi niścaye pratibandha niścayaḥ tadā na syāt  yadi te eva pratibandhaḥ tābhyām samāna upāyaḥ  vā pratibandhaḥ tayoḥ eva vā pratibandha paryavasānam te eva vā pratibandha niścaya upāyaḥ tatra upāya tvam sahacāra avasāye vā vyabhicāra śaḍkā nirāse vā vyabhicāra śaḍkā api upādhi darśanāt  vā upādhi śaṅkayā vā bhūyaḥ bhūyas  sahacaritayoḥ api ulabdhayoḥ kayoḥ cidarthayoḥ vyabhicāra anusandhāna mātreṇa vā iti tatra ca sahacāra avasāyaḥ tāvat indriya sannikarṣa adhīna utpattiḥ tad utpatti aniścaye api vahni dhūmayoḥ sidhyati vyabhicāra śaḍkā api darśana yogya upādhi adhīnā yogyā anupalambha bādhāt eva nirastā atīndriyāḥ tu upādhayaḥ anyatra pramāṇa paridṛṣṭāḥ śaḍkitā api yathā nivartante tathā vakṣyāmaḥ pramāṇa patha anavatīrṇa upādhi śaḍkā tu tad utpatti niścayam api āskandati iti katham sā tena nivartanīyā iti āha atra ucyata iti sahacaritayoḥ vyabhicāra darśana mātreṇa tu vyabhicāra śaḍkā kārya kāraṇayoḥ api samānā tad utpatti lakṣaṇa viśeṣa siddhau vipakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā śaḍgāni vṛttiḥ iti yadi tadā asmākam api svābhāvika saṃbandha siddhau vipakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā eva śaḍkā nivṛttiḥ iti samaḥ samādhiḥ viśeṣaḥ tu svābhāvika saṃbandhasya vyāpaka tvam avyāpaka tvam tu tad utpatti ādeḥ iti āha api ca iti tad idam uktam sa ca yaḥ  vā sa vā iti na ca samāna upāya tvāt ubhayoḥ anyatarā niścaye na anyatara niścaya iti sāmpratam pratibandhā niścaye api hutāśa bhasmanoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva avadhāraṇāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvā niścaye api dhāma dhūmayoḥ pratibandha avabodhāt  yad anatītam eva vahnim anumimata iti āha api ca kāryāt iti tayoḥ eva pratibandhaḥ paryavasyati iti pakṣam nirācaṣṭe api ca rasāt iti yad tu bhede sati vyāpya vyāpaka abhāva eva kārya kāraṇa bhāva eva kārya kāraṇa bhāva iti vyudapādi prajñā kareṇa tad  pāpāt api pāpīyaḥ tathā hi niyāmaka virahe bhinnāyoḥ avyabhicāraḥ śaṣ kāka laḍka aḍkita tvāt duravadhāraṇa iti tām apanetum kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  anena upanītaḥ sa ced  rūpa eva katham tad niścayena eva avyabhicāra niścayaḥ na ca etad  kīrteḥ anumatam yad  rasena rūpa anumāne anyathā abhyupāyam āha yadi ca sarva loka siddham ativāhya svayaṅkṛta lakṣaṇaiḥ vyavahāraḥ tadā bhede satī iti etad api parihīyatām avyabhicāra mātram tad utpattiḥ iti eva astu laghu ca evam sati lakṣaṇam syāt  tad ā ātmanaḥ  api etad asti iti ced  astu śiśapā api vṛkṣa kāryam katham tena eva tad kartavyam iti ced  kaḥ  doṣaḥ asiddham siddhena sādhyate na tu tad eva siddham asiddham ca iti ced  hantā evam anāgatam api katham vyāpaka tā mātreṇa kāraṇam asiddha tvāt vartamānam api katham vyāpya tā mātreṇa kāryam siddha tvāt  evam samāna kāle api katham avinā abhāva mātreṇa kārya kāraṇa bhūte asiddha avasthāyām ubhayoḥ api asādhakatva aviśeṣāt siddha avasthāyām ubhayoḥ api asādhyatva aviśeṣāt tasmāt  pūrva kāla bhāva niyamaḥ kāraṇa tvam kaścāt bhāvita aniyamaḥ kāryatvam avinā abhauvaḥ tu niyama mātram iti eva jyāyaḥ api ca rasa rūpayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva niścayaḥ  vahni dhūmayoḥ iva pratyakṣānupalambha sādhyaḥ  vā syāt  kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhau puñjāt  puñja antara utpāttiḥ iti nyāyena vā ādyaḥ tāvat  kṣaṇayoḥ aśakya eva tayoḥ eva pratyakṣa an ārohāt tatra tasya aniścāyaka tvāt  santānayoḥ api duravabodhaḥ na hi vahneḥ iva rūpasya pūrva kālatā niyamam dhūmasya iva rasasya praścāt bhāvitā niyamam laukikāḥ pratipadyante kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhi nyāyaḥ tu na laukika iti vastu tas  laukikānām rasataḥ  rūpa anumānam na syāt iti āha laukikānām ca idam iti api ca iti anena te eva pratibandha iti nirastam tādātmyam tu gamya gamaka bhāve pratyuta viruddham iti āha api ca iti na hi tad eva karma niśceyam kartṛ  ca sva niścayena niścāyakam ca niścitā niścitayoḥ paraspara virodhāt iti arthaḥ bhava tu abhede api gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ tathā api na śiśapā tvena vṛkṣatva anumānam anavasara dusthātvāt  na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ sāmānyam aniścitam niścitaḥ tu viśeṣa iti āśaḍkya kenacid  samarthitam utthāpya dūṣayati yatu iti bhinnayoḥ eva vyāvṛttyoḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ kim tu abhinna adhyavaseya saṃbandhāt tayoḥ api tādātmyam vyavahniyata iti sa yadi abhinna devadatta saṃbandhāt  chatra kuṇḍalayoḥ api abhedam vyavaharati kaḥ  vārayitā kevalam pramāṇa prayojanayoḥ vyāvṛttiḥ laukika virodhaḥ ca iti anena abhiprāyeṇa upasaṃharati tasmāt ita asya idam kāryam kāraṇam iti ekaḥ saṃbandhaḥ svābhāvikam saṃbandham upasaṃhṛtya tasya svarūpam āha tathā hi iti svābhāvikaḥ  nirūpa ādhiḥ iti arthaḥ yadi api vyabhicāra avi abhicāra vyāpte aupādhika tvān aupādhika tve tābhyām ca vyabhicāra avi abhicārau  iti niyamaḥ tau hi na tāvat nirnimittau sārvatrikatva prasaḍgāt niyata viṣayau ca upalabhyete na api animittau sa upādheḥ api avyabhicāre nirūpa ādheḥ api vyabhicāre aniyama prasaḍgāt  tathā sati kārya ātmanoḥ api kāraṇa ātma vyabhicāraḥ prasajyeta tasmāt upādhau  avaśyam vyabhicāraḥ  anupādhau avaśyam avyabhicāraḥ vyabhicāre avaśyam upādhiḥ avyabhicāre avaśyam upādhyabhāvaḥ tathā api yatra sphuṭaḥ  vyabhicāraḥ tatra niṣphalam upādhi anusaraṇam tad artha tvāt tasya asphuṭe tu vyabhicāre tasya upayogaḥ na tu upādhi ta damau  asiddhaye vyabhicāra avi abhicāra paryeṣaṇam upayujyate vyabhicāra ādi siddhau satyām upādhi tada bhāva parīkṣāyāḥ  niṣphala tvāt  tasmāt anyonya vyāpti pradarśana mātra prayuktaḥ  vyabhicāram udbhāvyā api upādhim āha yadā tu iti yatas  na svābhāvikaḥ  na nirūpa adhikaḥ tatas  na niyataḥ  na avyabhicāri iti arthaḥ atha dhūma ādīnām api vahni ādibhiḥ katham svābhāvika iti ata āha svābhāvikaḥ tu iti nanu asphuṭe vyabhicāre saphalam upādhi anusaraṇam tad  kim atra na asau sphuṭa iti ata āha kvacid vyabhicārasya adarśanāt iti nanu kvacid  kadācid  vyabhicāraḥ  api syāt ayogya tvāt ca na dṛśyeta api ityata āha anupalabhyamānasya api kalpanā anupatteḥ anupalabhyamāna vyabhicāra kalpanā t vārī bhūta upādhi abhāvāt iti arthaḥ atas  niyataḥ avyabhicāri iti arthaḥ nanu upādhya bhāve anupalabhyamāna vyabhicāra kalpa nāna vakāśaḥ sa eva tu upādhya bhāvaḥ kutastya iti āśaṅkate na ca iti pariharati avaśyam iti upādhiḥ hi pramāṇa padavīm avatīrṇa eva vaktavyaḥ anyathā sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ sarvadā sarvatra sarveṣām jātyā kaścid  anupalabhyamānaḥ  api syāt upādhiḥ iti śaḍkā tad utpattau  api brahmaṇā api apanetum aśakyā nānā pramāṇa gocara artha sākṣāt kāravataḥ sarvajñasya api svabhāvata eva anupalabhyaḥ kaścid arthaḥ  bhavet  bhavet ca sarva pramāṇa apoḍham api kadācid advaitam prakṛti puruṣau vā niḥsvabhāva tā vā jagataḥ vedānām vā prāmāṇyam tad  katham caitya vandana ādau  api bhikṣuḥ pravarteta artha sandehāt  pravṛttiḥ iti ced  yatra pramāṇāni paribhūya śaḍkā apiśācī prasarati kutas tatra artha saṃbhāvanā api āstām tāvat  para loka pravṛttiḥ ihaloka pravṛttiḥ api na syāt  iti āha antata iti yadi api viśiṣṭa āhāra anantaram bhūyaḥ bhūyas  puṣṭi dhātu sāmya ādi daśyate maraṇam tam roga ādi anantaram eva tathā api āhāra viśeṣaḥ  maraṇasya eva hetuḥ kadācid  bhavet  katham anyathā ante tad antaram asya upalambhaḥ yad tu iyantam kālam na māritavān tad mantra pratibaddha vahnivat  kenacid  pratibaddha tvāt  sa eva pratibandhakaḥ puṣṭi ādi hetuḥ iti api saṃbhāvyeta roga ādikam eva ca puṣṭi ādi hetuḥ tad tu puṣṭi ādi kāle adṛśya tvāt eva na apalabhyate na hi puṣṭi ādi kāraṇaiḥ dṛśyaiḥ eva bhavitavyam iti api kadācid  syāt  yathā ca aprāmāṇika upādhi śaḍkyā vyabhicāritva śaṅkayā vā anumāna nivṛttiḥ tathā prāmāṇika anartha śaṅkayā eva viśiṣṭa āhāra bhojana ādi nivṛttiḥ iti arthaḥ tasmāt utprekṣita artha niścayavat tad śaḍkā api bandhyā eva pramitasya eva tu niścayavat  śaḍkā api samīha upayoginī iti āha tasmāt iti tad ayam saṃkṣepaḥ vyabhicāra eva pratibandha abhāvaḥ upādheḥ eva vyabhicāra aśaḍkā pramāṇa niścita eva upādhi tvena śaṅkanīyaḥ sādhane sa upādhiḥ sādhye nirūpa ādhiḥ eva upādhi tvena niśceyaḥ atas  anyaḥ ca anyathā tvena iti pramāṇa paridṛṣṭeṣu eva kaścid upādhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ata āha prayatnena iti ayam prayatna arthaḥ pratyakṣa upalabhyāḥ tāvat  yogyā anupalabdheḥ eva nirastāḥ pramāṇa antara paridṛṣṭānām api vyāpakānām upādhi tve vahneḥ sārvatrikatva prasaṅgaḥ avyāpakānam api nityānām upādhi tve bahneḥ sadā anuvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ anityāḥ tu trividhāḥ ubhaya avi abhicāriṇaḥ ubhaya vyabhicāriṇaḥ anyatara avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca iti tatra prathama dvitīyā upādhi lakṣaṇa abhāvāt eva na upādhayaḥ anyatara avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca dvividhāḥ dhūma mātra avyabhicāriṇaḥ  vahni mātra avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca iti pūrve lakṣaṇa abhāvāt eva na upādhayaḥ vahni mātra avyabhicāriṇaḥ  api dvividhāḥ vyāpya mātra rūpā ubhaya rūpāḥ ca iti pūrvavat eva pūrve ubhaya rūpāḥ tu sāmagrītaḥ na api pare vidyante sā ca na kvacid upādhiḥ dhūmasya vahninā iva tayā api svabhāva saṃbandhāt vahni janana sāmagryām vahneḥ api antar bhāvāt ca na ca kṛtaka tvān uṣṇa tvayoḥ saṃbandhe tejaḥ jātīya itara tvavat iha api sādhya dharma jātīya itara tvam upādhiḥ tasya pramāṇa bādha eka mātra niyata tvāt  ata eva upādhim apaśyantaḥ  api virodhi pramāṇa sadasadbhāva niścaya vyagra tayā muhūrtam anumitau vilambāmahe tad evam sarvathā upādhi anupalambhāt  tad abhāva niścayaḥ  yathā dhūma saṃbandhe tathā anyatra api draṣṭavyaḥ tarkaḥ ca sarva śaḍkā nirākaraṇa paṭīyān vijayata iti nanu pramāṇa siddhe vastuni svabhāvaḥ  avalambanam na tu svabhāva avalambanena eva vastu vyavasthā iti āśayavān pṛcchati kena punar iti prathama darśanena eva vahni dhūmayoḥ avyabhicāra grahaṇam dvitīya ādibhiḥ tu śaḍkā mātram apanīyata iti keṣāñcit matam apanayan  eva prakṛtam prapañcayati yadā tāvat iti atra ca eṣa parama arthaḥ yaḥ  ayam upādhim ādāya yena saha saṃbadhyate sa nirūpa adhyavasthāyām tasya āgamakaḥ  yathā vahniḥ dhūmasya sa upādhi avasthāyām api upādheḥ kevalasya eva sāmarthye sa eva gamakaḥ  na tu upahitaḥ yathā āhāra pariṇati bhedasya eva gamaka tve maitra tanaya tvam yatra tu upādhiḥ kevalaḥ  vyabhicārī tatra sa upādhiḥ api gamaka eva yathā ārdra indhanavān vahniḥ dhūmasya iti tad  kasya hetoḥ viśiṣṭasya nirūpa adhi tvāt iti bhūyas darśanam iti tad janita saṃskāra sahitam indriyam iti arthaḥ agre ca etad eva sphuṭīkṛtam iti avirodhaḥ maṇi bheda tattvavat iti yathā maṇiḥ yaiḥ yaiḥ viśeṣaiḥ tad tad vyavahāra viṣayaḥ  bhavati dhārayituḥ ca tad tad phala bheda saṃpādakaḥ ca unnīyate te te sūkṣmā viśeṣāḥ parīkṣakaiḥ bhūyobhiḥ darśanaiḥ ūnnīyante tathā atrāpi iti tathā hi prathamatas tāvat  bhūyas darśanam kākatālīya nyāya vyudāsāya tatas  sātatya ūrdhva gati ādi viśeṣa avasāyāya tatas  upādhi śaḍkā nirāśāya atra ca na vāraṃsakhyā niyame abhyupayogaḥ mṛdu madhya adhimātra buddhi bhedena puṃsām vicitra śakti tvāt  na ca evam sati lakṣaṇa śāstra vaiyarthyam aniyata vāra viśiṣṭa tattva sākṣātkārau  adhiyoga abhyāsa upadeśavat iha api nirūpa ādhi saṃbandha bodha avadhi niyamāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva avagame api ayam eva mārgaḥ  na tu pañca pratyakṣa anupalambhāḥ anyatas  anāgatasya tatra asataḥ tad anantaram upalambhe api tatas  anyasmāt anutpatteḥ bhāva mātreṇa niścetum aśakyatvāt    kākatālīya nyāyena api saṃbhavāt  bhūyas pravṛttau tu yadi na vyabhicāra upalambhaḥ upādhi upalambhaḥ  api na syāt  dvaya upagame tu tad niyataḥ saṃbandha iti syāt etad  dhūma ādīnām maitra tanayatva ādīnām ca bhūyas darśanatva aviśeṣe api kutaḥ viśeṣāt ekasya gamaka tvam aparasya natyata āha na ca iti yad  tu atra uktam yathā hi anārda indhane vahnau na dhūma iti vahneḥ tad saṃbandhe tathāvidham indhanam upādhiḥ tathā yadi maitrāt jātasya api kasyacid  vivakṣita āhāra pariṇati viraheṇa śyāmatā upālapsyata sa upādhiḥ niraceṣyata na tu etad asti tathā sati api ca upādhivādaḥ  vyarthaḥ vyabhicārāt eva maitra tanayasya ahetu tvāt iti tad idam anavadhārita upādhi lakṣaṇasya sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam na kiñcid eva tathā hi na upahitasya niścita eva sādhya vyabhicāraḥ upādheḥ lakṣaṇam kim nāma sādhana avyāpaka tve sati sādhya vyāpaka tvam tad ca sādhya abhimata dhūma śyāma tve prati vyāpaka tvem ārdra indhana anna pāna pariṇati bhedayoḥ aviśiṣṭam aviśiṣṭam ca sādhana abhimata dahana maitra tanaya tve prati tayoḥ avyāpaka tvam iyān  tu viśeṣaḥ vahneḥ dhūmena iva ārdra indhanena api sākṣāt eva vinā abhāva upalabhyate maitra tanayasya tu śyāma tvena iva anna pāna pariṇāmena api upādheḥ eva unnīyata iti nanu vajre loha lekhya tvam prati pārthivatva hetoḥ ka upādhiḥ praśithila avayava tvam tarhi tad nivṛttau paveḥ iva sphaṭika ādau  api loha lekhyatva nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ na khalu nibiḍa avayava tvena ubhayoḥ kaścid  viśeṣaḥ na mṛd ādibhyaḥ  nibiḍa avayava tve api sphaṭikasya praśithila avayava tvāt eva na hi adbhyaḥ  medinī nibiḍa iti na praśithila avayavā iyān  tu viśeṣaḥ yathā yathā śaithilya apakarṣaḥ tathā tathā lekhituḥ prayatna prakarṣaḥ yadi tu śaithilyam aprayojakam tadā mṛd kāṣṭha pāṣāṇa ādiṣu prayatna prakarṣaḥ  api viphalaḥ pārthiva tvasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt sphaṭike katham eṣā pratipattiḥ iti ced  loha lekhya tvāt eva loha lekhyatva praśithila avayava tvayoḥ samavyāptika tvāt  ata eva anayoḥ ekatara pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ eva anyatara pravṛtti nivṛttī na tu pārthivatva pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ eva loha lekhyatva pravṛtti nivṛttī vajre adarśanāt    jala ādau darśanāt ca vahnau  anuṣṇatva sādhanasya tu kṛtaka tvasya tad jātīya itaratva lakṣaṇam upādhiḥ sa ca bādha eka niyata viṣaya iti na ati prasaṅga iti uktam tad etad sarvam hṛdi nidhāya āha iti ādaya iti yadi api dvitīya liṅga darśanasya smṛtyā saha vinaśyat avasthasya eva parāmarśa janaka tvam kvacid  tathā api yatra dṛṣṭa mātra eva vahni nivṛttau nivṛttaḥ  dhūmaḥ kāla antare jijñāsā vaśāt parāmṛśyate tatra dvayoḥ api liṅga darśanayoḥ atīta tvam iti āśayavatā uktam yadi api ityādi yena ca parāmarśaḥ  na iṣyate tena vākyasya caturthaḥ  avayava apanayaḥ  api na īṣitavyaḥ pakṣa dharma tā pratipādanena tasya upayogaḥ para artha anumāne sva artha anumāne tu sā dvitīya liṅga darśanāt eva avagata iti kim parāmarśena iti ced  na pakṣa dharma tā hi vyāptyā saha pratisaṃhita anumāna upayoginī tādṛśī ca upanayena pradarśyate na tu dvitīya liṅga darśanena tasya tu vyāpti anusandhāna rahitam pakṣa dharma tā mātram eva gocaraḥ na ca tad anumāna upayogi tasmāt upanaya arthaḥ  na dvitīya liṅga darśana viṣayaḥ tatas  sva artha anumāne yadi asti tasya upayogaḥ nūnam parāmarśaḥ  api tṛtīyaḥ svīkartavyaḥ na asti ced  para artha anumāne api liṅga parāmarśa eka arthaḥ upanayaḥ  api na adaraṇīyaḥ tulya viṣaya tvāt iti āśayavān saṃkalayya anayoḥ samāna viṣaya tvam āha saṃbandha iti nanu vyāpāra anubandhi tayā viṣaya tvam viṣaya tve ca vyāpāra anubandha iti paraspara āśraya tvam atha vyāpāra anubandhi tayā eva viṣaya tvam tathā api asaṃbaddhatva aviśeṣāt  katham tasya eva vyāpāra anubandhitā iti āśaḍkya pariharati na ca atiprasaṅga iti na dhūma jñānasya agniḥ svatantrasya vyāpāra viṣayaḥ  yena asaṃbaddhatva aviśeṣāt ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt  kim tu jñeya viśeṣaṇasya tasya ca jñāyamānasya dhūmasya agninā saha niyāmakaḥ svabhāva saṃbandha eva atas  na ati prasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ pūrvam lakṣya padārtha praśna avasare anumīyate anena iti kāraṇa artha iti uttaram dattam idānīm anumitiḥ kasyāñcit avasthāyām anumānam pramāṇam bhavena vā iti vijñāsā praśne bhāvaḥ karaṇam vā iti uttaram atas  na virodhaḥ  aśataḥ pauna rūkti am vā atas  ṭīkā kṛt  api vyāpāra tvena apramāṇyam pūrva pakṣayitvā phala antara hetutvena prāmāṇyam samarthayati sma iha yadi api vijñāna pramāṇayoḥ anyatara adhikāreṇa saṃskāra nirṇayayoḥ vyudāsaḥ vijñāna adhikāre hi tad pūrvakam anubhava kāraṇam anumānam iti sūtra saṃbandhaḥ na ca evaṃbhūtau saṃskāra nirṇaya viśeṣau tayoḥ anubhavam pratyahetutvāt  pramāṇa adhikāra api phalataḥ sa eva arthaḥ tad pūrvakam pramākaraṇam anumānam iti sūtra saṃbandhāt  tathā api vivakṣā bhedāt  vikalpena ubhayam ubhayatra saṃbhantsyata iti vivakṣitvā ekaika kaniṣṭhatayā ekaikam darśitam iti tathā eva vyākhyātavān vastutas tu ubhayam ubhayatra saṃbaddham iti nigarvaḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ iti vārttike bahu vrīhi samāsa sthitaḥ  viśeṣaṇa tayā vyatirekaḥ  niṣkṛṣya sva pradhāna tayā tad puruṣa padena pradarśitaḥ  vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ vyatireka iti atas  na vārttike hetu sāmāna adhikaraṇya virodhaḥ vyatireka abhāvam vyatireka nirūpaṇa abhāvam iti arthaḥ iha avastunaḥ  vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra viṣaya tvam laukika samīha anurodhāt  vā śukti rajatavat rajju sarpavat ca pramāṇa anurodhāt  vā gandham prati pṛthivīvat udakavat  vā vacana mātra anurodhāt  vā pradhānavat  śaśa viṣāṇavat ca mūḍha praśna anurodhāt  vā dharma antaram prati pūrvavat eva sva vacana virodha bhayāt  vā iti tatra prathamaḥ tāvat avastuni asaṃbhavī laukika pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ vastu mātra viṣaya tvāt dvitīya ādiṣu eva ca paramparayā praviśati iti na pṛthak  nirākriyate dvitīya nirākaraṇāya prāmāṇika niṣedha vyavahāra rītim āha sadbhyām iti yadi tad viviktā itara svabhāvaḥ  abhāvaḥ  yadi coma yatha atirikta svabhāvaḥ ubhayathā api niṣedhya niṣedha adhikaraṇābhyām eva nirūpyate na tu ekena satā niṣedhyena niṣedha adhikaraṇena vā iti arthaḥ nanu sata eva kutaścid  pramāṇa pratītāt nivartsyati iti ata āha pakṣāt anyasya iti tad anena asati adhikaraṇe nivṛtti nirūpaṇam pratiṣiddham nivṛttau tu mūka tā eva ucitā iti hṛdayam nivṛttiḥ eva pratiṣiddhā iti bhrāntaḥ tu codayati na nivartate ced iti nirūpaṇam ādāya eva pariharati yasya iti yatra khalu bhāvaḥ sarvathā eva na nirūpitaḥ tad adhikaraṇa tayā tasya anyatra upalabdhasya abhāvaḥ  nirūpyata iti dṛṣṭam yathā gavi dṛṣṭasya śruṅgasya śaśe yatra tu śṛḍga abhāvaḥ  api gagana kamala ādau nirūpayitum na śakyate tatra śṛṅgam eva nirūpyata iti alaukikam iti arthaḥ punar bhrāntaḥ śaṅkate tad  kim idānīm iti sva vacana virodha bhayam āśaṅkate nanu ca iti tad uktam jñāna śriyā dharmasya kasyacid avastuni māna siddhā bādhā vidhi vyavahṛtiḥ kim iha asti naḥ vā kkā apyasti ced  katham iyanti na ḍhūṣaṇāni na asti eva ced  sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ iti yadi api sva vacana virodha bhiyā api sarvathā vicāra asahor athaḥ svīkartum na śakyate vacanāt  vicāraḥ  garīyān iti nyāyāt  anyathā vikalpa śabdau na vastu gocarau  iti sva vacana virodhāt eva parihartavyam tathā hi sva lakṣaṇasya asādha araṇyena aśakya samaya gocara tayā śabdasya ca samaya adhīna pravṛttika tayā vikalpasya ca tad eka viṣaya tayā na tayoḥ vastu gocara tvam iti vicāre śabdasya kācid api vastuni māna siddhā bādhā vidhi vyavahṛtiḥ kim āha asti naḥ vā asti eva ced  katham iyanti na dūṣaṇāni na asti eva ced  sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ iti tulyā vibhīṣikā tathā api tattvam nirūpayan pariharati na vai tad tvata iti nanu yadi na ekatara niṣedhaḥ  vidhiḥ vā tad  kim ubhaya vidhiḥ niṣedhaḥ  vā tathā sati atitarā durghaṭam āpadyeta ityata āha naḥ khalu iti nanu sarva vyavahārā bhājanam iti api niṣedha vyavahāra bhājana tvena eva nirvahet  anyathā punar api sva vacana pratirodha iti ata āha upayoge vā iti sva vacana pratirodha bhayāt hi tadā niṣedha vyavahāra gocaratva svīkāraḥ syāt  yadi tathā sati bhayam nivarteta na tu etad asti naḥ khalu sakala vyavahāra ābhājanam ca tad niṣedha vyavahāra bhājanam ca iti vacanam parasparam avirodhi vidhi vyavahāra mātra abhiprāyeṇa abhājanatva vyavahāre kutaḥ virodha iti ced  hanta   sakala vidhi niṣedha vyavahāra abhājana tvena kiñcid  vyavahniyate na vā ubhayathā api sva vacana virodhaḥ ubhayathā api avastunā eva tena bhavitavyam vastunaḥ sarva vyavahāra viraha anupapatteḥ na iti pakṣe sakala vidhi niṣedha vyavahārā bhājanam iti anena eva vyavahāreṇa virodhāt  avyavahṛtasya niṣeddhum aśakyatvāt  vyavahniyata iti pakṣe tu viṣaya svarūpa paryālocanena eva virodhāt  na hi sarva vyavahāra ābhājanam ca vyavahniyate ca iti ca api ca yadi avastunaḥ  niṣedha vyavahāra gocara tvam vidhi vyavahāra viṣaya tā api kim na syāt  pramāṇa abhāvasya ubhayatra api tulya tvāt  bandhyā sutasya avaktṛ tve acetanatva ādikam eva pramāṇam vaktṛ tve tu na kiñcid iti ced  na tatra api suta tvasya vidyamāna tvāt  na hi bandhyāyāḥ sutaḥ  na sutaḥ tathā sati sva vacana virodhāt  vacana mātram etad na tu paramārthataḥ suta eva asau  iti ced  acetanasya api evaṃrūpa tvāt cetanāt anyat svabhāva antaram eva acetanam iti ucyate caitanya nivṛtti mātram eva vivakṣitam iha tad ca saṃbhavati eva iti ced  na tatra api asutatva nivṛtti mātrasya eva vivakṣita tvāt  asutatva nivṛtti mātrasya svarūpataḥ kṛti jñaptyoḥ asāmarthye samartham artha antaram avaseyam anantarbhāvya kutaḥ hetu tvam iti ced  na acaitanye api asya nyāyasya samāna tvāt  vyāvṛtti rūpam api ca tad eva gamakam yad atasmāt eva yathā śiṃśapā tvam bandhyā sutaḥ tu asutāt iva ghaṭa ādeḥ sutāt api devadatta ādeḥ vyāvartate atas  na hetuḥ iti ced  nanu acaitanyam api asya evam rūpam eva na hi bandhyā sutaḥ cetanāt iva deva datta ādeḥ cetanāt api kāṣṭha ādeḥ na vyāvartate atas  na hetuḥ iti vaktṛ tvam vastu eka niyataḥ  dharmaḥ sa katham avastuni sādhyaḥ  virodhāt iti ced  sa punar ayam virodhaḥ kutas  pramāṇāt  siddhaḥ kim vaktṛtva viviktasya avastunaḥ  niyamena upalambhāt  āhosvit  vastu viviktasya vaktṛ tvasya anupālambhāt iti na tāvat avastu kenacid  pramāṇena upalambha gocaraḥ tathā tve vā na avastu na api uttaraḥ samāna tvāt  na hi avaktṛ tvam api vastu viviktam kasyacid  pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ tad vivikta vikalpana mātram tāvat asti iti ced  tad saṃsṛṣṭi vikalpane api kaḥ  vārāyitā nanu vaktṛ tvam vacanam prati kartṛ tvam tad  katham avastuni tasya sāma arthya viraha lakṣaṇa tvāt iti ced  atha avaktṛ tvam api katham tatra tasya vacana itara kartṛtva lakṣaṇa tvāt sarva sāmarthya virahe vacana sāmarthya virahaḥ  na viruddha iti ced  atha sarva sāmarthya virahaḥ  bandhyā sutasya kutas  pramāṇāt  siddhaḥ avastu tvāt eva iti ced  nanu etad api katham sarva sāmarthya virahāt eva iti ced  soyam kevalaiḥ vacanaiḥ itas tatas  nirdhana adhamarṇika iva sādhūn bhrāmayan paraspara āśraya doṣam api na paśyati krama yaugapadya virahāt iti ced  na tad viraha siddhau  api pramāṇa anuyogasya anuvṛtteḥ suta tve ca parāmṛṣyamāṇe tad avinābhūta sakala vaktṛtva ādi dharma prasaktau kutas  krama yaugapadya viraha sādhanasya avakāśaḥ kutastarām ca avastu sādhanasya kutas tamām ca avaktṛtva ādi sādhanānām tatas ca pramāṇam eva sīmā vyavahāra niyamasya tad atikrame tu aniyama eva iti anena abhiprāyeṇa idam uktam upayoge vā niṣedha vyavahāra upayoge vā na nirūpa ākhyaḥ  na vidhi vyavahāra aviṣayaḥ yasmin kiñcid niṣidhyate pramāṇena tasmin kiñcid  vidhīra api iti niyamāt iti arthaḥ tatra praṣṭuru uttare vaktavye na viruddham anarthakam vā vaktum ucitam iti āśa yavān āha kasatarhi iti uttaram atha iti anuttara viṣaye ahṛdayaiḥ yad eva uttarīkriyate tad eva viruddham iti arthaḥ na ca kevalam atra uttara daḥ praṣṭāpya hṛdaya eva na hi apratīte deva datta ādau sa kim gaura kṛṣṇaḥ  vā iti vaiyātyam vinā praśnaḥ tatra api yadi ekaḥ  apratīta parama artha viṣaya eva uttaram dadāti na gaura iti aparaḥ  api kim na dadyāt  gaura iti na ca evam sati kācid artha siddhiḥ pramāṇa abhāva virodhayoḥ ūbha yatra api tulya tvāt  tad idam uktam ahṛdaya vācām iti nanu apratīte vyahāra abhāva iti yuktam kūrma roma ādayaḥ tu pratīyanta eva na hi ete vikalpāḥ kañcid artha bhedam anullikhanta eva utpadyante na ca pramāṇa āspadam eva vyavahāra āspadam iti asti niyama iti ata āha na ca atyanta iti yadi api sarvathā pratīte vyavahāra abhāva iti vadataḥ  bauddhasya api sva vacana virodha eva tathā api ayam virodhaḥ prāk eva udbhāvita prāya iti enam upekṣya śaḍkā mātram samarthitam tathā hi śaśaviṣāṇam iti jñānam anyathā khyātiḥ syāt asat khyātiḥ vā na tāvat ādyaḥ te rocate tathā sati kiñcid āropyam kiñci dāra upaviṣaya iti syāt  tathā cāra upaviṣayaḥ tatra eva asti āropaṇīyam tu anyatra iti jitam naiyāyikaiḥ na api dvitīyaḥ kāraṇa anupapatteḥ indriyasya jñāna janane sva viṣaya ādhipatyena eva vyāpārāt  liṅga śabda ābhāsayoḥ api anyathā ākhyāti janaka tvāt  apahastitasva arthayoḥ ca asat khyāti janaka tve śaśa viṣāṇa śabdāt  kūrma roma ādi vikalpānām api utpatti prasaṅgaḥ niyāmaka abhāvāt sa hi saḍketa u vā syāt  śabda svābhāvyam vā na tāvat ādyaḥ saḍketa viṣaya apratīteḥ nirākṛta tvāt  ata eva pratīteḥ itaretara āśraya tvam pada saḍketa balena tu pravṛttau sva artha aparityāgāt  tathā ca ananvitāḥ padārthā eva anvitatayā parisphuranti iti viparīta khyātiḥ eva āvartate sva artha parityāge tu punar api aniyamaḥ asāmayika artha pratyāyanāt  śabda sva abhāvyāt  tu niyame vyutpannavat avyutpannasi api tathāvidha vikalpa udaya prasaṅgaḥ vāsanā viśeṣāt iti ced  atha āsat ullekhinaḥ pratyayasya vāsanā eva kāraṇam uta vāsanā api na tāvat ādyaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādi pratyayānām sadātanatva prasaḍgāt kadācid  vāsanāyāḥ prabodhāt  kadācid iti ced  na prabodhaḥ  api sahakārī antaram vā atiśaya paramparā paripākaḥ  vā ādye vāsanā eva iti pakṣānupapatti dvitīyaḥ  api yadā artha antara pratyāsatteḥ tadā pūrvavat  sva santati mātra adhīna tve tu bāhya vāda vyāghātaḥ nīla ādi buddhīnām api vāsanā paripākāt eva utpādāt  vāsanā api iti pakṣe tu tad anyaḥ  api kaścat hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ sa vicāryamāṇaḥ pūrvam nyāyam na ativartata iti na ca śaśa viṣāṇa ādi śabdānām asat arthaiḥ saha sambandha avagamaḥ  api tathā hi para buddhīnām anullekhāt  tad viṣayasya api anullekha eva na ca artha kriyā viśeṣaḥ  api asti yatas  viṣaya viśeṣam unnīya tatra saḍketa u gṛhyatām na ca saḍketayituḥ eva vacanāt  tad avagamaḥ tad viṣayāṇām vacanānām sarveṣām eva apratīta viṣaya tvena agṛhīta samaya tayā apratipādaka tvāt  na ca śaśa viṣāṇa śabdam uccārayataḥ kaścid abhiprāyaḥ  vṛttaḥ tad viṣayaḥ  asya vācya iti sugrahaḥ samaya iti vācyam na hi evam ākāraḥ samaya grahaḥ gām badhāna iti ukte apratīta śabda arthasya abhiprāya mātra pratītau samaya graha prasaḍgāt  na ca viśeṣa antara vinākṛtaḥ kalpanā mātra viṣayaḥ  asya vācya iti sāmpratam ghaṭa kūrma roma ādīnā api tad arthatva prasaḍgāt na ca sarve pratipattāraḥ sva vāsanayā asat artha śabda sambandha pratipatti bhāja iti sāmpratam paraspara vārtā anabhijña tayā apara arthatva prasaḍgāt  na hi svayaṅkṛtam saḍketam agrāhayitvā paraḥ  vyavahārayitum śakyate na ca vyavahāra upadeśau  antareṇa grāhayitum api na ca gām badhāna itivat  śaśa viṣāṇa apadārthe vṛddha vyavahāraḥ na ca ayam asāvaḥ ca itivat upadeśaḥ na ca yathā gauḥ tathā gavaya itivat upalakṣaṇa atideśaḥ na ca iha prabhinna kamala udare madhūni madhukaraḥ pibati itivat  prasiddha pada sāmānādhikaraṇyam tad amūḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādi kalpanā na asat khyāti rūpāḥ tathā tve kāraṇa abhāvāt bhūka svapnavat asā vyavahārikatva prasaḍgāt ca tasmāt anyathā ākhyāti rūpā eva iti na etad anurodhena api avastunaḥ  niṣedha vyavahāra gocara tvam iti arthaḥ bhavatu tathā api na asau siddhi upālambha yogī iti āha kalpita gocaraḥ ca iti tathā hi kaḥ  ayam vyatirekaḥ  nāma yadyatas  vyatiricyate tasya tatra abhāvaḥ  vā tad abhāva svabhāva tvam vā tatra na tāvat  krama yaugapadyayoḥ śaśa viṣāṇe abhāvaḥ pramāṇa gocaraḥ vṛkṣa rahita bhūbhṛt kaṭakavat  krama yaugapadya rahitasya śaśa viṣāṇasya pramāṇa aviṣaya tvāt na api krama yaugapadya abhāva rūpa tvam śaśa viṣāṇasya prāmāṇikam ghaṭa abhāvavat  śaśa viṣāṇasya pramāṇeṇa anupalambhāt  ghaṭa abhāvaḥ  api na pramāṇa gocara iti ced  na tasya tad viviktā itara svabhāvasya api pramāṇata eva siddheḥ asiddhau vā tatra api avyavahāra eva ghaṭaḥ tāvat  svābhāva viraha svabhāvaḥ pramāṇa siddhaḥ tādrūpyeṇa kadācid api anupalambhāt  etāvatā eva tad abhāvaḥ  api ghaṭa viraha svabhāvaḥ siddha iti ced  na ghaṭa abhāvasya tad viraha svabhāvatva anabhyupagamāt  na ca anyasya svabhāve pramāṇa gocare tad anyaḥ  api siddhaḥ syāt  atiprasaḍgāt  evaṃbhūtau  eva ghaṭa tada bhāvau yad ekasya paricchittiḥ eva aparasya vyavasthitiḥ iti ced  na ghaṭavat  ghaṭa abhāvasya api prāmāṇikatva anabhyupagame svabhāva vāda anabhyupagamāt  pramāṇa siddhe hi vastuni svabhāva vāda ālambanam na tu svabhāva vāda ālambanena eva vastu paricchittiḥ iti hi bhavatām eva tatra tatra jayadundubhiḥ yad uktam vārtikālaḍkāre yaktiñcit ātma abhimatam vidhāya nirūttaraḥ tatra kṛtaḥ padeṇa vastu svabhāvaiḥ iti vācayam ittham tadā uttaram syāt  vijayī samastaḥ tad  kim idānīm svābhāva viraha svabhāvaḥ  ghaṭaḥ pramāṇān ā eva siddhaḥ tava dṛṣṭyā evam etad  ghaṭaḥ  hi yādṛś tādṛś svabhāvaḥ tāvat  pramāṇa patham avatīrṇaḥ tasya yadi paramārthataḥ abhāvaḥ  api kaścid  syāt  paramārthataḥ saḥ  api tad viraha svabhāva iti tathā eva pramāṇa āveditaḥ syāt  na ca etad abhyupagamyate bhavatā tasmāt  ghaṭavat  tad abhāvasya api prāmāṇika tvena eva anayoḥ paraspara viraha lakṣaṇa vyatireka siddhiḥ aprāmāṇika tve vā anayoḥ api na tathā abhāva iti śaśa viṣāṇa ādiṣu api iyam eva gatiḥ nanu kālpanika rūpa saṃpattiḥ eva astu anumāna aṅgam iti ata āha tasyāḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt ita dahanavattva ādi sādhane prameyatva ādau śabda anityatva ādi sādhane cākṣuṣatva ādau nityatva ādi sādhane kṛtakatva ādau  iti arthaḥ nanu pakṣa sa pakṣa vipakṣāḥ tāvat  vastu avastu bhedena dvi rūpāḥ tatra ye kalpanā upanītāḥ tatra kālpanikā eva pakṣa dharmatva anvaya vyatirekāḥ pramāṇa upanīteṣu tu prāmāṇikā eva iti vibhāgaḥ tad iha kālpanikāt niragneḥ yadi api prameyatva ādeḥ vyāvṛttiḥ kālpanikī siddhā tathā api prāmāṇikāt  jalahnada ādeḥ prāmāṇikyevaiṣitavyā sā ca na siddhā iti kutas tasya hetu tvam evam prāmāṇikāt  śabde api pakṣīkṛte prāmāṇika eva hetu sadbhāvaḥ  vaktavyaḥ na ca asau cākṣuṣa tvasya asti iti saḥ  api katham hetuḥ evam kṛtaka tvasya api vastu eka niyatasya dharmasya vāstava eva anvayaḥ  vaktavyaḥ vastunaḥ  vipakṣāt ca vāstava eva vyatirekaḥ  vaktavyaḥ na ca tasya tau staḥ tad  katham asau  api hetuḥ iti pralapitam etad  na hi niyāmakam antareṇa saṃpadam prati kalpanā tvarate vipadam prati tu vilambata iti śakyam vaktum tathā ca niragnikam api kūrma roma sa dhūmam iti kalpanā mātreṇa vipakṣa vṛtti tvāt  dhūmaḥ  na agni gamayet  vāstavyām rūpa saṃpattau kim amena kālpanika doṣeṇa iti ced  tarhi vāsta vya āmasaṃpattau kim kā alpa nikyā tayā iti samānam virodha avirodhau viśeṣa iti ced  kuta etad  ubhayoḥ ekatra vastu avastu tvāt anyatra avastuvat iti ced  tad  kim kālpanikaḥ  api dhūmaḥ  vastu bhūtaḥ  yena kūrma romṇaḥ tena saha virodhaḥ syāt  kvacid  vastu bhūta  iti ced  nirdhūma tvam api kvacid  vastu bhūtam iti tena api virodha eva tasmāt  yathā kālpanikī vipattiḥ na doṣāya tathā kālpanikī saṃpattiḥ api na guṇāya iti tasyāḥ ca sarvatra sulabha tvāt iti ṭīkā arthaḥ etad ca abhyupetya uktam vastutas tu na na nirūpa ākhyam kasyacid  vyavahārasya bhājanam iti nanu yadi āvayoḥ akuśala tayā sva vacana virodhaḥ atha praṣṭuḥ kim uttaram vaktavyam iti avaśiṣṭam upasaṃharan pariharati tasmāt iti yatra vacane sarvathā eva virodha sa tatra āvacanam eva śreya iti arthaḥ etena mūka tā hetu vikalpāḥ parihṛtā boddhavyā iti nanu eka rūpam avikalam idam katham gamakam gamaka tve vā vyatireka vikalavat  rūpa antara vikalam api tathā kim na syāt aviśeṣa ādityāśaḍkyāha na ca etāvatā iti rūpa antara vaikalyavat na vyatireka vaikalyam avinā abhā  kṣatim āvahati iti arthaḥ evam tarhi sati api vipakṣe vyatirekaḥ  na paryeṣaṇīya iti ata āha vipakṣa sambhave tu iti vipakṣe sati tatra vṛttiśaḍkā tatas tad nivṛtti artham tad upayogaḥ vipakṣa abhāve tu śaḍkā eva na asti yathā uktam prāk  na hi tāya abhyavaharaṇe api asamarthasya mumūrṣoḥ śaṣkulī bhakṣaṇam śaṅkate cetana iti arthaḥ sva mate tu iti asya tu kālpanikaḥ  api vipakṣaḥ pareṇa abhidhātum na śakyate abhidhāne sa pakṣatva āpatteḥ asapakṣa tve anabhidhāna prasaḍgāt  tatas ca abhidheya tve sādhye yaḥ kaścid heturūpa ādīyate tasya kim vipakṣe vṛttiḥ avṛttiḥ vā iti praśne anena uttara kovidena kim vaktavyam mūkībhūya tiṣṭhāsoḥ tu na kaścid  pratimalla iti svayam eva ullapitam anena na tu evaṃbhūtaḥ  ahetuḥ eva doṣa abhāvāt arūci mātrasya sarvatra sulabha tvāt iti bhāga asiddhi nirākāraṇāya vyāptyā iti vadataḥ pūrvavat iti atiśāyane matupaḥ  vidhānam atiśayaḥ ca vyāptiḥ eva iti āśayaḥ tad idam uktam ṭīkā kṛtā asti gandhavatu asya sādhyam na tu vyāptyā iti nanu sādhyasajātīye śeṣa śabdasya na kācid  vṛttiḥ iti ata āha sādhyasya upayukta tvāt iti pauna rūkti abhramam apākaroti padāni vibhajya iti na mantar bhāvya vyākhyāne sāmānyatodṛṣṭa padam evam yojanīyam ukta viśeṣa rahita tvena vipakṣa eva sāmānya iti ucyate tatra adṛṣṭam saptamyāḥ tasiḥ yogya darśana nivṛttyā ca dṛśya nivṛttiḥ vivakṣitā tena vipakṣe asat iti arthaḥ atas  siddhavat  trirūpa saṃpattim abhyupetya rūpa dvaya saṃpade cakāram avatārayati tathā ca iti tad evam tad pūrvakam iti anena liṅga parām arśaḥ  anumānam iti lakṣaṇa arthe vyākhyāte atha kim liṅkam katividham vā iti jijñāsāyām trividham iti avacchedena vyākhyāya kim lakṣaṇam iti jijñāsāyām pūrvavat ityādi eka vākya tayā vyākhyānena parāmarśa viṣayaḥ saṃjñitaḥ  vibhaktaḥ  lakṣitaḥ ca viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ abheda vivakṣayā ca sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti mantavyam evam anyāni api iti tad yathā manojña mattakāśinī saṃdarśanena saṃsāri rāga anumānam śatru darśanena krodha anumānam viṣaya bhogena sukha anumānam roga ādinā duḥkha anumānam avikala indriyasya yogya viṣaya avadhānena jñāna anumānam śraddhāvatām yathāvidhi yāga ādi anuṣṭhānena dharma anumānam niṣiddha ācaraṇena adharma anumānam paṭu abhyāsa ādara pratyayaiḥ saṃskāra anumānam mithyā pratyayena bhaviṣyat saṃsāra pravāha anumānam iti adhyātmam bāhye ca jvalantam tṛṇa rāśim upalabhya bhaviṣyat bhasma anumānam tathāvidha vṛṣṭyā bhaviṣyat nadīpūra ādi jñānam prakāra antara avagatena vāyunā tvarāvatā vṛkṣa ādi saṃkṣobha anumānam ityādi na iyam duravabodham iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭa svarūpasya eva avivecanāt iti arthaḥ udāharaṇa dvāreṇa tad vivecanam bhaviṣyati iti āha śeṣavat udāharaṇān atargatam ca iti śeṣavat lakṣaṇa yoge api tad udāharaṇa antara vailakṣaṇyena idam eva sāmānyatodṛṣṭa padārthe bhaviṣyati iti ata āhā na ca etāvatā iti na tāvat aśva karṇa ādi śabdavat ayam sūrya vrajyā anumāne vartate anyatra api vṛddha prayogāt  na api sūtrakārasya eva paribhāṣeyam niṣprayojana tvāt  tasmāt udāharaṇa vailakṣaṇya mātra vivakṣayā it amucyate tathā ca atiprasaṅga iti arthaḥ tasmāt  bhāṣya kāra vyākhyāna viruddha udāharaṇa mātra ākhyān am arocayamānaḥ sāmānyatodṛṣṭa padam vyākhyāyāni athā udāharaṇam āha iti yojanā kṣaya vṛddhi pratyaya aviṣaya tve sati iti spaṣṭa artham prāḍmukha upalabhya tve parivṛttya tad pratyaya viṣaya tvāt iti paryālocanayā eva avināśasya prāpta tvāt  na hi upalabdha vināśe upalabdham pratyabhijñāyate bhrāntau  api anupalabdham eva upalabdha tayā iti prāḍmukha upalabhya tve ca iti asya ṭīkayā sphoritasya prāḍmukha upalabdhasya prāḍmukhena anupalambhe sati iti arthaḥ nara antarasya tad samāna deśa sthasya iti mantavyam anyathā mārtaṇḍa maṇḍalasya api loka antara varti puruṣa apekṣayā prāḍmukha upalabhyatā durvāra iti asiddham viśeṣaṇam syāt  tad etad narapadena sūcitam tad abhimukha deśa saṃbandhāt iti śiṣya hita tayā vyabhicāra aupayika pāda viharaṇa jñāpanāya na hi yathā tathā pāda vihāraṇa mātram asya hetoḥ kṣatim āvahati iti satya vināśe iti ca draṣṭavyam sati draṣṭavyatva iti vā iti śeṣaḥ iha yadi api diśaḥ pratyakṣa tve sādhye aḍgulyā nirdeśaḥ  vyadhikaraṇaḥ tarū nagara ādiṣu eva aḍgulyā vyapadeśāt  diśaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam tvaḍgulī vyapadeśasya na tad adhikaraṇa tā sādhanam anyathā siddha tvāt tathā api yasyām diśi ete taravaḥ sā prācī iti tarva ādi bhedena api aḍgulyā vyapadeśaḥ  asti iti na vyadhikaraṇa tvam āhatya abhidhātum śakyata iti anena abhiprāyeṇa anyathā siddhim eva vārtika artham āha anyathā asiddhatayā iti upalakṣaṇam ca etad  calantīm patākām upalabhya ayam vāyuḥ vātī iti aḍa gulī nirdeśasya ācākṣuṣe vāyau  api gata tvena vyabhicārasya api saṃbhavāt  rūpeṇa sparśa anumānam iti ādau  ādi grahaṇena rasena rūpa anumānam gandhena rasa anumānam ityādi vṛkṣa adarśane sandehe vā na śiśapā darśana niścayaḥ  vā tatas  anavasara parāhatam eva anumānam vṛkṣa śabda prayoga lakṣaṇa vyavahāra anumānam tu na sva artham avidita samayena aśakya tvāt   vidita samayasya ca vyartha tvāt  paraḥ  api yadi vyutpannaḥ  yadi vidita śabda pravṛtti nimittaḥ tadā svayam eva vyavaharet  viparītaḥ tu śiśapā tvam api na pratīyāt  avyutpannaḥ ced  samayam agrāhayitvā vyavahārayitum aśakya eva na ca ayam samaya graha prakāraḥ tathā sati śiśapā tu ādayam vṛkṣaḥ  vyavahartavyaḥ iti śiśapā tvam eva vṛkṣa śabda pravṛtti nimittam ākalayet  na ca śiśapā tu ādayam vṛkṣa śabda pravṛtti nimittavān iti vākya arthaḥ vidita tad nimittam prati vyartha tvāt    viparītam pratyapraddhi viśeṣaṇatva prasaḍgāt sāmānya upakrame samaya graha anupapatteḥ   puruṣa icchā mātra adhīna tvācaca samayasya pakṣa dharma tayā niyantum aśakyatvāt    avidita samayam prati ca anvaya upakramasya ayukta tvāt ityata āha śrutena iti tad anena ye ca anye sādhya samāna kālāḥ te sarve sāmānyatodṛṣṭa anumāna saṃgrāhya tvena upalakṣitā iti sva matena vyākhyāna antaram na tu tātparya antaram iti arthaḥ pūrvam sādhyam tad yasya vyāptyā iti anena eka tātparyatvāt anena eva abhiprāyeṇa āha atra api yathāsaṃbhavam iti na anantarbhāva cakāra nirapekṣate ca asmin vyākhyāne pūrvasmāt  viśeṣaḥ sāmānyena kāryam vā kāraṇam vā anubhaya ātmakam vā avinā bhāvitayā dṛṣṭam niścitam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam eva ca yojanā tad idam uktam asandigdha tāmāha iti tatra tad pūrvakam iti sva rūpa vipratipatti nivṛttiḥ sva lakṣaṇa sāmarthyena nyūna adhika saṃkhyatva aśaḍkā nivṛttiḥ prathamam tātparyam niyama jñāpane tu aśakya lakṣaṇatva śaḍkā nivṛttiḥ tāt paryam iti na pauna rūktyam iti vṛttavartiṣyamāṇa anukīrtana phalam yadi api pratipannam pratyanumānasya na saṃśaya viparyaya nivṛttiḥ ajñāta jñānam vā upayogaḥ tathā api adhyavasita abhyanujñānam vastu bala āyātam apekṣite viṣaye anupekṣaṇīyam eva iti tasya api anumāna pratipādyeṣu gaṇanā tena ādi vākye pratipannaḥ pratipādayitā iti pratipanna eva pratipādayitā na tu pratipannaḥ pratipādayitā eva iti boddhavyam punar  paunarūkti aparihāra artham vṛttavartiṣyamāṇe anukīrtayati pūrvam siddhavat iti sākṣātkṛtya numityoḥ kriyayoḥ tulya tā viṣaya gatā draṣṭavyā tena ayam arthaḥ vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa yogyaḥ  dharmaḥ  yatra anumīyate tad  pūrvavat anumānam tad ayogyaḥ tu yatra tad  sāmānyatodṛṣṭam iti dhūma tvā eka artha samavāyibhiḥ iti satātparyam viśeṣaṇam na hi saṃtatam ūrdhva gamana mātreṇa agniḥ anumātum śakyate dhūlī paṭala ādau vyabhicārāt  eka dravyatva āt iti asya sa pakṣe rūpa ādau  anvayasya spaṣṭa tvāt  vipakṣa vyatireka eva uktaḥ dvividham eva hi iti na tu atra anvaya abhidhāna mātreṇa kevala vyatireki śaḍkā kartavyā samāna jātīya ārambhaka tvam śabdasya asiddham atas  sādhayati kārya tvāt iti kāryatvam punar asya anupalabdhi kāraṇa bhāve sati anupalabdhasya upalabhyamāna tvāt  vā pratyakṣāt  vā iti sarvatra upalabdhi prasaḍga ādityasya viparyayeṇa hetuḥ prayogaḥ tu evam avyāpya vṛttiḥ śabdaḥ āśraya aprāptau  api kvacid anupalabhyamāna tve sati kvacid upalabhyamāna tvāt  saṃyogavat iti yadi api ca etāvat mātreṇa guṇa tvam sidhyati tathā api bhāṣya kārīyaḥ  hetu rūpekṣitaḥ syāt iti atas avyāpaka tā mātram prasādhya eva prakṛte lagayati karṇa iti atra api prayogaḥ śabdaḥ  vīcī taraṅga nyāyena karṇa śaṣkulīm antam ākāśa deśam āsādayati prakāra antara asaṃbhave sati upalabhyamāna tvāt iti vyatirekī udāharaṇa artham vivecayati idam tu iti sat ādi abhedaḥ sattā yogaḥ anitya tvam kāraṇavat tvam sāmānya viśeṣavat tvam iti sādhya dharmiṇī asmad ādibhiḥ kadācid  pratyakṣeṇa anupalambhāt iti arthaḥ ābhiprāyikaḥ  hi arthaḥ pakṣa dharma tāyā viṣayaḥ sa eva abhiprāyeṇa vyāpyate yena vinā pratijñātor athaḥ na upapadyate ubhayathā saṃbhāvanāya akekataratra bādhaka upapattau  anyataraḥ pramāṇa antara gocaraḥ tatra vidhāyaka pramāṇa abhāve kevala vyatirekiṇaḥ  avatāraḥ tathā hi kṣiti ādikam sa kartṛkam kāryatvāt iti atra sarvajña tvam antareṇa kṣiti ādīnām kartṛ tvam eva na upapadyate paramāṇu adṛṣṭa ādīnām ajñāne tad adhiṣṭhāna anupapatteḥ tad adhiṣṭhāne vā asarvajñatva anupapatteḥ tasmāt  sarvajña tvam antareṇa pratijñāta artha anupapattau tad abhiprāya vyāptam ābhiprāyika tvāt ca pakṣa dharma tā gocaraḥ icchā ādayaḥ paratantrā guṇa tvāt iti atra punar ātmā na abhi prāya vyāptaḥ na hi icchā ādīnām kṣiti ādi pāratantryam asaṃbhāvit api tu mānasa pratyakṣa vedyatva ādi bhaḥ bādhitam dhūma gata nīla tvena iva dhūmasya apālāla tvam tasmāt ubhayathā api saṃbhavāt ātmā na eva abhiprāya vyāptaḥ tad avyāpta tvāt ca na pakṣa dharma tā tam aṅkam āropayitum arhati api tu icchā saṃbaddha para mātram ādāya eva nivartate etad uttara kālam kṣiti ādau bādhite tad anya asiddhau vidhāyaka pramāṇa abhāvāt niṣedha mukhena vyatirekī pravartate tam imam viśeṣam hṛdi nidhāya uktam bādhakaiḥ apanīte dravya aṣṭaka guṇatva iti nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt  yad rūpam siddham na tad  kevala vyatirekiṇā sādhyam yādṛśam ca tena sādhyam tādṛśam na kvacid  siddham tathā ca aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ pakṣaḥ na ca tathābhūte sandehaḥ  api kāraṇa abhāvāt samāna asamāna dharma vipratipattīnām anupalabdha cara aviṣaya tvāt ityata āha yadi api ca ayam iti sva rūpeṇa asādhāraṇa rūpeṇa iti arthaḥ na hi vākya artha sayā pūrva tayā padārthānām viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ  vihanyate tathā sati anvayinopi anutthānam iti pralīnam anumānena na ca dravya aṣṭaka atirikta ādi padārthā eva apūrve yena aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tā syāt  pakṣasya na ca evam sati śaśa śṛṅga dhanuḥ dhara ādau  api prasaṅgaḥ tatra api tadā artha mātrā prasiddheḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt iti vācyam sāmānyatodṛṣṭa pūrvakatva niyama sīmāyāḥ durlaḍghya tvāt  anyathā sāmānyatas  api asiddhaḥ katham niṣpramāṇaka śabda sāmarthya mātram āśritya parāmṛśyeta aparāmṛṣṭaḥ ca katham pramāṇa vyavahāram avatārayet  tad idam uktam adūra viprakarṣeṇa parāmṛṣṭa iti viśeṣa siddheḥ sāmānya sidbhiḥ adūra viprakarṣaḥ tad asiddhiḥ tu tad viparyaya iti arthaḥ evam ca saṃśayaḥ  api atra vādi vipratipatteḥ eva sugamaḥ icchā ādīnām ubhaya vādi siddhe sāmānyatas  adhikaraṇe dravya aṣṭaka atiriktā n atiḥ eka koṭyā ūrūbhābhyām samutthāpanāt  athavā pratyeka utthitaḥ saṃśayaḥ samudāye viśrāmyati iti nyāyaḥ tathā hi guṇa tvam pṛthivī āśrite gandha ādau tad atirikta āśrite sneha ādau ca dṛṣṭam icchā ādiṣu ca dṛśyate tad  kim icchā ādayaḥ pṛthivī āśritā uta tad atirikta āśritā iti anena ākāreṇa sarva dravyeṣu bhavan sandehaḥ samāna dharma darśanāt eva dravya aṣṭaka tad atirikta koṭyoḥ eva paryavasitaḥ  bhavati tad idam uktam dharmiṇi ca ityādi vibhāga vacanāt eva ityādi bhāṣya vakra vyākhyāyāḥ śaḍkā poṣaṇe tātparyam nanu sadasatī tattvam iti atra sat asat śabdābhyām bhāva abhāvau  uktau tad iha vartamāna āvartamāna arthatva vyākhyānam tad viruddham api kuta upādīya iti ata āha pratyakṣam hi iti atha tathā eva kim na syāt iti ata āha yadi api iti na viśeṣaṇtvam svātantryeṇa svātantrya abhidhānena iti arthaḥ āhaḥ nyāya upyasti iti asya akṣara arthena naḥ saṃbandha anupapatteḥ tātparya arthena saṃbandham āha na sandeha iti nyāya abhāvena hi tarkasya niścaya aparyāptau sandehaḥ tad avastha iti āśaḍkitam atas tad niṣedha eva uttaram yuktam iti asti eva nyāyaḥ sandeha virodhi niścaya samarthaḥ  yata iti śeṣaḥ nimitta tvam yadi viṣaya tvam tad na ātmani dṛṣṭānte atha upādāna tvam na tad sādhye samavāya iti ata āha nimitta tvam kāraṇa tvam iti nanu vyāpaka tvam parama mahat parimāṇa yogaḥ sarva saṃyogi samāna deśa tā vā tad ubhayam api samavāye na saṃbhavati iti ata āha sati upalabdhī iti upalabhyata iti ucyamāne ghaṭa ādeḥ api vyāpakatva prasaṅgaḥ ata uktam sarvatra iti deśasya avacchedaka tā mātreṇa saptamyā nirdeśaḥ  vane sihanāda itivat  tathā api asiddham lakṣaṇam na hi ātma ādayaḥ sarvatra upalabhyante iti ata uktam sati upalabdhi kāraṇa iti tathā api viṣayasya api upalabdhi kāraṇa tvāt  yatra yatra ghaṭa ādi paramāṇu antāḥ sva upalabdhi sāmagrī sahitāḥ tatra tatra upalabhyanta eva iti taiḥ eva vyabhicāra iti ata uktam antarā iti etad ca dravya rūpa kāraṇa antara abhiprāyeṇa draṣṭavyam anyathā yatra ghaṭa ādayaḥ  na santi tatra tatas  anyasya tad upalabdhi kāraṇasya tad indriya saṃyogasya abhāvāt eva teṣām anupalambhaḥ tad sadbhāve tu sarvatra upalambha eva iti etad api āśaḍkyeta tathā api paramāṇu ādi guṇaiḥ eva yāvat dravya bhāvibhiḥ āśraya adhīna nirūpaṇaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ tad nivṛtti artham aneka saṃbandhi tve sati iti draṣṭavyam etad ca sarvatra iti anena ṭīkā kṛtā sūcitam yadi api ca sarvatra astitvam vyāpaka tvam tathā api lakṣaṇam antareṇa tad  duravabodham iti tad eva uktam iti nyāya iti kartavya tā bhūtam tarkam pṛcchati kartrā avyāpāryamāṇasya karaṇasya svayam vyāpāra ayogāt itya āśayavān iti bhāvaḥ atha uktam anavasthāna prasaṅgam avatārayitum kim iti anādhāratva prasaṅga ucyate yāvatā svatantra eva ayam prasaṅgaḥ kim na syāt  na hi kāryasya anādhāra tvam asya iṣṭam eva ityata āha syāt etad iti paścāt  turyā saṃyukta iti śeṣaḥ na hi utpannaḥ api asaṃyukta eva turyā prathama īkṣaṇe paṭa iti kasyacid niścayaḥ atha ca pramāṇa balāt iṣṭa eva ayam arthaḥ tathā utpanne api prathame kṣaṇe tantuṣu asam aveta eva iṣyata iti pādau prasārya tiṣṭhataḥ  na idam uttaram iti arthaḥ tasmāt anavasthā prasaḍga avatāraṇāya eva idam uktam iti āha samavāyaḥ ca iti iti yadi api upādhi kathanena eva vṛttimat tvasya prāpti dharma tvam nirākṛtam tathā api prāpti tvasya anaikāntikatva sūcanāya punar api anavasthā prasaṅgam avatārayati atha iti anavasthā abhiyā avaśyam antatas  kācid  prāptiḥ ca na ca vṛttimatī iti svīkartavyam tatas ca tathā eva prāptimat tvam anaikāntikam iti arthaḥ atha anavasthā svīkāre kaḥ  doṣa iti āśaḍkya nirākaroti nanu iyam iti anāditāyām hi aḍkurotpāda anuguṇa samaya saṃbhavinā bījena janite aḍkureṇa janite bīje vartamānam bīja tvam tasyāḍkura pūrvaka tām avagamayati iti yujyate avikalasya hetoḥ pramāṇasya vidyamāna tvāt  idaṃprathama tāyām tu kārya utpāda anuguṇa samaye bhaviṣyat pravāhasya asattvāt prathamasya anutpāde tad āśrayasya hetoḥ tasmin  asati āśraya asiddha tayā sarvasya āgamaka tve pramāṇa abhāva iti arthaḥ abhyupeta kaṇāt āpta tvasya śāstra virodhaḥ ca ityādi kāryam akṛtaka saṃbandhavat iti pratijñāyām ghaṭa ādeḥ bhū tala ādinā api akṛtaka eva saṃbandhaḥ syāt  sa ca aniṣṭa iti pratijñām viśinaṣṭi sva upādānena iti sva samavāyinā iti arthaḥ kāryam iti ca samaveta mātra upalakṣaṇa param anyathā jāti ādiṣu vipakṣeṣu saṃbhave hetoḥ virodhaḥ syāt  athavā pratijñā yathā aśrutā eva ādhāravattva āditi atra ādhāra śabdena na āśraya mātram vivakṣitam kim tu adhikaraṇam kārakam tena adhikaraṇa kārakavat tvāt  iti arthaḥ na ca vācyam kārakavattva mātreṇa eva paryāptau kim adhikaraṇa grahaṇena iti pradhvaṃsena virodha prasaḍgāt  na kāryasya kāryaḥ saṃbandha iti arthaḥ mithas  saṃbadhyete ādhārya ādhāra bhāvena avatiṣṭhete iti arthaḥ saḥ  api samavāye na asti samavāya antara abhāvāt iti arthaḥ san  api asau na kāryam ādhāravat  karoti sva samavāyena eva tasya ādhāravat tvāt tad abhāve tu eka artha samavāyaḥ  api na syāt iti arthaḥ saha utpāde kāryam anādhāram syāt  sarvadā iti śeṣaḥ samavāyi kāraṇa abhāve asamavāyi kāraṇa śaḍkā api na asti tad pratyāsanna svabhāva tvāt tasya iti abhiprāyavatā tad upekṣya nimitta mātrāt utpattiḥ āśaḍkya nirākṛtā nanu vidhīyamāna niṣidhyamāna vyatirekeṇa jagati na svatantraḥ  nāma tad  katham dharma traividhyam iti ata āha atra ca iti vidhīyamānaḥ  vartamāna iti arthaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ avartamāna iti arthaḥ tatra ye vartamānāḥ teṣām kaścid  paratantraḥ  vṛttimān iti arthaḥ kaścid  svatantraḥ  vṛtti rahita iti arthaḥ pratiṣidhyamānāḥ tu paratantrā na santi asattvāt eva iti tad evam vidhīyamānaḥ svatantraḥ  vidhīyamānaḥ paratantraḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ svatantraḥ ca iti tisraḥ  vidhā iti arthaḥ tad evam avartamānaḥ  gharmaḥ pratiṣidhyamāna tayā eva vyavahriyate na ca asau pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ kim tu anumāna viṣaya iti darśitam tad ca anupapannam iti śaḍkā vārttika artham āha nanu iti asan  iti uddeśyam tena ayam arthaḥ asanna vartamānaḥ  na kevalam pratiṣedha vyavahāra viṣayaḥ kim tu vidhīyamānaḥ  api vidhi vyavahāra viṣayaḥ  api evam asau na kevalam anumāna viṣayaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ca kvacid  pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ ca iti arthaḥ kketyata āha yathā iti katham asau vidhīyamāna iti ata āha jāyamāna iti katham asau pratyakṣa viṣaya iti ata āha visphārita iti katham asau  avartamāna iti ata āha na ca asau  iti asat tayā sat tayā vā anabhyupagamāt iti sattāyā jāyamāna tayā virodhāt  asat tayā vidhiviṣayatayā iti bhāvaḥ katham na abhyupagamyate na hi sattā sattābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ  asti iti ata āha niṣedha viṣaya tayā tu iti vidhīyam āna tā pakṣe hi jāyamāna tā abhyupagame ubhayathā api virodhaḥ  na tu pratiṣidhyamāna tā pakṣe api iti arthaḥ tasmāt  jāyamāne ghaṭe na vidhāyaka pratyakṣa pravṛttiḥ virodhāt  niṣedhakam tam pratyakṣam pravartamānam api tad niṣedham eva gocarayet  na tu niṣedhyam ghaṭam tatas  siddhaḥ  viṣaya bheda iti sāram upapādanīya iti satkārya vādam apanīya apare tu iti artha atireka mātram artha padātireka mātram evam uttaratra api nanu kena etad uktam yad u bhaya pada vyabhicāra eva viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ  bhavati iti ata āha viśeṣaṇam iti nanu tathā api ubhayoḥ api pṛthivī dravya śabdayā ūru ubhaya vāci tvāt  katham viśeṣa pratipattiḥ iti ata āha na ca iti na hi bhavati pṛthivī tvam dravya tvam iti upalakṣaṇam pṛthivī tvam dravyam dravya tvam ca pṛthivī iti api na bhavati iti api draṣṭavyam na ca na antarīyaka artha śabdayoḥ api iyam eva gatiḥ astu iti vācyam aniyama prasaḍgāt  na antarīyakatva arthayoḥ api sāmānādhikaraṇyāt artha tvanā antarīkayoḥ api iti tatas tad vyavaccheda artham punar api prayatna antaram āstheyam tasmāt aneka artha tve api viśeṣa para eva ayam na antarīyaka śabda iti akāmena api abhyupeyam tathā ca pūrva dūṣaṇā nivṛttiḥ iti nanu aniyata prasareṇa asati na asti iti sahitena iṣṭalābhaḥ  yadi api tathā api sarvathā sa pakṣa āvṛtti rasādhāraṇaḥ  api nivartayitavyaḥ na hi pakṣa vyāpakaḥ  vipakṣe ca na asti eva etāvatā eva tasya nirākaraṇam tasya api evaṃbhūta tvāt tasmāt  tad tulye sadbhāva iti kartavyam eva iti āśaḍkyāha prasaktam apratiṣiddham anumatam eva iti prasaktasya pratiṣedhāt upādāne tad viparītasya hānam artha āyātam iti arthaḥ na ca asaṃbhavaḥ  api prasaktaḥ  yena aniṣedhāt  tasya api upādāne tad viparīta hānam saṃbhāvyeta prathame pade saṃbhavasya vidheya tvena iva asaṃbhavasya niṣedhya tvena anupādānāt iti samuccīyamāna ityādi vaicitryeṇa hi nipāta saṃbandhe vākya bheda prasaṅgaḥ atha eka vākya tvam icchan  avaicitryeṇa eva nipāta saṃbandham icchet iti arthaḥ etad eva anūdyamāna samuccayam āśaḍkyamānaḥ sphuṭayati na ca iti uditam hi anūdyate na tu anuditam na ca ubhayatva viśiṣṭam havirūditam kim tu haviḥ mātram tathā ca anuvāda pakṣe ubhaya tvam avivakṣitam ubhayatva vivakṣāyām tu na ayam anuvādaḥ kim tu vāda eva tathā ca vākya bhedaḥ evam dārṣṭa antike api yadi sādhya ayoga vyaccheda viśiṣṭaḥ  hetuḥ ūditaḥ yuktam idānīm yad tathā asauvanūdyate na tu etad asti hetu mātram tu aviśiṣṭam uddiṣṭam viśiṣṭasya tu tasya ayam eva prathamaḥ  vāda avatāraḥ tad yadi yasya iti ayam anuvādaḥ  nūnam anumeye sadbhāva eva iti avivakṣitam viśeṣaṇam vivakṣite tasmin  anena eva vākyena viśiṣṭaḥ  vādaḥ kartavyaḥ paścāt idam eva āvṛttyā anuvāda iti vākya bheda iti arthaḥ saḥ  ayam prayatna āntarīya sthāna śabdasya arthaḥ nanu yadi anu udyamānam aśakyam viśeṣṭum atha ārtiḥ api katham haviṣā viśeṣyata iti ata āha atra hi yadi api iti ananya gatika tvāt  prāptena haviṣā viśeṣaṇam ārteḥ ubhayatvasya tu na pūrva prāpta tvam na api tad antareṇa ārtiḥ aśakya pratipattiḥ sādhya ayomavyavacchedaḥ api hetoḥ īdṛśa iti arthaḥ yadi evam ubhaya vacanam kimartham iti ata āha pratīyamānam api ubhaya tvam avivakṣitam viśeṣaṇatayā iti śeṣaḥ ayam vākya arthaḥ ārti viśeṣaṇa tayā haviḥ tāvat upādātavyam tasya ca ājya puroḍāśa ādi aneka rūpa tvāt ubhaya tvam api asti iti prāyika tayā tad api upāttam tena idam siddham bhavati ekam anekam vā haviḥ yasya ārtim ārcchet ityādi ubhayatva vivakṣā pakṣe tu na eka eka haviḥ ārtau prāyaścitta vidhiḥ syāt iti doṣaḥ na ca evam astu iti vācyam vākya bheda prasaṅgasya tādavasthyāt iti na ca anumeye sadbhāva eva tad tulya eva sadbhāva iti vākya dvayam eva idam ubhaya vidhāyakam astu kaḥ  doṣa iti vācyam tri rūpa saṃpannasya hetu rūpasya ekasya arthasya alābha prasaḍgāt vākya bhede hi avaśyam artha bheda iti nyāyāt  śaṅkate atha iti avāntara vākya bhede api mahā vākyasya eka tvāt  vivakṣita eka artha pratilambha iti śaḍka arthaḥ atra naiyāyika samādhānam āśaḍkya bauddhaḥ sva bhāṣayā nirākaroti na ca iti yadi api tad tulya eva iti anya yoga vyavacchedasya vipakṣa mātra viṣaya tvam tadā syāt  yadi viṣaya antara saṃkocaḥ syāt  sa ca tad ekavākyatayā iti paraspara āśraya doṣaḥ anyathā ubhayoḥ api tad tulya anyatva aviśeṣe vipakṣa yogasya vyavacchedaḥ  na tu anumeya yogasya iti kutas  vihita tvāt  tasya iti ced  ata eva virodhāt eka vākyatva asaṅgatiḥ iti ucyate yasmāt  tad eka vākya tāyām eva satyām vipakṣa mātra viṣaya tvam asya vaktum śakyate sā api tasmin sati eva iti duru uttara doṣa āpattiḥ tathā api bauddhanaye śābddham vyavahāram āśritya samuccaya eva na nirvahet  kṛtam anayā virodhe sūkṣma īkṣikayā ityāśa yavān āha anya apoha iti saḥ  ayam sādhāraṇaḥ  api nyāyaḥ  aprastutatva bhiyā viśeṣa niṣṭhatayā avatārita iti yathoddeśam ca lakṣaṇāt iti bhāva padam lakṣaṇam āha iti anayoḥ madhye itiḥ pūraṇīyaḥ atra api iti apiśabdaḥ pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa upakṣayā nanu sādhyate anena iti sādhanam iti eva astu saṃbhavati ca ayam arthaḥ  jñānasya karaṇa tāyām tasya prasiddha sādharmya samuttha tvāt ityata āha tad etad iti na sāmānya atiriktam sādṛśyam anāśritasya anya āśraya tve dravyatva prasaḍgāt ananya āśritasya api ayuta siddha ubhaya vyaḍgya tve samavāyatva prasaḍgāt gogavaya ādi yuta siddha niṣṭhā abhivyakti anupapatteḥ ca yuta siddha abhivyaḍgya tve abhāvatva prasaḍgāt ayutasiddha avayavi avayava ādi niṣṭhā abhivyakti anupapatteḥ ca nityasya aneka āśraya tve jātitva prasaḍgāt eka āśraya tve tasya nāśe anāśrayasya avasthāna anupapatteḥ nitya tve pramāṇa abhāva prasaḍgāt ca sāmānyam hi eka āśraya nāśe api āśraya antare tādrūpyeṇa eva pratyabhijñānāt  nityam iti vyavasthāpyate idam tu na tathā iti katham nityam iti jñātavyam pratyuta anitya eka āśraya tvāt eva anitya tvam eva anumīyate nitya eka vṛtti tve tu sva rūpa sataḥ viśeṣatva prasaṃgāt  sattāsataḥ  guṇatva āpatteḥ anityeṣu ca sadṛśa vyavahāra hāna prasaḍgāt anityasya tu aneka āśraya tve guṇavataḥ  dravyatva prasaḍgāt   nirguṇa tve guṇatva prasaḍgāt eka āśraya tve saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ anapekṣa kāraṇasya karmatva prasaḍgāt tad viparītasya tu guṇatva prasaḍgāt guṇeṣu ca karmasu ca sādṛśya vyavahāraḥ  na syāt  teṣām samavāyi kāraṇatva abhāvena anitya dharma ayogāt  āśraya sādṛśyena tad vyavahāra upapattau visadṛśa āśrayāṇām guṇa karmaṇām tad vyavahāra anupapatteḥ kāraṇa traya vicāra anupapatteḥ ca iti arthaḥ sādharmya prasiddhiḥ api draṣṭavyā iti sūtre sā ca karma dhāraya samāśrayeṇa iti āpta vākyāt iti vākyāt ārabhyam pratyakṣa paryantena iti hṛdayam prajñāpanīyasya gavaya śabda vācyatayā iti vadatā atideśa vākyasya akṛta samaya saṃjñā samabhivyāhāraḥ  darśitaḥ tathā api karaṇa vyutpattyā sādhana pada vyākhyānasya parityāge na kācid upapattiḥ darśitā prajñāpanapadasya api karaṇa vyutpatti saṃbhavādata āha piṇḍasya hi iti pratyakṣāt  sādṛśyāt  prajānan tena prajñāpyata iti vadan sādṛśyasya eva prajñāyamānasya kāraṇa tvam abhipraiti tathā ca tena saha sādhya sādhana padasya vyadhikaraṇa tvāt anyasya ca karaṇasya abhāvāt  sādhya sādhana padam anarthakam āpadyeta yadi bhāva sādhanam na syāt  na ca tad jñānam eva astu karaṇam iti vācyam avāntara vyāpāra virahiṇaḥ karaṇatva ayogāt asamī cīne api sādṛśya jñāne tathā abhāva prasaḍgāt ca tad api hi sādṛśya jñānam eva pramāṇa anuvṛttyā tad nivṛttiḥ iti api na vācyam vṛttaiḥ eva padaiḥ samīhita siddhau  anuvṛtteḥ anavakāśāt sā api hi grantha vaicitryam āpādayantī pada antara vṛttiḥ eva tathā api prajñānam prasiddhi padārtha ūna tu prajñāpanam iti ata āha iti etad arthe pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ  avyavadhānena phala uparaktā prātisvikī kriyā jñāyamānasya sādṛśyasya karaṇa tvam āviṣkartum tasya anyatra acarita arthaḥ phala anuguṇa u vyāpāraḥ  darśita iti tātparyār athaḥ tatra iti tātparya artha akṣara arthayoḥ lakṣya padam hi lakṣaṇa vyavasthāpakam na bhavati paraspara āśraya tvam agatiḥ vā iti doṣāt  nanu upasthāpakam api iti āśa yavān āśaḍkya dvitīya pada upādāna tātparyam āha yadi api iti nanu evam sati prathamā eva astu na ca iyam aśoka vanikā tasyāḥ prathama tvāt eva prathamam buddhau  upanipātāt  na sādhya sādhana padena phala vācinā sāmānādhikaraṇya anupapatteḥ astu tarhi tad api karaṇa sādhanam evam yata iti adhyāhāra kaṣṭa sṛṣṭiḥ api na syāt  satyam eva etad  kintu phala abhāvena eva hetunā upamānasya prāmāṇyam apanīyate pareṇa tasmāt  tad avabodhāya niṣkṛṣya phalam asya darśanīyam iti tathā eva sūcitavān etad ca agre sphuṭam iti na iha ṭīkā kṛtā darśitam bhāṣya vārttikayoḥ virodham āśaḍkya āha vārtikakāreṇa iti tṛtīyā samāsa iti upalakṣaṇam artha siddhaḥ karmadhāraya samāsaḥ  api na nirasta iti draṣṭavyam aviruddha tvāt  prasiddham sādharmyam yasya iti bahu vrīhau  api karma dhāraya arthasya praviṣṭa tvāt  evam prasiddhena sādharmyam iti atra tṛtīyā tatpuruṣasya praveśāt  virodha antaram āśaḍkya āha bhāṣya kāreṇa hi iti na ayam arthaḥ  bhāṣya akṣarebhyaḥ śrūyata iti ata āha ākṣipra iti praścāt niṣkṛṣya abhidhānam kṛtam samaya pratipatteḥ phalasya tad āha samākhyā iti tathā api kim āyātam vārttika vi rodhasya ityata āha etad eva iti pratipadyatām ayam ityādi śaḍka uttara artha sūtra uktam karoti prasiddha sādharmyāt iti atra iti atra upamānasya phale vipratipadyamānān prati sa aśaḍkam jarat naiyāyikajayanta prabhṛtīnām parihāram āha yadi api iti saṃjñā karma saṃjñā karaṇam māna antaram śabdaḥ  vā śabda arthaḥ  vā liṅga bhūtaḥ tatra liṅga pakṣe upalakṣitaḥ pratipāditaḥ śabdāt avagatena gaḥ sādṛśyena pratipādyamānaḥ piṇḍa samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ  vyavacchinnaḥ śakyam avaganatum iti saṃbandhaḥ śabda pakṣe tu gaḥ sādṛśyena upalakṣitaḥ  viśiṣṭaḥ śabdāt avagamyamānaḥ piṇḍaḥ samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ  vyavacchinnaḥ śakyaḥ  avagantum guṇa karma ādivat  sādṛśyasya api samāna samāna jītīya vyavacchedaka tvāt iti sugamam gaḥ sadṛśaḥ  gavaya śabda vācya iti tāvat astu atha gaḥ sadṛśa eva ka iti āśaḍkā nivartana asāmarthya mateḥ pariplavaḥ enam eva artham kaścid ityādinā darśitavān tatra iti tarhi viśiṣṭā eva pratipattiḥ vākyāt astu iti ata āha na ca iti pratyakṣa mātrād bhaviṣyati iti ata āha na ca iti etena vākya pratyakṣa samāhāraḥ  api nirastaḥ sa hi pramāṇa samāhāraḥ  vā syāt  phala samāhāraḥ  vā ādye api pramāṇa tve sati samāhāraḥ samāhṛtayoḥ vā prāmāṇyam iti na tāvat  prathamaḥ phala aneka tve sati samāhāra anupapatteḥ tasya eka phalam prati paraspara ādhipatya rūpa tvāt na api dvitīyaḥ vākya pratyakṣayoḥ bhinna kāla tvāt vākya tad arthayoḥ smṛti dvāra upanītau  api gavaya piṇḍa saṃbaddhena api indriya ādinā tad gata sādṛśyān upanaye samaya pariccheda asiddheḥ phala samāhāre tu tad antarbhāve anumāna śabdayoḥ api pratyakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ tad  kim tad phalasya tad pramāṇa bahis bhāva eva antarbhāve vā kiyatī sīmā tad tad asādhāraṇa indriya ādi sāhityam asti tarhi sādṛśya ādi jñāna kāle api vistāritasya cakṣuṣaḥ  vyāpāraḥ na tasmin sati tasya anupayogāt  upalabdha gosādṛśya viśiṣṭa gavaya piṇḍasya vākya smṛtimataḥ kāla antare api anusandhāna balāt samaya pariccheda upapattiḥ iti tad etad jarat naiyāyika m atamāskandati nanu iti pūrve hi yathā gauḥ tathā iti eva vākyam gavaya padena apratīta samayena api prayoga mātra upayoginā sahitam saṃbandha pratipatti hetuḥ pratisaṃbandhinaḥ tu śabdāt  vā upalakṣaṇāt  vā upasthāpanam iti āhuḥ ādhunikāḥ tu pratisaṃbandhi upasthitiḥ pūrvavat eva samaya paricchedaḥ tu prayoga anumānāt iti āhuḥ avācaka prayogasya vākyān aṅgatayā iti tad virahiṇaḥ ca saṃbandhi upalakṣaṇa paryavasānāt iti manyamānā etad eva prayogam āropya darśayanti yaḥ  hi iti etena eva pariplavaḥ  nirastaḥ yadi hi saṃbandhaḥ  viditaḥ kaḥ pariplava arthaḥ atha na vidita iti tatra akāḍkṣa anuvṛtteḥ evam ucyata iti ced  tad api ayuktam na hi viśeṣa niṣṭhaḥ samayaḥ tathā satya śakya graha tvāt  api tu kiñcid  nimittīkṛtya deśa kāla ādi viśeṣa vinākṛta vyakti mātra niṣṭhaḥ tad eva nimittam na avagatam iti ced  avagatiḥ eva tarhi saṃndhasya saṃbandhinaḥ  anavagamāt iti kim pariplutam pramātuḥ na ca eṣa parama arthaḥ sādṛśya viśiṣṭa piṇḍa upakṣepe nimittasya api upakṣepāt  anyathā piṇḍa upakṣepe api nimittān upakṣepe manaḥ dharma ādi śabdānām jāti śabda tvam na syāt  avācaka tvam eva vā syāt  tad jātīyānām nitya parokṣa tvāt iti atra ucyate abhinava naiyāyikaiḥ pañcadhā hi vācya vācaka bhāva vyavasthā nimitta upalakṣaṇa rahite śṛṅga grāhikayā caitra maitravat  nirnimitte antar bhūta upalakṣaṇe nirvacanikayā pācaka ādi śabdavat nirnimitta eva taṭastha upalakṣaṇe paribhāṣaṇikayā ākāśa ādi śabdavat sa nimitte taṭastha upalakṣaṇa evaṃprakārikayā pṛthivī ādivat  viśeṣavat nimitte nimitta saṃḍkocanikayā svarga ādivat iti tatra prathama dvitīyayoḥ asaṃbhāvita tvāt iha vidita vṛttānta tayā tṛtīyam prakāram nirasya pañcamaḥ caturtham upayāti iti caturtham vyavasthāpayati na tāvat iti avidita gavaya śabda vṛttāntasya tu yad  bhaviṣyati tad anantaram eva vakṣyati tad idam uktam iti parama arthaḥ  vastu gatiḥ tatas ca tathābhūta eva piṇḍe saṃbandhaḥ  grāhyaḥ  na tu sādṛśya upalakṣaṇa upanīte piṇḍa mātra iti arthaḥ nanu nimittam api avagatam iti ata āha na ca iti na ca gaḥ sādṛśyena upalakṣyata iti upalakṣaṇam anumāpanam smāraṇam vā ubhayam api adṛṣṭa saṃbandhe anupapannam smaraṇa mātra apekṣayā daṇḍa puruṣa udāharaṇam etāvat eva ca syāt  yad uta gavaya śabdaḥ  vā gavaya tvam gamayet  yathā gauḥ tathā gavaya iti śabda arthaḥ  vā anumāpayet  avyabhicāra pakṣe vyabhicāra pakṣe tu smārayet iti nanu sādṛśyam eva jāti bhedam anantar bhāvya pratyetum na śakyam tasya bhinna pradhāna sāmānya vyakti guṇa avayava karma sāmānya bāhulya rūpa tvāt tasmāt  sādṛśayathātathā ādi śabdā eva tasya pratyāyakāḥ kevalam prasiddha aprasiddha sandehaḥ  avāśiṣyate tatra hastitva ādikam gaḥ śabdena nirastam mahiṣatva ādikam tu anucita viṣaya tayā anyathā upamāna svīkāre api apratīkārāt  tad ayam gaḥ sadṛśa iti asya arthaḥ gotaḥ  bhinna jātīyaḥ tad gata guṇa avayava ādi sāmānya bāhulyavān iti na etad api sādhīyaḥ darpaṇa iva candraḥ candra iva mukham mukham iva aravindam adaḥ  aravindam iva idam aravindam iti caturdhā sādṛśya gatau bhinna pradhāna sāmānya niyama ayogena tad anantar bhāvya eva sādṛśya pratipatti upapatteḥ kvacid  dṛṣṭam iha smaryeta tāvat iti ced  smaryatām tāvat atra avagatam na tu iha tad avagatam iti brūmaḥ tasmāt  gaḥ sāmānyena upalakṣyamāṇaḥ piṇḍaḥ kim tadvān eva gavaya śabdasya vācyaḥ  bhavatu paci kriyayā upalakṣyamāṇaḥ kartā iva pācaka śabdasya āhosvit  taṭa stham eva gaḥ sādṛśyam tad upalakṣita eva piṇḍa ākāśavat  tasya vācyaḥ  bhavet  kim vā upalakṣaṇam vihāya gandha apalakṣita pṛthivītva jātimān iva gaḥ sādṛśya upalakṣita jāti viśeṣavān eva piṇḍaḥ  asya vācyaḥ  bhaviṣyati itara niyata koṭi saṃśaya tiraskāreṇa koṭi traya avalambī sandeha eva jarat naiyāyikairūpa plutaḥ saṃbandha pariccheda iti ucyate etāsu avaśyam anyatamā koṭiḥ gavaya padārthaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti nirdhāraṇa saṃbhāvanām hṛdi nidhāya aitena manaḥ dharma ādi pratibandi grahaḥ pratyuktaḥ tatra api anumānena unnīyamānānām manaḥ vyaktīnām samāna guṇa tayā samāna artha kriyā kāritayā samāna jātīyatva anumānāt  sāmānya anavagatau tu tatra api aśakya eva samaya grahaḥ sāmānyam vā na tasya pravṛtti nimittam iti tad idam uktam sarvathā anupalabdheḥ iti yadi api gavayatva avagame api saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha an avagame tatra prayujyamāna tvāt iti hetuḥ asiddha eva na hi asati vṛtti antare tad viṣaya tayā prayogaḥ saṅgatim avijñāya jñātum śakayate prāk eva pramāṇa antarāt tad avagame tu kim anumānena sādhanīyam ata eva pratyakṣe api gavaye anumānam anavakāśam eva tathā api saṃbandhi avagame gavaya pada samabhivyāhṛtam vākyam eva saṃbandham bodhayiṣyati avācakasya api ca samabhivyāhāra upayokṣyate upamāna pakṣa iva tad api hi ati deśa vākyam vākyam eva iti matvā tad nirāsa artham saṃbandhina eva apratipatti rūpa pāditā ata eva āha kutaḥ vākyāt  vā iti ata eva vākyasya vyāpti para tā api nirākṛtā saṃbandhinaḥ  anavagamāt  na ca vyatireke tātparyam saṃketayituḥ abhiprāya upādhika tvāt  sat pratipakṣa tvāt ca iti yadi api vinigamanāyām hetu abhāve api na upamānasya kācid  kṣatiḥ ubhayoḥ api vācya tve saṃbandhasya tadānīm avadhāraṇāt tathā api vastu gati vivecayati tathā api kim ityādi tad anujānāti iti antam karabha vṛttāntam pariharati sādhyarmya grahaṇam ca iti upalakṣaṇa pada prayogaḥ ca avāntara bheda saṃsūcanāya tena iyam sūtra gatiḥ prasiddha sādharmyāt  sādhya sādhanam upamānam sa ca prasiddhaḥ  dharmaḥ samānaḥ pratiyogitayā tad upakṣiptaḥ  asamānaḥ ca iti bahu vrīhi pakṣe tu prasiddha dharmaṇa iti śeṣam pūrvavat  jarat mīmāṃsaka matam gaḥ sādṛśyam gavaya stham pratyakṣam eva iti vadatā nirastam śābaramatama aśaḍkya nirācaṣṭe gaḥ sthām iti jāti antara varti jāti antarasya iti prāyovādaḥ tathā api gavaya vyakti avacchinnasya na gaḥ vyakti avacchedaḥ  avagataḥ tatra upamānam avatariṣyati iti ata āha tasmāt  yathā iti dṛṣṭānte tātparyam prayogaḥ tu ityādi akṛta samaya saṃjñā asamāna adhikaraṇa vākya artha upadhānam pramāṇa vailakṣaṇyam iha draṣṭavyam viṣaya svarūpa vailakṣaṇyayoḥ asiddha tvāt ati pariśuddhi iha śabde trividhā vipratipattiḥ prāmāṇyataḥ  bhedataḥ  lakṣaṇataḥ ca iti tatra prathamaḥ kalpaḥ  vacana virodhāt eva nirastaḥ tad prāmāṇyam anabhyupagamya vivakṣita arthasya pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt    pratipādane vā tatas  eva tad prāmāṇya siddheḥ iti bhedaḥ tu parīkṣā parvaṇi nirūpaṇīyaḥ leśataḥ tu iha api vyāvartaka dharma yogāt eva bheda vyavahāraḥ  api lakṣaṇam ca tathā tatas  tad eva vivecanīyam tatra vipratipadyamānam prati tu parīkṣā avatāra iti āśayavān siddhavat  saṅgati bhāṣyam vyākhyāya lakṣaṇam avatārayati atha iti tatra samaya balena samyak parokṣa anubhava sādhanam śabda iti eke iha ca ādyena padena anumānam dvitīyena śabda ābhāsaḥ tṛtīyena sa vikalpaka pratyakṣam caturthena padārtha smaraṇam pañcamena kartṛ karmaṇī nirasyete apare tu ceṣṭāyām api gatam etad iti ati vyāpakam mattvā śabdatva samavāye satī iti āhuḥ atra prācayāna āmayam āśayaḥ yadi ceṣṭā na prāmāṇam aprasaṅga eva tasyāḥ kim śabdatva samavāye sati iti anena nirvartanīyam pramāṇam ced  tasyāḥ pratyakṣa ādi anantarbhāve pañcama pramāṇa abhyupagama prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt  śabda eva ceṣṭāyāḥ praveśaḥ samaya bala pravṛtteḥ śabda eva tu śabda vyavahāraḥ  laukikaḥ prāyika tvāt  cākṣuṣe jñāna darśana vyavahāravat iti te api sthūla dṛśvānaḥ ceṣṭā hi abhiprāya stha śabda smaraṇa mātra upayoginī lipivat  śabda eva tu ceṣṭā utpādita smaraṇa samārūḍhaḥ pramāṇam arthena ca smṛti utpādanāt  śabda viṣayam eva asyāḥ prāmāṇyam pramāṇa phalasya pramāṇa tvāt  na ca smṛtiḥ asyāḥ avāntara vyāpāraḥ yadi ceṣṭā upadhānam antareṇa avagataḥ  api śabdaḥ  na artham gamayet evam api saṃbhavet  na ca etad asti nanu evam sati ceṣṭayā eḍa mūka vyavahāra anupapattiḥ na hi asau tatas  śabda smṛtimān agṛhīta samaya tvāt iti ced  ata eva tam prati samaya balena śabdavat arthe api ceṣṭāyāḥ kuṇṭha tvam eva vyavahāraḥ tu anvaya vyatirekābhyām niyata viṣaya avinābhāva grahe pravṛtti nimitta aupayikaḥ abhiprāya anumānāt eva eḍamūkasya kari turagayoḥ kaśāḍ kuśa abhighātāt iva atha kṛta samayā api ceṣṭā eva kim na syāt  avinā abhāva abhāvāt  smārayatu vā padārthān tathā api na pramāṇam dvividhā hi sā samaya pramāra bhedāt  kṛtyanvayinī jñapti anvayinī ca tatra kṛtyanvayinī prayojaka abhiprāyam smārayantī pravartayati na tu kiñcid  pramāṇayati śaḍkha dhvanivat  atas  apramāṇam eva jñapti anvayinī tu kārakeṣu pratipadikā artha pradhānā kriyāsu vartamāna artha pradhānā tathā ca gauraśvaḥ puruṣa ityādi padaiḥ iva svatantreṣu padārtheṣu smāriteṣu paraspara anvaya yogaḥ pada eka deśa vibhakti viśeṣavat ceṣṭā eka deśa viśeṣāt prakaraṇa ādi viśeṣāt  vā kāraka ādi smṛti niyama iti ced  ceṣṭā eka deśa viśeṣa abhāvāt na hi atīta anāgata vartamāna pāka ādi pratipādakam ceṣṭā eka deśa viśeṣam paśyāmaḥ prakaraṇa ādayaḥ tu viṣaya viśeṣe śabdān niyamayanti na tu kāraka kāla viśeṣeṣu pravartayanti tathā tve vā gauraśvaḥ puruṣaḥ  hastī iti ādau  api karmatva ādīni unnīya vivakṣita artha avasāyaḥ syāt  na hi ceṣṭā kalāpe prakaraṇa ādayaḥ kāraka viśeṣa ādīn ākṣeptum alam na tu padakadambka iti asti niyamaḥ tathā ca kāla saṃkhyā kāraka viśeṣa pratipādaka vibhakti samabhivyāhāra vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ katham tarhi tatas  vyavahāra viśeṣāḥ saṃśaya pratibhayoḥ anyatarasmāt  viśeṣa anupalambhe vidūra vartini samāna dharmiṇi sthāṇu arthina iva iti tasmāt ubhayathā api ceṣṭā na pramāṇam atas  kasya caturṣu praveśa apraveśau cintanīyau etad ca saṃbhāvita prāmāṇyam aitihya ādi antar bhāvayatā ceṣṭā apa bhraṃśa lipi dhvani pada eka deśān sāvyavahārikān api akīrtayatā sūtra kṛtā sūcitam api manda matayaḥ  na gṛhṇanti iti tad anukampayā lakṣaṇam vyācakṣāṇa eva kiñcid udbhāvayati vākya jñānam tad artha jñānam vā iti ākāḍkṣā yogya tā sattimat pada kadambakam vākyam tasya jñānam jñāna mānam tad iti arthaḥ yathāśrutam uttaratra kim tu tatra api vākyam eva pradhānam asādhāraṇa tvāt indriya ādivat  sannidhi tāratamya vivecane tu sarvasmin  ayam nyāyaḥ hāna ādi buddhiḥ parāmarśa lakṣaṇā itarasyā anumāna phala tvāt tad anena nirākāḍkṣā yogyānāsannāni padāni nirasya ātā ceṣṭā ādayaḥ  api nirastā bhavanti iti vijātīya vyudāsaḥ sva artha dvārakam ca akāḍkṣa ādikam iti saṃgati graha pada pratisandhāna tad artha smaraṇa yogya tā ādi anusandhāna prakaraṇa ādikam uktam bhavati anena eva abhiprāyeṇa uktam padārtha smṛti ādayaḥ tu iti tad anena pratyakṣa ādeḥ samāna jātīyasya vyudāsaḥ anāpta vacasām ca āpta grahaṇena nirākaraṇam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa lābhaḥ nanu na ayam upadeśa śabdasya arthaḥ  yathāśruti ca avyāpaka tā siddhārtha asaṃgraha ādivat ityata āha yadi api iti na kevalam bhūta artha asaṃgrahaḥ sādhya artham api na kiñcid  saṃgṛhṇāti iti āha yadi api ca iti nanu pravartaka tvena vidheḥ ājñā adhyeṣaṇayoḥ kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ yena anayaḥ rūpa deśa padena asaṃgraha iti atas tābhyām vidheḥ vaidharmyam pratipādya tayoḥ api tatas  vaidharmyam uktam te hi iti tad  kim ājñā adhyeṣaṇā saṃgrahe api prayatnaḥ kartavyaḥ na iti āha tathā api iti ayam āśayaḥ yadi api lakṣaṇayā te api saṃgrahītum śakyete para sthāne prayoktṛ padam prakṣipya tathā api na asti asmākam tad asaṃgrahe api kācid  prayojana kṣatiḥ svarga apavarga upāya viṣayasya śabda viśeṣasya lakṣaṇa ārambhāt śāstrasya tad adhikāreṇa pravṛtteḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇe tu akṛte viśeṣa lakṣaṇān avatāra iti atas  prathamam tathā eva vyākhyātam vakṣyati ca diś nāga nirākaraṇa prastāve para padam apahāya prayojanavān iti eva vākya artha pratipattiḥ phalam iti ca lākṣaṇika pada prayogasya ca ayam eva upayogaḥ  yad ubhaya lakṣaṇa lābhaḥ prayojanam artha gatam asādhāraṇam grāhyam ca sādhāraṇam tu śabdasya sva artha pratipādaka tvam tad ca parasya eva tatas  tad apekṣayā para iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam syāt  nanu yadi upaniṣadaḥ prayojanavatyaḥ nūnam kañcid artham pratipādayantyaḥ kvacid  param pravartayeyuḥ pravṛtti aḍkita tvāt  prayojana sadbhāvasya na ced  param pravartayeyuḥ katham para prayojanavattyaḥ pravṛtti viraha aḍkita tvāt  prayojana abhāvasya ityata āha yadi api iti na kvacid iti ādau sākṣāt iti śeṣaḥ buddha ṛṣabha ādīnām anāpta tve kārakaḥ  hetuḥ māyā moha nimitta tvam jñāpakaḥ tu pramāṇa aviruddha sarva dharma kṣaṇika nairātmya ādi vacanam yathāśrutam bhāṣyam avyāpakam manvāna āha su dṛḍhena iti su dṛḍham paritas  nirasta vibhrama āśaṅkam pramāṇam pramā tathā avadhāritā viṣayīkṛtā iti na iyam nitya aniti avyāptim abhisandhāya nanu kāraṇam adhitiṣṭhata eva īśvarasya api kartṛ tvam tathā ca sthāna karaṇa ādīnām anvaya vyatirekābhyām varṇa nipatti prati sāmarthya avagamāt  tad adhiṣṭhāna śūnyatayā tasya na āgama kartṛ tvam bhavet  na ca śarīram antareṇa tasya sthāna karaṇa ādi saṃbhavaḥ teṣām tālu ādi vivṛta ādi rūpa tvāt iti āśayavān āśaṅkate tathā api iti bhāṣyam uttarayati ata āha upadeṣṭa iti na vayam asya bhagavataḥ kārya viśeṣeṇa anuvihita bhāva abhāva tayā upakaraṇam śarīram nirākurmaḥ tri aṇuka ādi niṣpattaye dvi aṇuka ādivat śarīra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi kārya niṣpattaye tad upagrahasya āpīṣyamāṇa tvāt api tu āyatana tayā kartṛtva nirvāhaka tayā vyāpaka tayā ca tad  tasya na iṣyate bhoga abhāvāt kartṛ tvasya nitya tvāt  kāryasya kartrā nirūpa adhi saṃbandhāt  śarīrasya vyabhicārāt ca iti abhiprāyavataḥ  vivaraṇam sthāna karaṇa iti tad evam rūpa āptaḥ kutas  pramāṇāt  niścetavyaḥ para citta vṛttī nām apratyakṣa tvāt  kāya vāc vyāpārayoḥ ca buddhi pūrvakam anyathā api saṃbhava āditya aśaḍkya mlecchā api hi ityādinā bhāṣyatāt paryam bruvāṇaḥ tad niścaya upāyam api leśataḥ  darśayati hetu darśana śūnyā iti ayam āśayaḥ dvividhaḥ  hi puruṣaḥ  asarvajñaḥ sarvajñaḥ ca iti tatra pūrvasya tāvat  sattva prasādhakāt eva pramāṇāt  rāga dveṣa moha viraha siddhau  anāpta tvam nirastam uttarasya api jñāna icchā prayatna sthāna karaṇa pāṭavāni tāvat upadeśa mātreṇa eva niścīyanta iti tatra sarveṣām avivāda eva jñānam tu yathārtham ayathārtham vā syāt  icchā api pratipipādayiṣā vipralipsā vā syāt iti sandehaḥ  avaśiṣyate tatra api abhyāsa daśa āpanne ayam arthaḥ  asya iti sāmānyatas  niścaye bhavati eva tad jñānasya yathārthatva niścayaḥ yathā abhyāsa daśa āpannam idam araṇyam amīṣām mleccha anām atas  asmin  ete mārgāḥ mārga vibhāga jñā iti pānthānām evam niścayaḥ vipralipsā ca hetu darśanena vyāptā hetau sati syāt  sa ca dvi rūpaḥ sva upakāraḥ para upakāraḥ  vā tatra tāvat  pāntheṣu vimārgeṇa pratiṣṭhamāneṣu mleccha ādīnām na kaścid  sva upakāraḥ svasya gṛhīta tvāt  śarīra mātrasya ca karaṇīya antara abhāvāt  bhāve vā aparityāgāt  na api dvitīyaḥ na hi anunmattā anapakāriṇam apakurvate na api para apakāra mātram puruṣa arthaḥ tathā sati sarvaḥ sarvam apakuryāt iti evam vipralipsā api nivāryate anabhyāsa daśā āpanna viṣaye tu pravṛtti sāmarthyāt  pramāṇa antara saṃvādāt  vā moha vipralipsayoḥ nivṛttiḥ iti mlecchā api āptā bhavanti yatas  pratīti gocarāḥ tatas  kaḥ sandehaḥ  mahā dhiyām āryāṇām ca tattva avadhāraṇa iti api śabda arthaḥ etena yad  yena rūpeṇa na niścitam na tad  tena vyavahriyate yathā rathyā puruṣaḥ sarvajña tvena na pratīyate ca abhimataḥ puruṣa āpta tvena iti vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ asiddha tvam uktam pareṣām avyāpakam āpta lakṣaṇam yathā aśrutasya ārī amlecchayoḥ abhāvāt  viśeṣaṇa antara prakṣepe tu asmad lakṣaṇa abhyupagama iti arthaḥ viparyastasya ayam praśnaḥ viparyāsaḥ ca pramāṇa ābhāsa mūlaḥ atas tam āha asti iti bhāga asiddha tām āśaḍkyāha atra yāvatī iti nanu para prayogam adūṣayitvā svātantryeṇa prayoga antara upādānam prakaraṇa sama ajātiḥ sat pratipakṣa tayā ced  svarga ādīnām pratyakṣa tvam kutas  setsyati iti ata āha yoga je tu iti hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt pramāṇe asati na pramā cakṣuḥ ādi ukta viṣayam paratantram bahis manaḥ iti tasmāt āpātatas tāvat  sat pratipakṣā eva ete hetava iti ata āha asmākam tu sabhyañca iti ayam āśayaḥ dṛśyate hi tāvat  bahis andriya uparame api asannihita deśa kāla artha sākṣātkāraḥ svapne na ca vācyam smṛtiḥ eva asau paṭīyasi iti na hi smaraṇa anubhava vibhāge api sākṣī praṣṭavyaḥ kim tarhi idam smarāmīdam anubhavāmi iti pratītyai  sva sākṣikaḥ  ayam arthaḥ na ca āropitam tatra anubhava tvam abādhānāt  smṛtitvānullekhanāt  anupalabdhasya sva śiraḥ ccheda ādeḥ avabhāsanāt ca smṛti viparyāsaḥ  asau  iti ced  yadi smṛti viṣaye viparyāsa iti arthaḥ tadā anumanyāmahe atha smṛtau  eva ayam anubhavatva viparyāsa iti arthaḥ tadā prāk eva nirastaḥ na ca saṃbhavati api na hi anyena ākāreṇa vyavasāya viṣayībhūtaḥ  ayam arthaḥ  anyena jñāna avacchedaka tayā anuvyavasīyate tathā ca sa ghaṭa iti utpannāyām smṛtau bhrāmyataḥ tam ghaṭam anubhavāmi iti syāt  na tu imam ghaṭam na hi ayam ghaṭa iti smṛteḥ ākāraḥ tasmāt anubhava eva asau svīkartavyaḥ asti ca svapna anubhavasya api kasyacid  satya tvam saṃvādāt  tad ca kākatālīyam api na nirhetukam sarva svapna jñānānām api tathātva prasaḍgāt hetuḥ ca atra dharma eva sa ca karma javat  yoga jaḥ  api yoga vidheḥ avaseyaḥ karma yoga vidhyoḥ tulyogakṣema tvāt  tasmāt  yoginām anubhavaḥ  dharmaja tvāt  pramā sākṣātkāri pramātvāt  pratyakṣa phalam dharma ājanaka bhāvanā prabhavaḥ tu na pramā iti vibhāga iti tad sāmagrī rahitatva āditya siddhaḥ  hetuḥ iti sūktam asmākam tu sabhyañca iti bahavaḥ ca iti anvācaye cakāraḥ yadi api ca asmākam parama sarvajña siddhau  avāntara sarva jñe na sidhyati api na kācid  prakṛta hāniḥ tathā api tad sadbhāve api pramāṇa sadbhāvāt  saḥ  api na upekṣām arhati iti iha dignāgena bhāva sādhanatva karma sādhana tvābhyām upadeśa padam vikalpya dūṣitam karaṇa sādhanatva pakṣaḥ tu asmat amitaḥ  api kuta upekṣita iti ata āha anyasmāt anyasya iti arthena hi sākṣāt  pratibandhaḥ pratyakṣasya eva paramparā pratibandhaḥ  anumānasya tad asya śābdasya vijñānasya sākṣāt artha pratibandhe pratyakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ paramparā pratibandhe tu anumānatva āpattiḥ apratibandhe tu aprāmāṇyam eva iti asaṃbhava eva karaṇa vyutpatti pakṣasya iti manyata iti arthaḥ atra bhāva vyutpatti pakṣe āptatva niścayaḥ śabda phalam tad dvārā vākya artha niścayaḥ  vā nanu āpta tvena niścitānām kim aparama visaṃvādi tvam avaśiṣyate yad niśceyam iti ata āha upadeṣṭa dṛṣṭṭṭaṇām iti artha iti arthasya sākṣātkāraḥ pratyakṣa tvam iti varṇa yojanā tena ayam arthaḥ āpta upadeśaḥ tasmin  eva āpte niścayam kurvan śabdaḥ pramāṇam atha vā āpte niścayam kṛtvā tad sahāyaḥ  vākya artha niścayam janayan  iti ubhayam dūṣayati iti āha imam iti anumānāt karūṇa abhyāsa hetu darśana śūnyatva ādeḥ karma sādhanatva pakṣam utthāpayati dvitīyam iti atra api upadarśita artha prāpti niścayaḥ tad dvārā artha tathātva niścayaḥ  vā śabdasya phalam tatra prathamam darśayati yasmāt iti dvitīyam darśiyati evam ca iti upadiśyamānor athaḥ prāptaḥ prāpta tvena niścitaḥ  yasmāt iti vā tathā tvena niścita iti vā sūtra yojanā ubhayam api dūṣayati iti āha dūṣayati iti nanu artha prāptyā artha tathā tvam niścīyamānam liṅga bhūtayā eva niścīyate tad  katham āha pratyekṣeṇa iti ata āha āptyā hi iti āpti niścaye api śabdasya vyāpāraḥ  na asti iti darśayitum artha tathātva niścayaḥ  api pratyakṣeṇa iti uktam mūla bhūta tvāt  tasya iti arthaḥ nanu śabda upalabdhasya arthasya kvacid anumānema api pratipattiḥ asti iti ata uktam prāyeṇa iti atra ca ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ āpta uktatva pravṛtti sāmarthya hetu pradhānayoḥ śabdasya prāmāṇya niścayaḥ phalam iti śaḍkitum ucitam api na śaḍkitam prāmāṇya niścaya avinābhūta tvāt  artha niścaya tad tathātva niścayayoḥ tasya tayoḥ eva antarbhūta tvāt iti manyamānena iti tam imam iti na āptatva sahāyaḥ  na āptatva niścaya sahāya iti arthaḥ prāptyā prāpti niścayena iti arthaḥ nanu anabhyupagatebhyaḥ pakṣebhyaḥ  na kañcid abhyupagatasya viśeṣam paśyāma iti ata āha etad uktam bhavati iti na āptatva hetukam na āptatva niścaya hetukam avisaṃvādi tvam avisaṃvāditva niścayaḥ anena sūtreṇa āgama artha tayā āgama phala tayā pratipādyate na api artha tathā tvam artha tathātva niścaya iti na iyam upalakṣaṇa tayā ca vidhādu ayam udāhṛtam yathā tu pūrva pakṣe vyākhyātam tathā atra api draṣṭavyam kim tarhi phalam asya ityata āha kim tu iti anena ullekhena anuvyavasāyena ya pratipattiḥ viṣayīkriyate sā iti arthaḥ yadi evam tarhi kkāptā uktatva niścaya upayujyata iti ata āha āpta tvam ca iti āpta ukta tvam ca iti arthaḥ nanu prāmāṇyam artha avyabhicāraḥ sa khalu katham artham apratyāyya pratyāyayitum śakyet
