hi hetuḥ na syāt  sādhya vā ādye asiddha eva dvitīye tu kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kva idānīm viruddhaḥ anyatarā niścaye api sandigdhā siddha iti āśakṅkya uktam vārttika kṛtā yasmāt ami upagatam bādhata iti na asiddhaḥ pakṣe niścita tvāt  na api kāla atītaḥ pramāṇa antareṇa balavatā abādhanāt  kim tu ayam eva sisādhayi pitam bādhata iti vārttika arthaḥ sugama eva dvitīyam vārttikam abhyupagatena bādhyate iti tad api yadi api pratijñā arthena tad bādhane asiddhaḥ syāt  tathā api virodhasya eva yatra udbhaṭa tvam tatra tad ullaṅghanena prayatna sādhyam asiddha tvam na udbhāvyam eva daivataḥ tad pratīkāre niranuyojya anuyoga āpatteḥ viruddha dvāreṇa eva āsiddheḥ api vyavasthāpane tad udbhāvanasya āvaśyaka tvāt ca iti sugamam uttara vārttika anurodhena tu vyācaṣṭe sva rūpeṇa hetu tvena vā iti arthaḥ atra udāharaṇa bhāṣyam ityādi uktam iti artha iti antaṣṭīkāyām bhāṣyasya iti śeṣaḥ virodha nigraha sthānāt etasyāma idam āśaṅkya yathā parihṛtam vārttika kṛtā tad anurodhena vyākhyātam pratijña āśrita tvam iti virodha vaibhavena ca udāharaṇāni vārttike vastutas tu sva mate māna antara siddhasya arthasya anyathā vacanam apasiddhāntaḥ vākya aṃśayoḥ eka artha bhāva abhāva viṣaya tvena vyādhātī virodhaḥ viparyaya vyāpta tvena niścitaḥ  viruddhaḥ  hetvābhāsaḥ sa ca vidhi sādhane svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ iti trividhaḥ tad yathā dhūmavān ayam yogyasya sataḥ tadvat tayā anupalabhyamāna tvāt  niragnika tvāt  jalāśaya tvāt iti niṣedha sādhane api svabhāva upalabdhiḥ vyāpya upalabdhiḥ iti dvividhaḥ tad yathā niragnikaḥ  ayam tadvat tayā upalabhyamāna tvāt  dhūmavat tavāt iti sarvaḥ ca ayam viśeṣaṇa dvārā api pratisandheyaḥ yathā kṛṣṇa aguruḥ āru prabhava vahnimānayam kaṭukā surabhi vipāṇḍura dhūmavat tvāt iti saṃkṣepaḥ yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ iha khalu hetvābhāsānām tad tya anusaṃhitānām yathāsaṃkhyam saṃśayaḥ  vivakṣita viparīta jñānam jijñāsā ajñānam vyāpti bādhaḥ ca iti phalāni tatra phala dvārakam prakaraṇa sama lakṣaṇam upakramyateyasmāt ityādi tad etad  bhāṣya mukhane vyācaṣṭe prakaraṇa iti yasmāt  prakriyamāṇa artha jijñāsā mātram bhavati sa prakarasama iti saṃkṣepaḥ tathā hi pakṣe sama bala bādhaka saha pravṛtteḥ na tattva nirṇayaḥ pratibalena pratiruddha tvāt  na api tatas  anusandhānena api sahasā vyāpti bādhaḥ anugṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tayā sama bala tvāt  na api ajñānam eva pakṣe vidyamāna tayā eka koṭi prasañjaka tvāt na api viparīta jñānam tena avyāpteḥ na api sandehaḥ koṭi dvaya anupanāyaka tvāt  tasmāt ekām koṭim upanayan sama balena pratiruddhaḥ katham atra nirṇayaḥ  bhavatu iti jijñāsām janayan prakaraṇa sama itarebhyaḥ  bhidyata iti tad ca sat pratipakṣa tvam siddha ubhaya hetukam asiddha ubhaya hetukam siddha sādhya ubhaya hetukam ca prathamam arūpa dravyatva ulabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna tvayoḥ tṛtīyam śrāvaṇatva kṛtaka tvayoḥ madhyamam iha udāhariṣyate tad anurodhena vyācaṣṭe sa khalu iti yadi api jijñāsā mātram atra upayoti tathā api saṃśaya anuvṛtti nivṛttyoḥ jijñāsā anuvṛtti nivṛttī iti mattvā uktam tatra sandigdhe tad vā jijñāsate iti nanu yata eva jijñāsā katham tam eva prekṣāvān tattva nirṇayāya prayokṣyata iti ata āha vicitra abhisandhitayā iti pūrva samayaḥ  duṣpratyayaḥ jātu prayojya buddhiḥ iti hi sādhana uttara ābhāsa prayoge hetava iti arthaḥ nanu eka eka pakṣa niyata tayā katham ubhaya pakṣa sāmyam anupalabdheḥ iti ata āha sā iyam iti nanu vyutpattim āśritya ced  prakaraṇa sama padam pravartate kṛtam tarhi yasmāt ityādi lakṣaṇa antareṇa ityata āha vyutpatti iti atha etad eva pravṛtti nimittam kim na syāt iti ata āha anyathā iti atra bhāṣya kāreṇa savyabhicārāt  prakaraṇa samam bhedayatā tasya saṃśaya hetu tvam asya ca prakaraṇa pravṛtti hetu tvam uktam tad ca saṃmugdham pakṣa pratipakṣau prakaraṇam iti prāc vyākhyānāt sūtra virodhāt ca na hi yasmāt  prakaraṇam iti sūtram api tu yasmāt  prakaraṇa cintā iti ata āha etad uktam bhavati iti api tu sat pratipakṣa tayā eva hetvābhāsa tvam iti jijñāsā mātra hetu tayā nirṇaya anutpādaka tvāt iti bhāvaḥ etena bhāṣye prakaraṇa śabdaḥ  jijñāsā para iti uktam nanu nitya dharma anupalabdhiḥ kādācid kī vivakṣitā sa dātanī vā ādyā anaikāntikī iva ākāśa ādau  api kadācid nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ dvitīyā tu asiddhā eva na hi nitya dharma upalabdhyā śabde kadācid api na bhavitavyam iti pramāṇam asti tathā ca asiddha tvam vihāya kutas  prakaraṇa sama tvam udbhāvayati iti ata āha na ca tattva anupalabdhiḥ iti ayam arthaḥ yasya evam viśeṣa grahaḥ tasya tāvat asiddha eva ayam iti aḥ tu yaḥ tu upalambha abhāvena sulabhām anupalabdhim matvā viśeṣam apratisandhāya pratibalena ca pratibandham upanyasyati tam prati kim ayam ābhāsatām yātu na vā na tāvat na yāti tathā sati sādhayet  evam ca tatas  agṛhīta viśeṣā dvitīyā api sādhayet eva na ca evam na ca anābhāsam asādhaka mati prasaṅgāt  na ca tadānīm doṣa antaram atra parisphurati anyatra pratibalena pratibandhāt iti yatra api yugapad aneka doṣa parisphuraṇam tatra api sat pratipakṣa tvam api udbhāvya viramyate na hi yāvat asti tāvat udbhāvyam anyatra saṃbhūya pratijñāyām sarvatra udbhāvana niyamāt iti yadi api pratyakṣavat  tattva anupalabdhiḥ api na kevalā api tu samāna dharma darśana ādi sahitā eva saṃśaya kāraṇam tathā ca codya cuñcoḥ abhimata bhraṃsaḥ tathā api tam upekṣya sva siddhānta avarodhena pariharati na hi akāraṇānām iti nanu ubhaya iti ekasmin pakṣe ubhaya padam vihāya aparasmin vyāvṛtti dvāra iti padam adhyāhṛtya phakkikā bodhaḥ api tu tattva anupalabdhiḥ eva asmad uktā prakaraṇa sama udāharaṇam iti śeṣaḥ evam jijñāsā hetutva abhāvāt prakaraṇa sama lakṣaṇa ayogi tayā śarīrāt anya tvam na tad udāharaṇam iti uktam idānīm saṃśaya hetu tayā anaikāntika lakṣaṇa ayogāt tad udāharaṇam eva idam iti āśayavān āha iti āha itas ca iti kecid  tu manyante tattva anupalabdhiḥ eva param prakaraṇa samaḥ  hetvābhāsaḥ tad nirākaraṇam sūcayati evam anyāni api iti na agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām anupalabdhyoḥ anyayoḥ vā dharmayoḥ kaścid  viśeṣaḥ  gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām tu yathā anyasya anyatra hetvābhāse antarbhāvaḥ tathā anupalabdheḥ api iti sā api tyājyā na ca anupalabdhyoḥ ātyantikam agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tvam ubhayoḥ siddha tve vastuna ubhaya anubhaya ātmakatva prasaṅgāt  ekasya asiddha tve vā katham agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tvam ātyantikam ubhayoḥ api vāstavyām asiddhau punar ubhaya anubhaya ātmakatva prasaṅgāt iti sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya tvāt sādhya samaḥ tasmāt  sādhya tvāt asiddha tā iti sādhya tayā asiddha tayā sādhyena aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sā ca asiddha tā kasyacid ityādi sugamam tad evam śiṣya pratipatti lāghavāya vākya gauravam vastutas tu asiddhaḥ sādhya sama iti etāvat eva lakṣaṇam uktam asiddha iti asya api pakṣa dharma tayā na niścita iti arthaḥ parāmarśa viṣayaḥ pakṣa dharma tā sā ca sva sādhyena nirupādhi saṃbandhasya pakṣa saṃbandhaḥ tathā api ca vyāpti niścaya sahitena saṃbandhi dvaya niścayena niścīyate vyāpti liṅga pakṣeṣu tu ekatamā niścaye api na iti tatra pakṣā niścayāt āśraya asiddha liṅgasya eva aniścayāt svarūpa asiddhaḥ vyāpteḥ aniścayāt anyathā asiddhaḥ eteṣām ca aniścayaḥ sandehāt  vā abhāva niścayāt  vā iti na kaścid  phalam prati viśeṣaḥ etena vyoma padmān sugandhi padmātvāt  ityādayaḥ  api saṃgṛhītā bhavanti anyathā yaḥ pakṣe asan  iti lakṣaṇena etad labhyate yathā hi asati sa pakṣe vipakṣe ca pratiṣedhaḥ kartu na śakyate tathā pakṣe api iti satyā eva iti satyena abhyupagatāyā iti arthaḥ tasyāḥ  nityatva abhāvāt iti tad asiddham iti ced  na kadācid upalambha lakṣaṇena api anitya tvena sādhya siddheḥ teṣām vyañjaka vaicitrye api vyakti āśraya saṃbandhinām upalambham antareṇa anupalambha niyamāt upalambhe vā tattva anupapatte sadā upalambha prasaṅgāt ca tejasā abhibhūta tvāt na tathā iti ced  na āśraya anabhibhave teṣām anabhibhāvāt  tad abhibhave tu teṣām upalambhe tad upalambha prasaṅgāt  ata eva na bhā bhāvasya tad vyañjaka tvam tasmāt  kadācid upalambha eva asyāḥ sāmānya avirūpa tām pratikṣipati iti na api karma iti sva āśrayam prāc deśāt  vibhajya deśa antaram prāpayat  karma tad tāyām vyavatiṣṭhate na atas  anyathā calana vyavahāra sya anākasmika tvāt anya nimitta abhāvāt evaṃbhūta artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt ca chāyāyāḥ tu āśraya eva tauvat na upalabhyate prāk eva tasya viprayojana saṃprayojane iti arthaḥ na guṇa u dravya asamavāyāt iti dravya asamavetam hi adravya samavetam vā asamavetam eva vā syāt  ubhayathā api guṇave vyāghātaḥ sāmānyavataḥ svatantrasya dravyatva āpatteḥ niḥsāmānyasya guṇa lakṣaṇa vyāghātāt  sāmānyavāna guṇaḥ ityādi hi tad  guṇa karmaṇām nirguṇa tayā guṇasya tatra samavāya virodhena tad samavāye sāmānya rūpatva upapatteḥ iti arthaḥ dravya asamavāyāt iti hetum sādhayati na mana iti teṣām viśeṣa guṇa virahāt  sāmānya guṇa u ayam bhavet  tathā ca āśraya saha upalambha niyame tad apratyakṣa tāyām niyamāt apratyakṣatva prasaṅga iti arthaḥ na api ātma guṇa iti iyam hi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tā idantā sāmāna adhikaraṇyena vyāptā tad ātma guṇa tām ādāya nivartamānam anātma guṇa tāyām viśrāmyati iti arthaḥ na api nabhaḥ nabhasvatoḥ iti cākṣuṣataḥ  hi guṇānām rūpi dravya samavāyena vyāptā tad ca rūpi tvam gagana pavanābhyām vyāvartamānam cākṣuṣa guṇa saṃbandham api vyāvartayati iti arthaḥ na api tejasaḥ tad guṇa tvam hi pratītau tad avirodhi tvena vyāptam anyathā guṇinaḥ sva guṇa pratīti paripanthi tve guṇasya nitya anupalambha prasaṅgāt  sati samavāye upalambha virodhāt  asati samavāye ca asattvāt tad ca atas  nivartamānam tad guṇa tvam api nivartayati iti arthaḥ tad sahacarita guṇa antara anupalabdheḥ ca iti ayam arthaḥ na tāvat  chāyā tejasaḥ  rūpam etad rūpasya śukla bhāsvara tu niya mātṛ na ca indranīla prabhā rūpavat āśrayaḥ vidhānāt tasmāt  guṇa antaram eva idam tasya iti vācyam tathā ca cakṣuṣā upalabhyamānam na rūpam anantar bhāvya upalabdhum śakyate cakṣuṣaḥ tathā eva sāmarthya akalanāt iti ata eva iti ayam arthaḥ cakṣuḥ mātra grāhya tayā tāvat chāyā na guṇa antara tvena śaṅkā āspadam rūpam tu saṃbhāvyeta tad ca upalabhyamānam pātha sa upalabhya śaitya dravatva ādi vyāptam atādṛśaḥ toyatva ayogāt pṛthivyāḥ tu upalabhya gandha ādi vyāptam atathābhūtasya pṛthivītva ayogāt tad ca śaitya gandha ādi sāhacaryam atas  nivartamānam anupalambhena tad guṇa tām api nivartayati iti api ca iti ataijasa dravya rūpa grahaṇe hi bāhya āloka vyāptasya eva cakṣuṣaḥ sāmarthyam adhigatam na ca yad sahitasya yasya yatra sāmarthyam tad rahitena tena tad karaṇam tathā sati vahni rahitam api ārdram indhanam dhūmam vidadhyāt iti arthaḥ virodhakaḥ tu adhika  iti āha tasmiḥ tu iti etena pārthivam rūpam āropitam tama iti nirastam bāhya āloka sahakāri virahe cakṣuṣaḥ tathā ārope api asāmarthyāt  tad eva hi dharmi antare vā samāropyeta pitta pītim avat  tatra eva vā niyata deśe avagamyamāne aniyata deśa tvam iti nedīyasyaṇīyasi api mahat tvavat  ubhayathā api tad prathamam antareṇa anupapattiḥ ekatra āropya tvāt anyatra āra upaviṣaya tvāt tasya eva na ca ālokam antareṇa rūpa grahaṇe cakṣuṣaḥ sāmarthyam iti uktam na cāra upyāra upa viṣaya aprathane bhrānti saṃbhavaḥ na ca ubhayoḥ anyatarasmin  avyāpṛtasya eva cakṣuṣaḥ  bhrānti janaka tvam na ca ayam acākṣuṣaḥ pratyayaḥ tad anvaya vyatirekayoḥ ananyathā siddha tvāt iti na api dravyam iti na pṛthivī agandha tvāt  na jalamarasa tvāt  na tejaḥ anuṣṇa tvāt  na vāyuḥ asparśa tvāt  nākāśam aśabda samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt na dikkālaḥ paratva aparatva asam avāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga anādhāra tvāt na ātmā buddhi anādhāra tvāt na manaḥ  jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga anādhāra tvāt iti arthaḥ na api anyat iti na idam adravyam rūpi dravyam asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt  asmad ādi pratyakṣam hi indriyeṇa vyāptam tad ca niyata viṣaya sāmarthyena vyāptam tad ca vipakṣān nivartamānam indriyam nivartayat  pratyakṣa tvam api nivartayati iti arthaḥ asparśa tvāt iti na idam aneka dravyam dravyam asparśa tvāt  asparśa tā hi dravyasya anārabhya tayā vyāptā sa ca niṣedhyāt aneka dravyān nivartamānā sva vyāpyam sparśa rahita tvam gṛhītvā tad viparīte viśrāmyati iti arthaḥ anārambhaka tvena iti avidyamānam ārabhbhakam yasya tad  tathā uktam tasya bhāvaḥ tatvat tvam iti etena āśraya asiddhiḥ parihṛtā yad  tu uktam manasā dravya antara anārambhe vaiyarthyam upādhiḥ na punar asparśa tvam tad  kim vaiyarthyāt anā ārambhaka tvam unnīyate anārambhakāt  vā vaiyarthyam iti na tāvat ādyaḥ sarva utpattimat prayojanasya asmad ādibhiḥ piśita locanaiḥ anākalanāt  tasmāt  yadi ārambhaka svabhāva tvam manasaḥ tadā kadācid ārambhe prayojanam api kiñcid  bhaviṣyati iti na ced  tad svabhāvaka tvam prayojana sahasreṇa api na ārambhaḥ svabhāva anuvidhāyīni hi prayojanāni na tu prayojana anuvidhāyinaḥ svabhāvāḥ pratyakṣa bādhaḥ tu tadā syāt  yadi tama eva apahnūyeta dravya tve pratyakṣasya ajāgaruka tvāt  nīlima guṇa śālinaḥ pratīteḥ katham evam etad iti cetṛ na vastu tas  asya nīlatve acākṣuṣatva prasaṅgāt  āloka sahakāriṇa eva cakṣuṣaḥ tatra sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt iti uktam śukla bhāsvara virodhitā sāmyāt  tu tathā vyavahāraḥ evam tarhi rakta ādi vyavahāraḥ  api prasajyata iti ced  na vyavahāre hi sati nimitta anusmaraṇāt  na tu nimittāmasti iti eva vyavahāraḥ yathā śaṣayoḥ śavi avahāraḥ  gauḍānām varṇatva nimitta aviśeṣe api na kādi vyavahāraḥ adṛṣṭa ādi sāmagrī viśeṣāt niyamaḥ  na atra api daṇḍa vāritaḥ iti tad  kim na kiñcid evac chāyā iti ata āha tasmāt  bhā bhāva eva c chāyā iti na ca vācyam saḥ  api katham ālokam antareṇa pratiyogi smaraṇa adhikaraṇa grahaṇa virahe vidhi mukhena cākṣuṣaḥ  viṣaya iti yad grahe hi yad apekṣam cakṣuḥ tad abhāva grahe api tad apekṣam eva evam hi tad itarasām agrahī sākalyam syāt  tad iha api āloka abhāve tad āloka apekṣā syāt  yadi āloke api tad apekṣā bhavet  na ca etad asti pratyuta virodha eva tasmin sati hi tad abhāva eva na syāt  kim tad sāpekṣeṇa cakṣuṣā gṛhyeta divā ca pratiyoginaḥ prabhā maṇḍalasya grahe eva pradeśa antare tad grahaṇam iti na kiñcid anupapannam anyadā api na rātrim apratisandhāya andhakāra grahaḥ rātri jñānam ca na divasam apratisandhāya tathā hi nirasta etad dvīpa varti ravi raśmi jālaḥ kāla viśeṣaḥ  atra rātriḥ iti ucyate giridarī vivara vartinaḥ tu yadi yoginaḥ  na timira ālokinaḥ timira darśinaḥ ced  nūnam smṛta ālokā iti adhikaraṇam api dṛṣṭam anumitam smṛtam vā iha idānīm andhakāra iti pratyayāt  vidhi mukhaḥ tu pratyayaḥ asiddhaḥ na hi na aprayoga mātreṇa vidhi tvam pralaya vināśa avasthāna ādiṣu vyabhicārāt  na artha antarbhāvena vākya arthe pada prayogāt adoṣa iti ced  iha api mātsaryam apanīya eṣā eva rītiḥ anugamyatām iti suṣṭhu upa saṃhṛtam tasmāt  bhā bhāva eva c chāyā iti deśa antara prāptimattva prayuktam hi gatimat tvam na tu deśa antara darśana prayuktam tad ca prayojakam iha niścita vyāvṛtti tathā hi svātantrayeṇa deśa antara prāptau vāraka anuvidhāna niyamaḥ  na syāt  prabhā tulya tve tejaḥ prabhā āśrayeṣu ratna viśeṣa iṣu c chāyā divase na syāt  chāyayā eva abhibhave vā bahalatame tamasi teṣām ālokaḥ  na syāt  āloka antareṇa eva abhibhave chāyāyāḥ  api udbhāvaḥ  na syāt iti saṃkalayati sā iyam iti asiddhiḥ anirūpaṇam na ca etāvatā iti vācyam iti śeṣaḥ kutas  savyabhicāra tvāt iti ayam arthaḥ yadi api tatra api svābhāvika saṃbandha virahāt asti eva hetutva asiddhiḥ na hi asti saṃbhavaḥ svabhāva pratibaddhaḥ ca savyabhicāra ādiḥ ca iti tathā api na tāvat  svarūpata āśrayataḥ  vā tatra asiddhiḥ udbhāvayitum śakyate tayoḥ niścita tvāt  na api upādhita upādhi apekṣayā vyabhicāra ādeḥ laghu pratipattika tvāt  upādheḥ tu tad dvārā eva pratipatteḥ yadi ca tena dūṣayitum na śakyate tad dvārā api apādhiḥ eva udbhāvyeta na ca etad asti vyabhicāra ādau hi udbhāvite sutarām nivartate upādhau tu kadācid  vipratipadyate tasya durūha tvāt iti astu tarhi savyabhicāravat aprayojakaḥ  nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ  hetvābhāsaḥ tasya api evaṃrūpa viśeṣa śāli tvāt ityata āha anyathā siddhasya tu iti bhavet evam yadi aupādhika tvam svābhāvika saṃbandha virahāt anya tṛ na tu etad asti anaupādhika tvam hi saṃbandhasya svābhāvika tvam aupādhika tvam ca tad varahaḥ tasmāt  viśeṣa antara abhāvāt sādhya sama samāna lakṣaṇavat tvāt ca tatra eva tasya antar bhāva iti arthaḥ bhāṣye gatimat tvāt iti sandigdhaḥ vārttike satī chāyā gatimatī deśa antare darśanāt iti viśeṣaṇa dvārā āśraya asiddhaḥ ayam eva sattvam vihāya niścita upādhi saha vṛttiḥ anyathā siddhaḥ tad etāvanta eva asiddha bhedā iti bhrama nirāsa artham udāharati ta eta iti cākṣuṣa tvāt iti niścitā asiddhaḥ aśarīra tvāt iti dharmita eva āśraya asiddhaḥ maitra tanaya tvāt iti saṃndigdha upādhi saha vṛttiḥ anyathā siddhaḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ atra yathā śruta bhāṣya vārttika darśanāt sarvam asamañjasam iti mattvā sva vyākhyām sthāna antarīya bhāṣya ādi upanyāsena saṃvadan  āha atra ityādinā anuṣṇa ityādinā pratiṣedhya vidheya dharma grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ darśitaḥ dharmi grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ tu ghaṭaḥ  vyāpakaḥ sattvāt ākāśavat iti pratyakṣeṇa paramāṇuḥ sa avayavaḥ  mūrta tvāt  ghaṭavat iti anumānena meruḥ pāṣāṇa mayaḥ parvata tvāt  vindhyavat iti āgamena hetu grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ tu jala anila aviṣṇau pṛthivītaḥ  viparīta sparśava tvāt  tejaḥvat iti pratyakṣeṇa manaḥ  vibhu jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt ātmavat iti anumānena brāhmaṇasya rājasūyam karma svarga sādhana tvāt  agniṣṭomavat iti āgamena evam navavidhaḥ  ayam ekavidha upamāna bādhena saṃkṣepataḥ  daśavidha iti nanu bādhaḥ  nāma na avinā abhāva bhaṅgāt aparaḥ kaścid  saḥ  api na trairūpya pracyavāt anya iti ata āha bādhā iti na hi bādham avyavasthāpya anaikāntika tvam apakṣa dharma tvam vā avatārayitum śakyam atas  asya avaśya udbhāvyatayā avaśya abhyupagantavyaḥ anyathā virodham api na abhyupagacchet virodhe hi hetoḥ abhāve svarūpa asiddhiḥ sādhya abhāve apakṣa dharma tā durnivārā atha virodhasya eva prathamam buddhau  upanipātāt  tad udbhāvanam antareṇa pakṣa dharma tvasya udbhāvayitum aśakya tvāt ca saḥ  avaśya abhyupagantavyaḥ tad etad samānam anyatra api iti uktam iti arthaḥ yadi evam bhāṣyam idānīm katham iti ata āha evam iti atha yadi ayam arthaḥ  bhāṣya kārasya vivakṣitaḥ kim iti na etad anurūpam udāharaṇam iti ata āha atra ca iti tathā api aihikam udāharaṇam asaṅgatam iti ata āha para matena eva iti atha etad udāharaṇam sva mate pañca koṭiṣu kva antarbhaviṣyati iti ata āha sa punar iti tad  kim iti na udbhāvayāṃbabhūva evam iti ata āha sthūlatayā iti vārttikam idānīm katham iti ata āha yasya apadiśyamānasya ityādi bhadantam pratyeka deśinaḥ parīhāraḥ samīkṛte abhidhānāt iti tad  vivṛṇoti ayam artha iti hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇa prakaraṇam chala prakaraṇam evam yatnena udbhāvanīya pariharaṇīya hetu ābhāsava prakaraṇam samarthitam atha sādhana vādī pramādī prativādī vā sat uttara samādhānayoḥ aparisphūrtau tayoḥ vijigīṣuḥ tad ābhāsam api brūyāt iti tad ābhāsa vyutpādana avasaraḥ tatra api jāteḥ sva pakṣa vyāghāta āpādaka tvena jaghanya tvāt  chalasya tu tātparyataḥ duṣṭa tve api vacanataḥ  aduṣṭattvāt asphūrti daśāyām api tad eva prayoktavyam tasya api asphūrtau jātiḥ iti viśeṣa jñāpana artham jāteḥ pūrvam chala uddeśaḥ sā eva lakṣaṇe api saṃgatiḥ iti bhāṣya artham āha uddeśa iti nanu ati vyāpakam idam lakṣaṇam artha vaicitrya upapattyā vacana vighātasya jātau  api saṃbhavāt ityata āha yathā vaktuḥ iti iha vāc vṛtti viparyāsena pratyavasthānam na tu tatra iti bheda iti arthaḥ nanu vibhāgaḥ  na udāhṛtaḥ tad katham vibhāge tu udāharaṇāni iti bhāṣyam iti ata āha vibhajyata iti yadi evam katham vibhāgaḥ ca iti kṛtvā vibhāga sūtram eva paṭhati iti ata āha vibhajyate anena iti ukti pūrvaka tvāt  tātparyasya tad anusaṃdhāna pūrvaka tvāt upacārasya uddeśa kamaniyamaḥ tad anurodhāt ca lakṣaṇa krama niyamaḥ pariśuddhiḥ abhidhā vṛtti saṃcāraḥ  yatra c chale tad vākchalam iti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ vāci iti viṣaya saptamī bhramam nivārayati vāci nimitta iti nanu etad  sarva  chala sādhāraṇam iti ata āha nava kambala ityādi tad idam vāc chalam uttara daśāyām navavidham tad yathā bhūbhṛdayam vīrya śālī mahāvayavattva āditi atra dharmi pada saṃcāreṇa na nakha prasūna āñcita kara pallavaḥ  ayam nitya karma kara tvāt iti atra sādhya pada saṃcāreṇa atā garbhavatī rakta vilocana tvāt iti atra ubhaya pada sañcāreṇa tad etad pratijña āśrayam trayam āḍhyaḥ  ayam nava kambala tvāt iti atra asiddhatva udbhāvanena gajaḥ  ayam viṣāṇītva āditi atra virodha udbhāvanena durālokaḥ  asau rājā tejaḥ maya tvāditi tra anaikāntikatva udbhāvanena tad etad hetu āśrayam trayam duvyam vāyuḥ sāvayava tvāt ambaravat iti atra sādhana vikala tvena asmad ādi durāsadāḥ tārakā gaganecara tvāt  pataṅgavat iti atra sādhya vikala tvena paśuḥ eṣa viṣāṇi tvāt  govat iti atra ubhaya vikala tvena tad etad  dṛṣṭantā śra trayam pratyuttara daśāyām tu pratipakṣa sādhane navavidham eva anyatra tu yāvat dūṣaṇa bhedam tad  yathā anyathā asiddhaḥ  asiddhaḥ ca iti vyāghātaḥ katham api siddha tvāt  sādhya viparyaya vyāptaḥ  ayam iti guṇa eva anyathā sādhya abheda prasaṅgāt  ambareṇa anaikāntikam iti asaṅgatam tasya api anitya tvāt na ayam pakṣī kutaḥ asya pakṣa bādha saṃbhāvanā ityādi svayam ūhyam asya pratyavasthānam ityādi bhāṣyam na pūrva sūtra vyākhyānam na uttara sūtra param vetyata āha tad etad chalam iti sambhavatoḥ athasya ati sāmānya yogāt asambhūta artha kalpanā sāmānyacchalam yatra tātparya saṃkrāntiḥ tad  sāmānyacchalam iti sūtra arthaḥ tad ca kvacid  saṃbhava vidhi viśeṣyeṣu yathā saṃbhavat vidyā caraṇa saṃpadayam brāhmaṇa tvāt  anityaḥ śabdaḥ śatam dvijātayaḥ bhojitā iti kvacid  tu hetutva uddeśa viśeṣaṇeṣu yathā brāhmaṇāt upajātaḥ  ayam brāhmaṇa tvāt  anityam kāryam dvija śatam bhojitam iti tad etad sarvam vivakṣitam āpnoti ca atyeti ca ubhaya samānam ca iti atisāmānyam ucyate etad nimittakam chalam sāmānyacchalam iti bhāṣya anurodhāt viśeṣa niṣṭham vyācaṣṭe saṃbhavata iti tatra ādyam udāharaṇam sphuṭam eva dvitīyam tu anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti ukte dhaṭaḥ api anityaḥ tarhi kṛtaka tvāt  śabdaḥ syāt  tṛtīyam tu śatam dvijātayaḥ bhojitā iti ukte śata saṃkhyā avacchinnā api bhojitāḥ sanakādayaḥ  na dvijātaya iti caturtham tu brāhmaṇāt jātaḥ  ayam brāhmaṇa tvāt iti ukte saṃbhāvanā viṣayaḥ  ayam abhihitaḥ  na hetuḥ iti pañcamam tu anityam kāryam anitya tvāt iti ukte sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ  hetuḥ iti ṣaṣṭham tu dvija śatam bhojitam iti ukte dvijā bhojitāḥ na tu tad matā śata saṃkhyā iti evam pratyuttara daśāyām api etad  ṣaḍvidham eva iti dharma vikalpa nirdeśer athasadbhāva pratiṣedha upacāracchalam upacāra vṛtti vyatyayaḥ yatra tad upacāra  chalam iti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ etad api uttare najavidham tad  yathā ayam māṇavakaḥ siṃhaḥ ayam siṃhaḥ  rājñaḥ ayam puruṣa siṃhaḥ  rāja śārdūlasya iti pratijñā māritya trayam varṣāṣu nausaṃcāryā iyam bhūmiḥ gaṅgā tvāt  ghoṣāṇām sukha vasati hetavaḥ te deśā gaṅgā tvāt  sa pradeśaḥ  dhana kāśa ādi vanaḥ  gaṅgā tvāt iti hetum āśritya trayam ye dhvani hetavaḥ te krośanti yathā mañcāḥ ye krośanti te dhvani hetavaḥ  yathā mañcāḥ ye krośana prayojanavantaḥ te krośanti yathā mañcāḥ iti dṛṣṭāntam āśritya trayam pratyuttare tu pratisādhane tāvat eva anyatra tu yāvat doṣa bhedam tad yathā aśarīra tvāt iti hetuḥ ayam āśraya asiddha iti ukte na evam hetu āśrayasya ākāśasya siddha tvāt  na ca hetuḥ asiddhatva ādīnā dūṣyate api tu liṅgam eva atas  niranuyojya anuyogaḥ  bhavata ityādi dharma vikalpa nirdeśa śabdena abhidhāna dharmaḥ  dvedhā abhidhīyata iti vārttika eka vākyatām āpādayitum bhūmim racayitvā yathā śruta bhāṣyam upekṣya khaṇḍa khaṇḍam vyācaṣṭe śabdasya iti dyayapi na iha sphuṭam tathā api ekatra vastu sadbhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate na eva kroṣṭāraḥ  mañcā iti parīkṣā vārttikam anāgatam avekṣya āha vārttika mate tu iti vākchalam eva upacāra  chalam tad aviśeṣāt saṃgatiḥ hi dvedhā bhavavati antar bhāva lakṣaṇā ānantarya lakṣaṇā ca tatra na tāvat  pūrvā chala parīkṣā sūtrāṇām lakṣaṇasya adhyāya artha tvāt adhyāya anantarbhūtasya ca āhnika prakaraṇayoḥ antar bhāvāt  parīkṣā tvena dvitīya ādau  eva antar bhāva arha tvāt ca na api uttarā ṣoḍhā api atra saṃbhāvyate smāraka abhāvena prasaṅga abhāvāt tayā vinā eva prakṛta siddheḥ upodghāta abhāvāt jāti nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇa avarodhena avasara abhāvāt uttara prabandham prati akāraṇa tvena hetutva ayogāt chala parīkṣāyāḥ  uttaratra avyavahāreṇa anirvāhaka tvāt  chala parīkṣā jāti ādi lakṣaṇa sūtrāṇām prakṛta upayogi eka kārya ayogena tad nibandhanāya api saṃgateḥ abhāvāt ityata āha parīkṣā parvaṇa iti prāsaṅgikī saṃgatiḥ prasaṅgāḥ ca parīkṣā parva sannidhānena upodvalita iti arthaḥ pṛthak sūtraṇāt  sādharmya sahitāyāḥ  viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ca saṃśaya parīkṣitam satsu vivacitam sugraham su pariharam chalam bhaviṣyati iti parīkṣā prayojanam sphuṭīkṛtya pūrva pakṣam āha yathā hi iti lakṣaṇa abhedāt eka tvam iti arthaḥ na tad artha antara bhāvāt na tad artha antara bhāvāt iti siddhānta sūtram tatra ca bhāṣyam anya artha antara kalpanā anyor atha sadbhāva pratiṣedha iti tad etad aviśadam artha antara kalpanāyā ubhayatra api pūrva pakṣe darśita tvāt  artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ tu yathā kathañcit sarva sādhāraṇaḥ anyathā vacana vidhātatva lakṣaṇa kṣateḥ paramārthataḥ tu na kvacid api vārttikam tu ekatra dharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate anyatra dharmi iti etad ca asiddham na hi atra mañcā eva dharmiṇaḥ pratiṣidhyante api tu kambala dharma saṃkhyāvat  mañca dharmaḥ krośanam iha api pratiṣidhyata iti ata āha vidheyam vastu iti atra eva uttara śaṅkā antaram apanayati kim tu iti tad etad samādhānam prakṛta udāharaṇa apekṣam draṣṭavyam sarva vyāpakam tu mukhya upacāra vṛtti anugata tvena anayoḥ bhedakau niyatau dharmau  iti aviśeṣe vā kiñcid sādharmyāt eka  chala prasaṅgaḥ avi ṅgaḥ iti chala prakaraṇam purūṣā śakti liṅga doṣa sāmānya lakṣaṇa prakaraṇam yadi api asat uttara tayā jāteḥ chala prakaraṇa eva antarbhāvaḥ  yuktaḥ tathā api pratijñāhāni ādeḥ nigraha sthānasya api tathā abhāvāt tām saṃgatim upekṣya artha dūṣaṇatva abhiprāyeṇa prayogasya sāmyāt uttara prakaraṇa eva antarbhāvaḥ tatra antarbhūtāyāḥ ca jāteḥ pṛthak karaṇe uddeśa eva prayojanam uktam pratijñāhāni ādi apekṣayā ca anudbhaṭa aparādha tayā para vyāmohana hetutvāt  parājaya daśāyām prayoktavyatva jñāpana artham tasmāt  prāk uddeśaḥ sā eva saṃgatiḥ iha api iti āha uddeśa iti chalasya samyak dūṣaṇasya ca iti upalakṣaṇam pratijñā ahānyādeḥ iti api draṣṭavyam na ca chale iti upalakṣaṇam tathā eva tathā api samyak dūṣaṇasya avyudāsaḥ tasya api hetutaḥ vaidharmyeṇa hetvābhāsa sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthāna rūpa tvāt ityata āha na ca iti ayam ca mātra śabda arthaḥ  jātīnām avatāram vāde pratiṣedha tā asat uttaratva khyāpanena eva sūtra kṛtā sūcitaḥ bhāṣye jāti pada vyutpādana prayojanam darśayati jalpe hi iti vapratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam nigraha sthānena eva samasta kathā mudraṇāt arthataḥ  asya paścāt abhidhānam tad  kim iti atra saṃgati anusaraṇena iti āśayavān sūtram pratyāharati vipra nam iti yadi api loka vyavahāra kathā vyavahārayoḥ puruṣasya aparādha eva nigraha sthānam aparāddhaḥ  hi nigraham śāstim khalīkāram prāpnoti anyatra loke śarīra viḍambanā kathāyām tu aparādha mātra udbhāvāna mātram anyatra vādinoḥ kāma cāraḥ aparādhaḥ ca kathāyām vipratipatti apratipatti bhāga dvaya paryavasitam tātkāli kam atattva jñānam eva tathā api tasya sva rūpeṇa udbhāvayitum aśakya tvāt  nirartha ka apārthaka ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyā anupapatteḥ ca tad unnayana upāya upalakṣaṇa tayā sūtram vyākhyātam tena kathāyām pravṛttayām vādinoḥ atattva jñāna jñāpikā kriyā nigraha sthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ etad ca pratijñāhāni ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyena prayukta nigraha sthāna pada padārtha ālocanayā sva rūpeṇa śakyā udbhāvana pratipādaka vārttika darśanāt ca sugamam bhāṣye api anantaram eva sphuṭībhaviṣyati syāt etad  na pratipatteḥ virīta tvāt anyat  kṛtsita tvam iti ata āha sūkṣma iti katham asau nigraha sthānam iti katham asau svarūpataḥ  apratīyamānā eva sattā mātreṇa nigraha sthānam bhaviṣyati na hi apratītam eva para dāra dharṣaṇam nigrahāya paryāptam iti arthaḥ vipratipadyamāna iti yatas  vipratipadyamānaḥ prāpta parājayaḥ bhavati atas  parājaya prāpti dvāreṇa unnetum śakyate atha parājaya prāptiḥ eva kā iti ata uktam nigraha sthānam pratijñāhānyādi khalu spaṣṭam parājaya prāptiḥ iti bhāṣyam sphuṭam iti arthaḥ yadi api adhike vipratipatti apratipattī saṃbhavataḥ tad asaṃbhave nigraha sthānatva anupapatteḥ tathā api vipratipanna vastu gocara tvena na tu tatra iti tad anigraha sthānatva bhrama nivāraṇa artham asamāsa karaṇam iti arthaḥ adhikam nāma iti upalakṣaṇam punaruktam api draṣṭavyam dūṣyam vā iti āgāmi pakṣa apekṣayā vā śabdaḥ yathoddeśam iti yathoddeśa kramam bhavatu lakṣaṇam na tu lakṣaṇa kramān atikrameṇa parīkṣā bhaviṣyati prathamata eva vyatikramāt ityata āha yathālakṣaṇam yathāsvarūpam iti artha iti nanu evam sati prathama dvitīya sūtre tātparya antareṇa avaṣṭabdha tvāt na trividha śāstra pravṛtti antar bhāvinī ārthyā vṛttyā prathama sūtrasya uddeśa antarbhāve api dvitīya sūtram alagnakam asaṃgatika tvāt ityata āha tasmāt iti aupodghātikyā saṃgatyā prathama uddeśam aṅgatam eva dvi toya sūtram arthāt  śrutyā ca prayojana paratayā iti na prakaraṇa asaṃgatiḥ iti arthaḥ śeṣam sūbodham iti kīrttyata iti kīrtitam tathā ca yathāyogam abhisaṃbandha iti sukha bodham iti arthaḥ anabhyāsa jñeyāt śruti vivara garbheṣu laghutaḥ sukha grāhyān mandaiḥ kusuma sukumārāt  prathamatas  manaḥ śrīmat vācaspati vacana vinyāsa visarāt trasatyadya api etad muhur iva muhur nirvṛtam api
